	Chhut-Ai-Kip8-Ki3 (2)
[1]	I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3-kiaN2 tak8-e5 toa3 i e5 ke-koan3 kap Nga2-kok kau3 Ai-kip8, in e5 mia5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  2). Liu5-pian7, Se-bian7, Li7-bi7, Iu5-tai7;  3). I2-sat-ka, Se-pou3-lun5, Pian7-nga2-bin2;  4). Tan3, Na2-hut-tha-li7, Ka-tek, A-siat.  5). Tui3 Nga2-kok sou2-siN--e5, kiong7 u7 chhit-chap8 lang5; Iok-sek i2-keng ti7 Ai-kip8.  6). Iok-sek kap i e5 hiaN-ti7 kap hit-tai7 e5 lang5 long2 si2.  7). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 gau5 siN, gau5 thoan5, ke-thiN choe7-choe7, koh heng-ong7, kek8-ki5 kiong5-seng7; chhiong-moa2 hit e5 toe7.
	8). Ai-kip8 u7 sin e5 ong5 heng-khi2, m7-bat Iok-sek e5.  9). I tui3 i e5 peh-siN3 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, chit e5 peh-siN3, I2-sek-liat8 lang5, pi2 lan2 khah-choe7, khah-kiong5;  10). lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 eng7 ke3-chhek lai5 khoan2-thai7 in, kiaN-liau2 in ke-thiN chin-choe7; au7-lai5 na7 tu2-tioh8 kau-chian3 e5 su7, in kap lan2 e5 tui3-tek8 lian5-hap8, lai5 kong-kek lan2, koh tui3 chit e5 toe7 chiuN7--khi3.  11). Tui3 an2-ni siat-lip8 tok-kang--e5 koan2-hat in, eng7 tang7-taN3 khou2-chhou2 in; in chiu7 ka7 Hoat-lo2 khi2 Pi2-tong Lan5-sek nng7 e5 siaN5 choe3 hu2-khou3.  12). Chong2-si7 na2 khou2-chhou2 in, in na2 choe7 na2 khui-khoah.  Tui3 an2-ni chiu7 ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khoa3-lu7.  13). Ai-kip8 lang5 chiu7 tok-chek I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3 khou2-kang;  14). hou7 in choe3-kang tioh8-boa5, seng-hoat8 kan-khou2, chhiau-thou5 choe3-chng, kap choh chhan5--nih hiah e5 kang; ti7 it-chhe3 sou2 choe3 e5 kang bo5-m7-si7 chin-giam5.
	15). U7 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 khioh-chia2-bu2, chit8-e5 mia5 Si-hut-lah8, chit8-e5 mia5 Phou2-a.  16). Ai-kip8 ong5 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 ka7 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 khioh kiaN2, khoaN3 in lim5-phun5 e5 si5; na7 si7 ta-pou gin2-a2, tioh8 hou7 i si2; na7 si7 cha-bou2 gin2-a2, thang hou7 i oah8.  17). Chong2-si7 khioh-chia2-bu2 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3, bo5 chiau3 Ai-kip8 ong5 e5 beng7-leng7 lai5 kiaN5, keng2-jian5 lau5 ta-pou gin2-a2 e5 oah8-mia7.  18). Ai-kip8 ong5 chiu7 kio3 khioh-chia2-bu2 lai5, tui3 in kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 an2-ni choe3, lau5 ta-pou gin2-a2 e5 oah8-mia7?  19). Khioh-chia2-bu2 tui3 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Hi-pek-lai5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap Ai-kip8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 bo5 tang5; in khah khoai3-pian7, khioh-chia2-bu2 iau2-be7 kau3, in i2-keng siN-liau2.  20). Siong7-te3 ho2 khoan2-thai7 khioh-chia2-bu2; peh-siN3 ke-thiN chin-choe7, kek8-ki5 kiong5-seng7.  21). Khioh-chia2-bu2 in-ui7 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3, Siong7-te3 chiu7 hou7 in chiaN5-ke.  22). Hoat-lo2 hoan-hu3 i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2, Hoan7 sou2 siN e5 ta-pou-kiaN2 lin2 tioh8 ka7 i hiat-loh8 ho5; it-chhe3 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2, lin2 tioh8 lau5 i e5 siN3-mia7.

[2]	U7 chit8 e5 Li7-bi7 chok8 e5 lang5, khi3 chhoa7 chit8 e5 Li7-bi7 chok8 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2.  2). Hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 hoai5-in7, siN chit8 e5 kiaN2; khoaN3-kiN3 i si7 chheng-siu3 e5 gin2-a2, chiu7 khng3 i saN-geh8-jit8 ku2.  3). Au7-lai5 khoaN3 boe7 koh khng3--tit, chiu7 ui7-tioh8 i chhu2 lou5-tek-a2 e5 siuN, eng7 chioh8-iu5 kap lek8-chhiN kou5 i; chiong gin2-a2 he7 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7, lok ti7 ho5-piN, lou5-ui2 e5 tiong-kan.  4). I e5 toa7-chi2 hng7-hng7 khia7--teh, ai3 chai i oe7 tu2-tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7.  5). Hoat-lo2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 loh8-lai5 ho5--nih, beh soe2-ek8; i hiah e5 lu2-pi7 kiaN5-iu5 ti7 ho5-piN; i khoaN3-kiN3 lou5-ui2 e5 tiong-kan u7 siuN, chiu7 chhe chit8 e5 lu2-pi7 gia5--lai5.  6). Hian-khui khoaN3-kiN3 gin2-a2; khoaN3 ah, gin2-a2 teh hau2.  I chiu7 lin5-bin2 i, kong2, Che chiu7-si7 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 gin2-a2.  7). I e5 toa7-chi2 ka7 Hoat-lo2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kong2, Goa2 khi3 ti7 Hi-pek-lai5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 tiong-kan kio3 chit8 e5 lin-bu2, ka7 li2 io chit e5 gin2-a2, ho2 mah?  8). Hoat-lo2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ka7 i kong2, Li2 thang khi3 ah.  Cha-bou2-kiaN2 chiu7 khi3, kio3 gin2-a2 e5 lau7-bu2.  9). Hoat-lo2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ka7 i kong2, Pho7 chit e5 gin2-a2 khi3, ka7 goa2 io i, goa2 beh hou7 li2 kang-chiN5.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 pho7 gin2-a2 khi3 io i.  10). Gin2-a2 chiam7-chiam7 toa7, hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 toa3 i kau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 hia, choe3 i e5 kiaN2.  I ka7 i ho7-mia5 kio3 Mou5-se, kong2, In-ui7 goa2 tui3 chui2--nih kiu3 i chhut-lai5.
	11). Au7-lai5 Mou5-se i2-keng tiong2-seng5, i chhut-khi3 kau3 i e5 hiaN-ti7 hia, khoaN3-kiN3 in teh taN-teh; khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 phah chit8 e5 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5, chiu7-si7 i e5 hiaN-ti7.  12). I khoaN3 cho2-iu7, khoaN3 bo5 lang5 ti7-hia, chiu7 phah-si2 Ai-kip8 lang5, iam2 ti7 soa--nih.  13). Keh-jit8 koh chhut-khi3, khoaN3-kiN3 u7 nng7 e5 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 lang5 saN-phah, chiu7 tui3 hit e5 m7-tioh8--e5 kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 phah li2 e5 tang5-phoaN7?  14). Hit e5 lang5 kong2, Chi7-chui7 siat-lip8 li2 choe3 siu2-leng2 kap sim2-phoaN3-koaN lai5 koan2 goan2? Li2 siuN7 beh phah-si2 goa2, chhin-chhiuN7 phah-si2 hit e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 mah? Mou5-se kiaN kong2, Chit e5 tai7-chi3 chin-chiaN3 lou7-chhut.  15). Hoat-lo2 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 siuN7 beh thai5 Mou5-se.  Chong2-si7 Mou5-se siam2-pi7 Hoat-lo2, chau2-khi3 Bi2-tian5 toe7 khia7-khi2; che7 ti7 chiN2-piN.  16). Bi2-tian5 e5 che3-si u7 chhit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; in lai5 chhiuN7-chui2 kau3 moa2 cho5, hou7 lau7-pe7 e5 iuN5-kun5 lim.  17). Hiah e5 kou3-iuN5--e5 kau3, koaN2 in; Mou5-se chiu7 khi2-lai5 pang-chan7 in, hou7 in e5 iuN5-kun5 lim.  18). In lai5 kau3 lau7-pe7, Liu5-jiN2, hia; i kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 lin2 chaiN2-iuN7 hiah-kin2 to3--lai5?  19). In kong2, U7 chit8 e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 kiu3 goan2 thoat-li7 kou3-iuN5 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, koh thoe3 goan2 chhut-lat8 chhiuN7 chui2, hou7 iuN5-kun5 lim.  20). I tui3 i hiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kong2, Hit e5 lang5 ti7 tah-loh8? Lin2 siaN2-su7 pang3 i ti7-hia? tioh8 chhiaN2 i lai5 chiah8.  21). Mou5-se goan7 kap hit-lang5 tiam3; i chiu7 chiong i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Se-pho-lah8, ke3 hou7 Mou5-se.  22). SiN chit8 e5 kiaN2; Mou5-se ka7 i ho7 mia5 kio3 Kek-sun7; in-ui7 kong2, Goa2 kia3-kha ti7 goa7-pang.
	23). Lek8-ke3 choe7-choe7 ni5 Ai-kip8 ong5 si2; I2-sek-liat8 lang5, in-ui7 choe3 khou2-kang, chiu7 thou2-khui3 au5-kio3; in choe3 khou2-kang au5-kio3 e5 siaN kau3 hou7 Siong7-te3 thiaN-kiN3.  24). Siong7-te3 thiaN-kiN3 in e5 hiN-hiN-chhan; Siong7-te3 chiu7 ki3-tit I kap A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok sou2 lip8 e5 iok.  25). Siong7-te3 khoaN3-kou3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, Siong7-te3 ia7 chai in e5 tai7-chi3.

[3]	Mou5-se kou3 i e5 tiuN7-lang5, Bi2-tian5 e5 che3-si, Iap8-thek-lo5, e5 iuN5-kun5, koaN2 iuN5 khi3 khong3-ia2 e5 au7-bin7, kau3 Siong7-te3 e5 soaN, chiu7-si7 Ho5-liat8 soaN.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 ti7 chhi3-phe3-lai7 he2-iam7-tiong tui3 i chhut-hian7, i khoaN3-kiN3, khoaN3 ah, chhi3-phe3 hou7 he2 sio, chhi3-phe3 ia7 bo5 toh8--khi3.  3). Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 taN beh oat-ke3--khi3, khoaN3 chit e5 toa7 e5 keng2-siong7, chit e5 chhi3-phe3 chaiN2-iuN7 bo5 toh8--khi3 ah.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-kiN3 i oat-khi3 beh khoaN3, Siong7-te3 chiu7 tui3 chhi3-phe3-lai7 kio3 i kong2, Mou5-se, Mou5-se.  I chiu7 kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia.  5). I chiu7 kong2, Li2 boh8-tit kun7-oa2 lai5; tioh8 thng3 li2 kha--nih e5 oe5, in-ui7 li2 khia7 e5 sou2-chai7 si7 seng3-toe7.  6). Koh kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 chou2-kong e5 Siong7-te3, A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3, Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3.  Mou5-se jia i e5 bin7; m7-kaN2 khoaN3 Siong7-te3.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5, in e5 khun3-khou2 Goa2 sit8-chai7 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 lah; in ui7-tioh8 tok-kang--e5 lai5 au5-kio3, Goa2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 lah; Goa2 pun2 chai in e5 thong3-khou2.  8). TaN Goa2 loh8--lai5 beh kiu3 in thoat-li7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chhoa7 in chhut hit e5 toe7, kau3 pui5-sui2 khui-khoah e5 toe7, kau3 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Ka-lam5, Hek, A-mou5-li7, Pi2-li7-se2, Hi-bi7, Ia5-pou3-su, hiah e5 chok8 e5 sou2-chai7.  9). TaN I2-sek-liat8 lang5 au5-kio3 e5 siaN kau3 hou7 Goa2 thiaN-kiN3; Goa2 ia7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ai-kip8 lang5 khou2-chhou2 in e5 kan-khou2.  10). TaN li2 lai5, Goa2 beh chhe li2 khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2, chhoa7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8.  11). Mou5-se tui3 Siong7-te3 kong2, Goa2 si7 sim2-mih8 lang5 thang khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2, chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 ah?  12). I kong2, Goa2 sit8-chai7 beh kap li2 ti7-teh; li2 chhoa7 peh-siN3 chhut Ai-kip8 liau2-au7, lin2 beh ti7 chit e5 soaN hok8-sai7 Siong7-te3; che beh choe3 Goa2 chhe li2 e5 cheng3-ku3.  13). Mou5-se tui3 Siong7-te3 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, goa2 kau3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hia, tui3 in kong2, Lin2 chou2-kong e5 Siong7-te3 chhe goa2 lai5 lin2 chia; in na7 mng7 goa2 kong2, I kio3 sim2-mih8 mia5? goa2 beh ka7 in kong2 sim2-mih8 ah?  14). Siong7-te3 tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 si7 Chu7-jian5 Ji5-jian5-e5; koh kong2, Li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 an2-ni kong2, Chu7-jian5-e5 chhe goa2 kau3 lin2 chia.  15). Siong7-te3 koh tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 an2-ni kong2, Chhe goa2 kau3 lin2 chia e5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lin2 chou2-kong e5 Siong7-te3, A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3, Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3; che si7 Goa2 eng2-oan2 e5 mia5, che si7 Goa2 e5 ki3-liam7 kau3 ban7-tai7.  16). Li2 khi3 chio-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiuN2-lo2, ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa, lin2 chou2-kong e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3, tui3 goa2 chhut-hian7, kong2, Goa2 sit8-chai7 koan3-kou3 lin2, lang5 ti7 Ai-kip8 sou2 khoan2-thai7 lin2 e5, Goa2 ia7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.  17). Goa2 ia7 bat kong2, Goa2 beh chhoa7 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 kan-khou2, kau3 Ka-lam5, Hek, A-mou5-li7, Pi2-li7-se2, Hi-bi7, Ia5-pou3-su, hiah e5 chok8 e5 toe7, kau3 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7.  18). In beh thiaN li2 e5 oe7; li2 kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiuN2-lo2 tioh8 khi3 kiN3 Ai-kip8 ong5, ka7 i kong2, Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng tu2-tioh8 goan2; taN kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 goan2 khi3 khong3-ia2, kiaN5 saN-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7, beh che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goan2 e5 Siong7-te3.  19). Goa2 chai sui-jian5 eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, Ai-kip8 ong5 ia7 m7 hou7 lin2 khi3.  20). Goa2 beh chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2, eng7 Goa2 ti7 Ai-kip8-tiong sou2 beh kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 ki5-su7 lai5 phah i; jian5-au7 i chiah chun2 lin2 khi3.  21). Goa2 beh hou7 chit e5 peh-siN3 tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 lin2 chhut-khi3 e5 si5, bo5 khang-chhiu2 khi3;  22). chiah e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 tak8-e5 beh tui3 i e5 chhu3-piN kap toa3 ti7 i e5 ke-lai7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 tho2 gun5-khi3, kim-khi3, kap i-hok8, thang hou7 li2 e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 eng7; an2-ni lin2 beh chhiuN2 Ai-kip8 lang5.

[4]	Mou5-se in3 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, in beh m7-sin3 goa2, ia7 m7-thiaN goa2 e5 oe7; in-ui7 in beh kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa be7-bat tui3 li2 chhut-hian7.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i kong2, Ti7 li2 chhiu2--nih si7 sim2-mih8? I kong2, Si7 koaiN2-a2.  3). Kong2, Hiat ti7 toe7--nih.  I chit8-e7 hiat ti7 toe7--nih, chiu7 piN3-choe3 choa5; Mou5-se chiu7 chau2-siam2 i.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Chhun li2 e5 chhiu2 liah8 i e5 be2; (chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 liah8 i, ti7 chhiu2-tiong iu5-goan5 piN3-choe3 koaiN2-a2;)  5). an2-ni thang hou7 in sin3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in e5 chou2-kong e5 Siong7-te3, A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3, Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3, u7 tui3 li2 chhut-hian7.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh tui3 i kong2, He7 li2 e5 chhiu2 ti7 li2 e5 heng-cheng5.  Chiu7 he7 chhiu2 ti7 heng-cheng5; thiu--chhut-lai5 e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, chhiu2 i2-keng thai2-ko, peh8 chhin-chhiuN7 seh.  7). Koh kong2, Koh he7 li2 e5 chhiu2 ti7 li2 e5 heng-cheng5.  (I chiu7 he7 ti7 i e5 heng-cheng5; thiu--chhut-lai5 e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, i2-keng chiau3-goan5, kap thong seng-khu e5 bah bo5 koh-iuN7.)  8). Koh kong2, Siat-su2 in bo5 beh sin3 li2, ia7 bo5 beh thiaN thau5-chit8 e5 sin5-jiah, chiu7 beh sin3 te7-ji7 e5 sin5-jiah.  9). Hit nng7 e5 sin5-jiah in na7 long2 m7-sin3, ia7 m7-thiaN li2 e5 oe7, li2 tioh8 tui3 ho5--nih iuN2 chui2, to3 ti7 ta-toe7; li2 tui3 ho5--nih sou2 iuN2 e5 chui2 beh ti7 ta-toe7 piN3-choe3 huih.
	10). Mou5-se tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Chu2 ah, goa2 peng5-sou3 m7-si7 oe7 kong2-oe7 e5 lang5, tui3 Li2 ka7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 kong2-oe7 e5 liau2-au7 ia7 si7 an2-ni; goa2 si7 chhui3-chih8 tun e5 lang5.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i kong2, Chhong3-cho7 lang5 e5 chhui3 si7 chi7-chui7 ah? hou7 lang5 e2-kau2, chhau3-hi7-lang5, bak8-chiu kim, chhiN-mi5 e5, si7 chi7-chui7 ah? kiam2-m7-si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa mah?  12). TaN li2 khi3 ah, Goa2 beh siuN2-su3 li2 khau2-chai5, ka3-si7 li2 sou2 eng-kai kong2--e5.  13). I kong2, Chu2 ah, Li2 hap8-i3 chhe chi7-chui7, chiu7 chhe i khi3.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se hoat-chhut siu7-khi3, kong2, Kiam2-m7-si7 u7 li2 e5 hiaN, Li7-bi7-lang5, A-lun5 mah? Goa2 chai i si7 oe7 kong2-oe7 e5 lang5.  Koh i taN chhut-lai5 ngia5-chih li2; i chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 sim-lai7 chiu7 hoaN-hi2.  15). Li2 tioh8 tui3 i kong2, eng7 sou2 eng-kai kong2 e5 oe7 thoan5 hou7 i; Goa2 ia7 beh siuN2-su3 li2 kap i u7 khau2-chai5, koh beh ka3-si7 lin2 sou2 eng-kai kiaN5 e5 su7.  16). I beh thoe3 li2 tui3 peh-siN3 kong2-oe7; i beh tui3 li2 chun2-choe3 chhui3, li2 beh tui3 i chun2-choe3 Siong7-te3.  17). Li2 e5 chhiu2 tioh8 kiah8 chit ki koaiN2-a2, eng7 i lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah.
	18). Tui3 an2-ni Mou5-se chiu7 khi3, to3--khi3 i e5 tiuN7-lang5 Iap8-thek-lo5 hia, ka7 i kong2, Kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 goa2 to3--khi3, khoaN3 goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5, khoaN3 in iau2 ti7-teh a2-bo5.  Iap8-thek-lo5 ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 thang an-jian5 khi3 lah.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Bi2-tian5 tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 khi3 to3--khi3 Ai-kip8, in-ui7 ai3 hai7 li2 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 long2 si2 lah.  20). Mou5-se toa3 i e5 bou2 kap nng7 e5 kiaN2, hou7 in khia5-lu5, to3--khi3 Ai-kip8 toe7; Mou5-se chhiu2--nih kiah8 Siong7-te3 e5 koaiN2-a2.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 to3--khi3 Ai-kip8 e5 si5, tioh8 chu3-i3 chiong Goa2 sou2 kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2 it-chhe3 e5 ki5-su7 kiaN5 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5; chong2-si7 Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 sim ngi7, i ia7 bo5 beh pang3 chit e5 peh-siN3 khi3.  22). Li2 tioh8 ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8 si7 Goa2 e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 toa7-kiaN2;  23). Goa2 bat tui3 li2 kong2, Tioh8 thau2-pang3 Goa2 e5 kiaN2 khi3, thang hok8-sai7 Goa2; li2 ia7 m7-chun2 i khi3; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh thai5-si2 li2 e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 toa7-kiaN2.  24). Mou5-se ti7 lou7--nih, ti7 kheh-tiam3, Ia5-ho5-hoa tu2-tioh8 i, beh hou7 i si2.  25). Se-pho-lah8 chiu7 theh8 chit8 te3 lai7-chioh8, koah i e5 kiaN2 iong5-but2 e5 phe5, hiat ti7 i e5 kha-cheng5, kong2, Li2 si7 goa2 huih e5 tiong7-hu.  26). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 pang3 i soah.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Li2 si7 huih e5 tiong7-hu, in-ui7 kat-le2 e5 ian5-kou3.
	27). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 A-lun5 kong2, Li2 khi3 khong3-ia2 ngia5-chih Mou5-se.  I chiu7 khi3, ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 soaN tu2-tioh8 i, chiu7 ka7 i chim.  28). Mou5-se chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe i kong2 e5 oe7, kap hoan-hu3 i kiaN5 e5 sin5-jiah, long2 ka7 A-lun5 kong2.  29). Mou5-se A-lun5 chiu7 khi3 chio-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 cheng3 tiuN2-lo2;  30). A-lun5 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 long2 kong2 i, koh ti7 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiaN5 hiah e5 sin5-jiah.  31). Peh-siN3 chiu7 sin3; in thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa koan3-kou3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, koh khoaN3 in e5 kan-khou2, chiu7 aN3-thau5 keng3-pai3.

[5]	Au7-lai5 Mou5-se A-lun5 jip8--khi3, ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, in thang ti7 khong3-ia2 ui7 Goa2 siu2-choeh.  2). Hoat-lo2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 chi7-chui7 hou7 goa2 tioh8 thiaN I e5 oe7, chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khi3 ah? Goa2 m7-bat Ia5-ho5-hoa, ia7 m7-chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khi3.  3). In kong2, Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 Siong7-te3 tu2-tioh8 goan2; kiu5 li2 chun2 goan2 khi3 khong3-ia2 kiaN5 saN jit8 e5 lou7, che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3, kiaN-liau2 I eng7 un-ek8 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 goan2.  4). Ai-kip8 ong5 tui3 in kong2, Mou5-se A-lun5, lin2 siaN2-su7 hou7 peh-siN3 hong-hoe3 in e5 kang ah? lin2 khi3 taN lin2 e5 taN3 lah.  5). Hoat-lo2 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, chit sou2-chai7 e5 peh-siN3 hian7-chai7 chin-choe7, lin2 keng2-jian5 hou7 in soah in e5 taN-taN3.  6). Tng hit-jit8 Hoat-lo2 hoan-hu3 peh-siN3 e5 tok-kang--e5 kap in e5 thau5-bak8, kong2,  7). Lin2 m7-thang chiau3-ku7 eng7 chhau2 hou7 chit e5 peh-siN3 choe3 chng; hou7 in khi3 ka-ki7 khioh chhau2.  8). In cheng5 choe3 chng e5 siau3-giah8, lin2 iu5-goan5 hou7 in an2-ni choe3, m7-thang sio2-khoa2 kiam2-chio2; in-ui7 in pin5-toaN7, sou2-i2 au5-kio3 kong2, Chun2 goan2 khi3 che3-su7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3.  9). Lin2 tioh8 eng7 khah-tang7 e5 kang hou7 in choe3, hou7 in tioh8-boa5; bo5 khi3 thiaN bo5-iaN2 oe7.  10). Peh-siN3 e5 tok-kang--e5 kap in e5 thau5-bak8 chhut-khi3 ka7 peh-siN3 kong2, Hoat-lo2 an2-ni kong2, Goa2 m7 eng7 chhau2 hou7 lin2.  11). Lin2 khoaN3 tah-loh8 u7 chhau2, chiu7 ka-ki7 khi3 hia khioh; chong2-si7 lin2 e5 kang long2 boe7 chio2--tit.  12). Tui3 an2-ni peh-siN3 si3-soaN3 pian3 Ai-kip8 toe7, khioh chhau2-a2-iu3 lai5 choe3 chhau2.  13). Tok-kang--e5 pek in kong2, Lin2 jit8-jit8 tioh8 choe3-oan5 lin2 e5 kang kap i2-cheng5 u7 chhau2 bo5 koh-iuN7.  14). Hoat-lo2 tok-kang--e5 phah i sou2 phai3 koan2-li2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 thau5-bak8, kong2, Lin2 cha7-jit8 kin-a-jit8 chaiN2-iuN7 bo5 choe3-oan5 lin2 e5 kang, chiau3 chiong5-cheng5 e5 siau3-giah8 choe3 chng ah?  15). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 thau5-bak8 lai5 tui3 Hoat-lo2 kiu5-kio3, kong2, SiaN2-su7 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8?  16). Bo5 eng7 chhau2 hou7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8, koh ka7 goan2 kong2, Tioh8 choe3-chng; khoaN3 ah, li2 e5 lou5-pok8 siu7-phah; sit8-chai7 si7 li2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 ke3-sit.  17). I kong2, Lin2 pin5-toaN7, lin2 pin5-toaN7; sou2-i2 lin2 kong2, Chun2 goan2 khi3 che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  18). TaN lin2 khi3 choe3-kang, chhau2 m7 hou7 lin2, chong2-si7 chng tioh8 chiau3-giah8 lai5 kau.  19). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 thau5-bak8 thiaN-kiN3 kong2, Jit8-jit8 choe3 chng e5 giah8 boe7 thang kiam2-chio2, chiu7 chai hai7 lah.  20). In li7-khui Hoat-lo2 chhut-lai5, tu2-tioh8 Mou5-se A-lun5 khia7 ti7 in e5 thau5-cheng5, chiu7 tui3 in kong2,  21). Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kam3-chhat lin2, sim2-phoaN3 lin2; in-ui7 lin2 hou7 goan2 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kap i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 chhau3-mia5, eng7 to he7 ti7 in e5 chhiu2 lai5 thai5 goan2.  22). Mou5-se to3-tng2-khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia, kong2, Chu2 ah, Li2 siaN2-su7 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 chit e5 peh-siN3? siaN2-su7 chhe goa2?  23). In-ui7 tui3 goa2 kiN3 Hoat-lo2, thok Li2 e5 mia5 lai5 kong2 e5 si5, i chiu7 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 chit e5 peh-siN3; Li2 ia7 long2 bo5 kiu3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3.

[6]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 sou2 beh kiaN5 ti7 Hoat-lo2--e5, taN li2 beh khoaN3-kiN3; in-ui7 eng7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, i beh chun2 in khi3, koh eng7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, i beh koaN2 in chhut i e5 toe7.
	2). Siong7-te3 koh tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  3). Goa2 mia5 choe3 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 chhut-hian7 ti7 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, chong2-si7 Goa2 e5 mia5 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa Goa2 be7 u7 hou7 in bat Goa2.  4). Goa2 koh kap in lip8 Goa2 kian-kou3 e5 iok, beh chiong in sou2 chhut-goa7 e5 Ka-lam5 toe7 siuN2-su3 in, chiu7-si7 in kia3-kha e5 toe7.  5). Goa2 ia7 thiaN-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hiN-hiN-chhan, chiu7-si7 Ai-kip8 lang5 tok in choe3 khou2-kang; Goa2 ia7 ki3-liam7 Goa2 e5 iok.  6). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Goa2 beh tui3 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 hou7 lin2 taN e5 tang7-taN3 chhoa7 lin2 chhut-lai5, koh beh kiu3 lin2 thoat-li7 in sou2 hou7 lin2 choe3 e5 khou2-kang.  Goa2 ia7 beh eng7 chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2 kap toa7 e5 sim2-phoaN3 kiu3-siok8 lin2.  7). Goa2 ia7 beh liah8 lin2 choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 ia7 beh choe3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3; lin2 beh chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, si7 tui3 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 hou7 lin2 taN e5 tang7-taN3 chhoa7 lin2 chhut-lai5.  8). Goa2 chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 beh hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok hit e5 toe7, Goa2 beh chhoa7 lin2 jip8 khi3 hia, chiong hit e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 lin2 choe3 giap8; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  9). Mou5-se chiong chit-e5 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2; chong2-si7 in ui7-tioh8 sim-lai7 iu-bun7, ia7 choe3 khou2-kang, m7-kheng2 thiaN Mou5-se.
	10). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  11). Li2 jip8--khi3 ka7 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 kong2, tioh8 chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut i e5 toe7.  12). Mou5-se ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 siong7-chhiaN2 m7-thiaN goa2, Hoat-lo2 thai2-tho2 beh thiaN goa2 chit-e5 chhui3-chih8 tun e5 lang5 ah?  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 tioh8 thoan5-beng7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2, thang chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7.
	14). I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 pang5-tiuN2 e5 mia5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; I2-sek-liat8 toa7-kiaN2 Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2; Hap-lok8, Hoat-lou7, Hi-su-lun5, Ka-bi2; chiah-e5 si7 Liu5-pian7 hiah e5 ke.  15). Se-bian7 e5 kiaN2; Ia5-bou2-li7, Nga2-bin2, O-hat, Nga2-kun, So2-hat, i2-kip8 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 sou2 siN e5 So3-lo5; chiah-e5 si7 Se-bian7 hiah e5 ke.  16). Li7-bi7 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5 chiau3 in e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; Kek-sun7, Ko-hat, Bi2-lah8-li7; Li7-bi7 hiong2-siu7 chit8-pah saN-chap8-chhit he3.  17). Kek-sun7 e5 kiaN2, chiau3 in e5 ka-chok8; Lip8-ni5, Si7-mui2.  18). Ko-hat e5 kiaN2; Am3-lan5, I2-su-hap, Hi-kek-lun5, OU-siat; Ko-hat hiong2-siu7 chit8-pah saN-chap8-saN he3.  19). Bi2-lah8-li7 e5 kiaN2; Boat8-li7, Bou2-si7.  Chiah-e5 si7 Li7-bi7 hiah e5 ke, chiau3 in e5 se3-he7.  20). Am3-lan5 chhoa7 i e5 kou, Iok-ki-piat, choe3-bou2; i ka7 i siN A-lun5 kap Mou5-se; Am3-lan5 hiong2-siu7 chit8-pah saN-chap8-chhit he3.  21). I2-su-hap e5 kiaN2; Kho2-lah8, Ni5-hui2, Se3-ki-li7.  22). OU-siat e5 kiaN2; Bi2-sa-li7, I2-li7-sat-hoan2, Se-the5-li7.  23). A-lun5 chhoa7 A-bi2-na2-tat8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Na2-sun7 e5 sio2-be7, I2-li7-sa-pa choe3 bou2; i ka7 i siN Na2-tap, A-pi2-hou7, I2-li7-a-sat, I2-tha-ma2.  24). Kho2-lah8 e5 kiaN2; A-sek, I2-li7-ka-na2, A-pi2-a-sat; chiah-e5 si7 Kho2-lah8 hiah e5 ke.  25). A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat chhoa7 Phou2-thiat chit8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3-bou2; i ka7 i siN Hui-ni5-hap.  Chiah-e5 si7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 pang5-tiuN2, chiau3 in e5 ka-chok8.  26). Chit e5 A-lun5 Mou5-se chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 in kong2, Tioh8 chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5.  27). Tui3 Ai-kip8 ong5, Hoat-lo2, kong2 beh chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 e5, chiu7-si7 chit e5 Mou5-se, A-lun5.
	28). Tng Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 tui3 Mou5-se kong2-oe7 e5 jit8,  29). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Goa2 tui3 li2 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, li2 long2 tioh8 ka7 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 kong2.  30). Mou5-se ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, goa2 si7 chhui3-chih8 tun e5 lang5, Hoat-lo2 thai2-tho2 beh thiaN goa2 ah?

[7]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 hou7 li2 tui3-ti7 Hoat-lo2 choe3 siong7-te3; li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 beh choe3 li2 e5 sian-ti.  2). KiN3-na7 Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2--e5, li2 long2 tioh8 kong2 i; li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 tioh8 tui3 Hoat-lo2 kong2, hou7 i chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut i e5 toe7.  3). Goa2 beh hou7 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, ia7 beh ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 kiaN5 Goa2 choe7-choe7 e5 sin5-jiah ki5-su7.  4). Chong2-si7 Hoat-lo2 bo5 beh thiaN lin2; Goa2 beh chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2 ti7 Ai-kip8, eng7 toa7 e5 sim2-phoaN3 chhoa7 Goa2 e5 kun-tui7, Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, chhut Ai-kip8 toe7.  5). Goa2 chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2 ti7 Ai-kip8, chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 in tiong-kan chhut-lai5 e5 si5, Ai-kip8 lang5 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  6). Mou5-se A-lun5 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5; Ia5-ho5-hoa chaiN2-iuN7 hoan-hu3 in, in chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.  7). In kap Hoat-lo2 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, Mou5-se poeh-chap8 he3, A-lun5 poeh-chap8-saN he3.
	8). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se tui3 A-lun5 kong2,  9). Hoat-lo2 na7 tui3 lin2 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 kiaN5 chit8 kiaN7 ki5-su7 lai5 khoaN3-mai7--cheh; li2 tioh8 tui3 A-lun5 kong2, Kiah8 li2 e5 koaiN2-a2 lai5 hiat ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 i piN3-choe3 choa5.  10). Mou5-se A-lun5 jip8--khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2, chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3--e5; A-lun5 chiong i e5 koaiN2-a2 hiat ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 bin7-cheng5, koaiN2-a2 chiu7 piN3-choe3 choa5.  11). Hoat-lo2 ia7 tiau3 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 kap sai-kong lai5, in si7 Ai-kip8 e5 phok-su7, ia7 eng7 in e5 sia5-sut8 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.  12). In tak8-lang5 hiat in e5 koaiN2-a2, long2 piN3-choe3 choa5; chong2-si7 A-lun5 e5 koaiN2-a2 thun in e5 koaiN2-a2.  13). Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, bo5 beh thiaN in, tu2-tu2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5.
	14). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Hoat-lo2 e5 sim kou3-chip, i m7-chun2 peh-siN3 khi3.  15). ThiN-kng-cha2 li2 khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2; khoaN3 ah, i chhut-khi3 chui2-piN; li2 tioh8 khia7 ti7 ho5-piN tan2-chih i; li2 e5 chhiu2 tioh8 kiah8 hit-ki piN3-choa5 e5 koaiN2-a2,  16). tui3 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa , Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 Siong7-te3, chhe goa2 lai5 kiN3 li2, kong2, Chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, thang ti7 khong3-ia2 hok8-sai7 Goa2; khoaN3 ah, kau3-taN li2 iau2-be7 u7 thiaN.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 beh tui3 chi2 chit8-kiaN7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; khoaN3 ah, goa2 beh eng7 goa2 chhiu2--nih e5 koaiN2-a2 phah ho5-tiong e5 chui2, chui2 chiu7 piN3-choe3 huih.  18). Ho5--nih e5 hi5 beh si2, ho5 ia7 beh chhau3-bi7; Ai-kip8 lang5 iam3-chian7 m7-ai3 lim ho5 e5 chui2.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 ka7 A-lun5 kong2, Kiah8 li2 e5 koaiN2-a2, chhun li2 e5 chhiu2 ti7 Ai-kip8 chiah e5 chui2 e5 teng2-bin7, chiu7-si7 ti7 in e5 kang, ho5, ti5, kap it-chhe3 e5 chui2-khut e5 teng2-bin7, hou7 in long2 piN3-choe3 huih; ti7 Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7, bo5-lun7 chha5 e5 khi3-ku7, chioh8 e5 khi3-ku7, long2 beh u7 huih.  20). Mou5-se A-lun5 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3; ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiah8-khi2 koaiN2-a2, phah ho5--nih e5 chui2; ho5--nih e5 chui2 long2 piN3-choe3 huih .  21). Ho5--nih e5 hi5 long2 si2; ho5 ia7 chhau3-bi7; Ai-kip8 lang5 boe7-oe7 lim ho5--nih e5 chui2; Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7 long2 u7 huih.  22). Ai-kip8 e5 phok-su7 ia7 eng7 in e5 sia5-sut8 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5; Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, m7-thiaN in; tu2-tu2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5.  23). Hoat-lo2 to3--khi3 i e5 kiong-lai7; chit e5 su7 i ia7 bo5 khoa3-sim.  24). Ai-kip8 lang5 ti7 ho5 e5 siang-peng5 kut8 toe7, ai3 tit-tioh8 chui2 thang lim; in-ui7 ho5 e5 chui2 in boe7 lim--tit.  25). Ia5-ho5-hoa phah ho5 liau2-au7 lek8-ke3 chhit-jit8.

[8]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 jip8--khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2, ka7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, thang hok8-sai7 Goa2.  2). Li2 na7 m7-chun2 in khi3, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 chhan5-kap-a2 phah-phaiN2 li2 e5 keng2-lai7.  3). Ho5 beh siN-thoaN3 chhan5-kap-a2, in beh chiuN7-lai5 jip8 li2 e5 kiong-tian7, li2 e5 khun3-pang5, chiuN7 li2 e5 bin5-chhng5, jip8 li2 e5 jin5-sin5 e5 chhu3, chiuN7 li2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 seng-khu, jip8 li2 e5 chau3-khang, kap li2 chhiau-mi7 e5 khi3-ku7.  4). Koh beh chiuN7 li2, kap li2 e5 peh-siN3, i2-kip8 li2 cheng3 jin5-sin5 e5 seng-khu.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 ka7 A-lun5 kong2, Li2 e5 chhiu2 kiah8 koaiN2-a2, chhun ti7 kang, ho5, ti5 e5 teng2-bin7, hou7 chhan5-kap-a2 chiuN7-lai5 Ai-kip8 toe7.  6). A-lun5 chiu7 chhun i e5 chhiu2 ti7 Ai-kip8 chiah e5 chui2 e5 teng2-bin7; chhan5-kap-a2 chiu7 chiuN7-lai5 jia-kham3 thong Ai-kip8 toe7.  7). Phok-su7 eng7 in e5 sia5-sut8 ia7 an2-ni kiaN5, hou7 chhan5-kap-a2 chiuN7-lai5 Ai-kip8 toe7.  8). Hoat-lo2 kio3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2, ChhiaN2 lin2 kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 chiah e5 chhan5-kap-a2 li7-khui goa2 kap goa2 e5 peh-siN3; goa2 chiu7 chun2 chit e5 peh-siN3 khi3 thang che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  9). Mou5-se tui3 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Goa2 chun-chhun5 li2 e5 i3-su3; goa2 tioh8 ui7 li2, kap li2 e5 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 li2 e5 peh-siN3, ki5-kiu5 ti7 sim2-mih8 si5 thang tu5-biat8 chhan5-kap-a2 li7-khui li2, kap li2 hiah e5 chhu3, chi2-u7 lau5 ti7 ho5--nih ah?  10). I kong2, Bin5-a2-jit8.  Kong2, Thang chiau3 li2 e5 oe7; hou7 li2 chai goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 chit8-e5 oe7 pi2-pheng7--tit.  11). Chhan5-kap-a2 beh li7-khui li2 kap li2 hiah e5 chhu3, kap li2 e5 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 li2 e5 peh-siN3, chi2-u7 lau5 ti7 ho5--nih.  12). Mou5-se A-lun5 li7-khui Hoat-lo2 chhut-khi3; Mou5-se ui7-tioh8 I sou2 chhe lai5 hai7 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhan5-kap-a2 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 chiau3 Mou5-se e5 oe7 lai5 kiaN5; kiN3-na7 ti7 chhu3-lai7, iN7-tiong, chhan5--nih e5 chhan5-kap-a2 long2 si2.  14). Lang5 khioh in kui-tui, pian3-toe7 long2 chhau3-bi7.  15). Hoat-lo2 khoaN3-kiN3 tai7-chi3 u7 khah-khoan, chiu7 ngi7 i e5 sim, m7-thiaN in; tu2-tu2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2 e5.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 ka7 A-lun5 kong2, Chhun-chhut li2 e5 koaiN2-a2, phah toe7--nih e5 thou5-hun2, hou7 i ti7 Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7 piN3-choe3 sat-bu2.  17). In chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5; A-lun5 kiah8 koaiN2-a2, chhun-chhiu2 phah toe7--nih e5 thou5-hun2, chiu7 ti7 lang5 kap cheng-siN e5 seng-khu long2 u7 sat-bu2; toe7--nih e5 thou5-hun2 ti7 Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7 long2 pian3-choe3 sat-bu2.  18). Phok-su7 ia7 eng7 in e5 sia5-sut8 chiau3 an2-ni choe3, ai3 siN-chhut sat-bu2, chong2-si7 boe7-oe7; an2-ni ti7 lang5 kap cheng-siN e5 seng-khu long2 u7 sat-bu2.  19). Phok-su7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Che si7 Siong7-te3 e5 chhiu2-toaN7; Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, m7-thiaN in; tu2-tu2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2 e5.
	20). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 chheng-cha2 khi2-lai5; khoaN3 ah, Hoat-lo2 beh kau3 chui2-piN; li2 khia7 ti7 i e5 bin7-thau5-cheng5, ka7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, thang hok8-sai7 Goa2.  21). Li2 na7 m7-chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, Goa2 beh chhe kui-tin7 e5 hou5-sin5 kau3 ti7 li2, kap li2 e5 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 li2 e5 peh-siN3, ia7 beh jip8 li2 hiah e5 chhu3; koh Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 chhu3, kap in sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, long2 beh u7 kui-tin7 e5 hou5-sin5 moa2-moa2.  22). Tng hit-jit8, Goa2 beh hun-piat Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 Ko-san toe7, ti7-hia bo5 beh u7 kui-tin7 e5 hou5-sin5; thang hou7 li2 chai Goa2 ti7 thiN-e7-tiong choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  23). Goa2 beh hun-piat Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 kap li2 e5 peh-siN3; bin5-a2-chai3 beh u7 chit e5 sin5-jiah.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kiaN5; chiu7 u7 hou5-sin5 kui toa7-tin7 lai5 jip8 Hoat-lo2 e5 kiong-tian7 kap i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 chhu3, kap Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7; toe7 in-ui7 chit e5 kui-tin7 e5 hou5-sin5 siu7 pai7-hoai7.  25). Hoat-lo2 kio3 Mou5-se A-lun5 lai5, kong2, Lin2 khi3, ti7 chit e5 toe7 che3-su7 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  26). Mou5-se kong2, An2-ni kiaN5 bo5 hap8-gi5; in-ui7 goan2 beh eng7 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 iam3-ouN3 e5 mih8 che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goan2 e5 Siong7-te3; goan2 na7 ti7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, eng7 in sou2 iam3-ouN3 e5 mih8 lai5 hian3-che3, in kiam2 bo5 beh eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 goan2 mah?  27). Goan2 beh khi3 khong3-ia2, kiaN5 saN-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7, che3-su7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiau3 I sou2 beh hoan-hu3 goan2.  28). Hoat-lo2 kong2, Goa2 beh chun2 lin2 khi3, ti7 khong3-ia2 che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3; tok8-tok8 m7-thang khi3 hng7; lin2 tioh8 thoe3 goa2 ki5-to2.  29). Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 beh tui3 li2 chia chhut-khi3 ia7 beh kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 kui-tin7 e5 hou5-sin5 bin5-a2-jit8 li7-khui Hoat-lo2, kap i e5 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 i e5 peh-siN3; chong2-si7 Hoat-lo2 m7-thang koh khui2-cha3, m7-chun2 peh-siN3 khi3 che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  30). Mou5-se chiu7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 hia chhut-khi3, ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  31). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 chiau3 Mou5-se e5 oe7 kiaN5, hou7 kui-tin7 e5 hou5-sin5 li7-khui Hoat-lo2, kap i e5 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 i e5 peh-siN3; bo5 lau5 chit8-chiah.  32). Chit-pai2 Hoat-lo2 koh ngi7 i e5 sim, m7-chun2 peh-siN3 khi3.

[9]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 jip8--khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2, ka7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa, Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, thang hok8-sai7 Goa2.  2). Li2 na7 m7-kheng2 hou7 in khi3, iu5-goan5 bian2-kiong2 lau5 in,  3). khoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 beh chhun ti7 li2 chhan5--nih e5 cheng-siN, be2, lu5, lok8-to5, gu5-kun5, iuN5-kun5; beh u7 tang7 e5 un-ek8.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hun-piat I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng-siN kap Ai-kip8 e5 cheng-siN; hoan7-na7 siok8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5, bo5 si2 chit8-chiah.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tiaN7-tioh8 si5-ki5, kong2, Bin5-a2-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 chit e5 toe7 kiaN5 chit e5 su7.  6). Keh-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 kiaN5 chit e5 su7; Ai-kip8 e5 cheng-siN long2-chong2 si2; chong2-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 cheng-siN long2 bo5 si2 chit8-chiah.  7). Hoat-lo2 chhe lang5 khi3, khoaN3 ah, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 cheng-siN, lian5 chit8-chiah ia7 bo5 si2.  Chong2-si7 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim kou3-chip, m7-chun2 peh-siN3 khi3.
	8). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 put kui2-na7 phong2 lou5--nih e5 he2-hu, Mou5-se tioh8 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ng3-thiN ia7--khi3;  9). beh ti7 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 piN3-choe3 tin5-ai; ti7 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7, ti7 lang5 kap cheng-siN e5 seng-khu, long2 siN liap8-a2, chiaN5-choe3 chhng.  10). In chiu7 put lou5--nih e5 he2-hu, khia7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5; Mou5-se ng3-thiN ia7--khi3, chiu7 ti7 lang5 kap cheng-siN e5 seng-khu siN liap8-a2, chiaN5-choe3 chhng.  11). Phok-su7 in-ui7 liap8-a2 ti7 Mou5-se e5 bin7-cheng5 khia7-boe7-tiau5; in-ui7 phok-su7 kap it-chhe3 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 seng-khu long2 u7 hit-ho7 liap8-a2.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, ti3-kau3 m7-thiaN in; tu2-tu2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se sou2 kong2 e5.
	13). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 chheng-cha2 khi2-lai5, khia7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa, Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, hou7 in thang hok8-sai7 Goa2.  14). In-ui7 chi2-chit8-pai2 Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 chai-e7 kau3 ti7 li2 e5 sim, kap li2 e5 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 li2 e5 peh-siN3, hou7 li2 chai ti7 phou2-thiN-e7 bo5 chit8-e5 oe7 pi2-pheng7 Goa2.  15). Goa2 na7 chhun-chhiu2, eng7 un-ek8 kong-kek li2 kap li2 e5 peh-siN3, li2 chiu7 i2-keng biat8 ti7 toe7-chiuN7;  16). chong2-si7 Goa2 hou7 li2 khia7-chai7, si7 tiau5-kou3-i3 beh eng7 li2 hian2-beng5 Goa2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5, hou7 Goa2 e5 mia5 po3-iong5 ti7 pian3-toe7-chiuN7.  17). Li2 iau2-ku2 tui3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 chu7-ko, m7-chun2 in khi3 mah?  18). KhoaN3 ah, bin5-a2-jit8 chiong-kun7 chit-si5, Goa2 beh loh8 toa7-phauh8, tui3 Ai-kip8 khai-kok i2-lai5 be7-bat u7 an2-ni.  19). TaN li2 tioh8 chhe lang5, chiong li2 e5 cheng-siN kap li2 chhan5--nih it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5, pek in jip8--lai5; hoan7-na7 ti7 chhan5--nih, bo5 siu to3--lai5 ke--nih-e5, bo5-lun7 lang5 kap cheng-siN, phauh8 beh loh8 ti7 in e5 sin-chiuN7, in chiu7 beh si2.  20). Hoat-lo2 jin5-sin5 e5 tiong-kan, kiaN-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 e5, chiu7 hou7 i e5 lou5-pok8 kap cheng-siN chau2 jip8 chhu3-lai7;  21). chong2-si7 hit-e5 bo5 liah8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 choe3 iau3-kin2 e5, chiu7 chiong i e5 lou5-pok8 kap cheng-siN lau5 ti7 chhan5--nih.
	22). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 ng3-thiN chhun-chhiu2, hou7 phauh8 loh8 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 pian3-toe7, phah lang5 kap cheng-siN, i2-kip8 chhan5--nih e5 chhai3-soe, thong Ai-kip8 toe7 long2 an2-ni.  23). Mou5-se ng3-thiN chhun-chhut i e5 koaiN2-a2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 khi2-lui5 loh8-phauh8, u7 he2 kiaN5 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7; Ia5-ho5-hoa loh8-phauh8 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7.  24). Tui3 an2-ni u7 phauh8 , ia7 u7 he2 chham ti7 phauh8 e5 lai7-bin7, chin li7-hai7; tui3 Ai-kip8 khai-kok i2-lai5 pian3-toe7 be7 bat u7 an2-ni.  25). Ti7 Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7, kiN3-na7 ti7 chhan5--nih-e5, bo5-lun7 lang5 a2-si7 cheng-siN, long2 hou7 phauh8 phah; phauh8 ia7 phah chhan5--nih it-chhe3 e5 chhai3-soe, koh phah-chih8 chhan5--nih it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7-bak8.  26). Tok8-tok8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 tiam3 e5 Ko-san toe7 bo5 loh8-phauh8.  27). Hoat-lo2 chhe lang5 kio3 Mou5-se A-lun5 lai5, ka7 in kong2, Chi2-chit8-pai2 goa2 u7 hoan7-choe7; Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kong-gi7, goa2 kap goa2 e5 peh-siN3 si7 phaiN2.  28). TaN chiah e5 chhe3-lui5 kap phauh8 i2-keng kau3-giah8 lah; kiu5 lin2 ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; goa2 chiu7 chun2 lin2 khi3, m7-bian2 koh tiam3 chia.  29). Mou5-se ka7 i kong2, Goa2 chit8-e7 chhut-siaN5 chiu7 beh ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiah8-khi2 goa2 siang ki chhiu2; lui5 beh soah, phauh8 ia7 bo5 koh loh8; hou7 li2 chai choan5-toe7 long2 siok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  30). Chong2-si7 lun7-kau3 li2 kap li2 e5 jin5-sin5, goa2 chai lin2 iau2 si7 bo5 kiaN-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3.  31). Hit-si5 moa5 kap toa7-beh8 siu7 phah-phaiN2; in-ui7 toa7-beh8 i2-keng chhut-sui7, moa5 ia7 khui-hoe.  32). Tok8-tok8 sio2-beh8 kap chhou-beh8 bo5 siu7 phah-phaiN2; in-ui7 iau2-be7 toa7-chang5.  33). Mou5-se li7-khui Hoat-lo2 chhut-siaN5, kiah8-khi2 siang-chhiu2 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lui5 kap phauh8 chiu7 soah, hou7 ia7 bo5 koh piaN3-loh8 toe7.  34). Hoat-lo2 khoaN3-kiN3 hou7, phauh8, kap lui5 long2 soah, chiu7 it-hoat hoan7-choe7; i kap i e5 jin5-sin5 long2 ngi7-sim.  35). Hoat-lo2 sim ngi7, m7-chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khi3, tu2-tu2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se sou2 kong2 e5.

[10]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 jip8-khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2; in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng hou7 i e5 sim, kap i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 sim, kong-ngi7, thang hou7 Goa2 hian2-beng5 Goa2 chiah e5 sin5-jiah ti7 in tiong-kan;  2). ia7 beh hou7 li2 chiong Goa2 sou2 choe3 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 su7, kap Goa2 ti7 in tiong-kan sou2 kiaN5 chiah e5 sin5-jiah, thoan5 hou7 li2 e5 kiaN2 kap li2 e5 sun thiaN, thang hou7 lin2 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  3). Mou5-se A-lun5 chiu7 khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2, ka7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa, Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 Siong7-te3, an2-ni kong2, Li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 m7-kheng2 ka-ki7 khiam-pi, beh kau3 sim2-mih8 si5 ah? tioh8 chun2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, hou7 in hok8-sai7 Goa2.  4). Li2 na7 m7-kheng2 hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 khi3, khoaN3 ah, bin5-a-jit8 Goa2 beh hou7 chhau2-meh jip8 li2 e5 keng2-lai7;  5). in beh jia-kham3 toe7-bin7, ti3-kau3 boe7 khoaN3-kiN3 thou5; koh beh chiah8 hit-e5 tui3 chai-e7 sou2-chhun--e5, chiu7-si7 phauh8 sou2 phah bo5 liau2 e5; ia7 beh chiah8 chhan5--nih ui7 lin2 sou2 hoat it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7-bak8;  6). chhau2-meh beh chhiong-moa2 li2 e5 chhu3, kap li2 e5 cheng3 jin5-sin5 e5 chhu3, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 chhu3, tui3 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap li2 e5 chou2-kong chhut-si3 kau3 taN, be7-bat khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ni.  Mou5-se chiu7 oat8-tng2-sin, li7-khui Hoat-lo2 chhut-khi3.  7). Hoat-lo2 e5 jin5-sin5 tui3 i kong2, Chit lang5 choe3 lan2 e5 lo5-bang7, beh kau3 sim2-mih8 si5 ah? tioh8 chun2 chiah e5 lang5 khi3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3; Ai-kip8 i2-keng pai7-hoai7, li2 kiam2 m7-chai mah?  8). Tui3 an2-ni, Mou5-se A-lun5 siu7 tiau3 to3-tng2--lai5 kiN3 Hoat-lo2; Hoat-lo2 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 khi3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3; tok8-tok8 hiah-e5 beh-khi3--e5, si7 sim2-mih8 ho7 lang5 ah?  9). Mou5-se kong2, Goan2 beh kap goan2 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 lau7-lang5 khi3, ia7 beh toa3 goan2 e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, kap goan2 e5 iuN5-kun5 gu5-kun5 choe3 chit8-e7 khi3; in-ui7 goan2 tioh8 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 choeh.  10). Hoat-lo2 tui3 in kong2, Ho2--lah, goa2 chun2 lin2 kap lin2 e5 gin2-a2 khi3 lah, goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap lin2 ti7-teh; lin2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, chai-e7 ti7 lin2 bak8-chiu-cheng5 lah;  11). an2-ni boe7-choe3--tit; lin2 chiah e5 toa7-lang5 thang khi3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 che si7 lin2 sou2 kiu5 e5.  Chiu7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2 in chhut-khi3.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 chhun-chhiu2 ki2 Ai-kip8 toe7, hou7 chhau2-meh chiuN7-lai5 Ai-kip8 toe7, chiah8 toe7--nih it-chhe3 e5 chhai3-soe, chiu7-si7 phauh8 phah bo5 liau2 e5.  13). Mou5-se chiu7 chhun i e5 koaiN2-a2, ki2 Ai-kip8 toe7; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 hou7 tang-hong thong-jit8 thong-mi5 chhe ti7 toe7--nih; kau3 bin5-a2-cha2-khi2, tang-hong chiu7 chiong chhau2-meh chhe--lai5.  14). Chhau2-meh chiuN7-lai5 Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7, hioh ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 si3-keng2, li7-hai7 kau3-kek8; chiong-cheng5 bo5 u7 an2-ni e5 chhau2-meh, i2-au7 ia7 bo5 beh an2-ni;  15). in-ui7 in jia-kham3 choan5-toe7, ti3-kau3 toe7 long2 ou-am3; koh chiah8 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 chhai3-soe, kap chhiu7--nih e5 ke2-chi2, phauh8 sou2 phah bo5 liau2 e5.  Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7, bo5-lun7 chhiu7-bak8, a2-si7 chhan5--nih e5 chhai3-soe, bo5 lau5 chit8-hang7 chhiN-chhui3 e5 mih8.  16). Tui3 an2-ni Hoat-lo2 koaN2-kin2 kio3 Mou5-se A-lun5 lai5, kong2, Goa2 tek-choe7 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ia7 tek-choe7 lin2.  17). TaN kiu5 li2, kan-ta chi2-chit8-pai2 sia3-bian2 goa2 e5 choe7, kiu5 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, hou7 goa2 thoat-li7 chi2-chit8-pai2 e5 si2-bo5.  18). Mou5-se chiu7 li7-khui Hoat-lo2, khi3 kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tng2 chin-thau3 e5 sai-hong chiong chhau2-meh chhe--khi2-lai5, koaN2-jip8 Ang5-hai2; ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 si3-keng2 bo5 lau5 chit8-chiah chhau2-meh.  20). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, m7-chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khi3.
	21). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 chhun-chhiu2 ng3-thiN, hou7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ou-am3, chit e5 ou-am3 kau3 oe7-bong-tit.  22). Mou5-se chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 ng3 thiN, Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7 chiu7 saN-jit8 ku2 ou-ou am3-am3;  23). saN-jit8 ku2 lang5 boe7 khoaN3-kiN3 lang5, ia7 bo5 khi2-lai5 li7-khui i e5 sou2-chai7; tok8-tok8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 chhu3 long2 u7 kng.  24). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 kio3 Mou5-se lai5 kong2, Lin2 khi3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tok8-tok8 si7 lin2 e5 iuN5-kun5 gu5-kun5 tioh8 lau5-teh, lin2 e5 gin2-a2 chiu7 thang kap lin2 saN-kap khi3.  25). Mou5-se kong2, Li2 ia7 tioh8 chiong seng-le2 kap sio-che3 e5 mih8 kau goan2 e5 chhiu2, hou7 goan2 thang che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3.  26). Goan2 e5 cheng-siN ia7 tioh8 kap goan2 khi3, lian5 chit8-chiah ia7 m7 lau5-teh; in-ui7 goan2 tioh8 tui3 hit tiong-kan chhu2 i, lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3; koh goan2 iau2-be7 kau3 hia m7-chai tioh8 eng7 sim2-mih8 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  27). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, m7-kheng2 hou7 in khi3.  28). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 li7-khui goa2 khi3; li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7 ka-ki7, m7-thang koh kiN3 goa2 e5 bin7; in-ui7 li2 kiN3 goa2 e5 bin7, hit-jit8 li2 oe7 si2.  29). Mou5-se kong2, Li2 an2-ni kong2, ho2; goa2 bo5 beh koh kiN3 li2 e5 bin7 lah.

[11]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 beh koh hou7 chit8-hang7 chai-e7 kau3 ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap Ai-kip8, jian5-au7 i beh chun2 lin2 li7-khui chia; i chun2 lin2 khi3 e5 si5 beh koaN2 lin2 long2 tui3 chia chhut-khi3.  2). Li2 tioh8 thoan5 hou7 peh-siN3 thiaN, hou7 in lam5-lu2 tak8-lang5 tui3 in e5 chhu3-piN tho2 kim-khi3, gun5-khi3.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 peh-siN3 tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5; koh Mou5-se chit-lang5 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, ti7 Hoat-lo2 jin5-sin5 e5 bak8-chiu-tiong, kap peh-siN3 e5 bak8-chiu-tiong, khoaN3-choe3 chun-toa7.
	4). Mou5-se kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Iok-liok8 poaN3-mi5, Goa2 beh chhut-khi3 pian3 kiaN5 Ai-kip8.  5). KiN3-na7 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 toa7-kiaN2, tui3 che7-ui7 e5 Hoat-lo2 e5 toa7-kiaN2, kau3 ti7 oe-bo7 e5 lu2-pi7 e5 toa7-kiaN2, kap it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN thau5-chui2-siN--e5, long2 beh si2.  6). Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7 beh u7 toa7 thi5-khau3 e5 siaN, chiong-cheng5 be7 bat u7 an2-ni, au7-lai5 ia7 bo5 koh an2-ni.  7). Lun7-kau3 I2-sek-liat8-tiong, bo5-lun7 si7 lang5 si7 cheng-siN, lian5 kau2 ia7 m7-kaN2 pui7 in; hou7 lin2 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Ai-kip8 lang5 kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 hun-piat in.  8). Li2 hiah e5 jin5-sin5, long2 beh loh8 lai5 kiN3 goa2, phak ti7 goa2 bin7-cheng5, kong2, Kiu5 li2 kap kun-te3 li2 e5 peh-siN3 long2 chhut-khi3; jian5-au7 goa2 beh chhut-khi3.  Tui3 an2-ni Mou5-se toa7 siu7-khi3, li7-khui Hoat-lo2 chhut-khi3.
	9). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Hoat-lo2 bo5 beh thiaN lin2, hou7 Goa2 e5 ki5-su7 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ke-thiN na2 choe7.  10). Mou5-se A-lun5 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiaN5 che it-chhe3 e5 ki5-su7; chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, m7-chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 li7-khui i e5 toe7.

[12]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 tui3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  2). Chit geh8 tioh8 choe3 lin2 e5 chiaN-geh8, choe3 ni5-ni5 e5 thau5-chit8-geh8.  3). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 choan5-hoe7 kong2, Pun2-geh8 chhoe-chap8 jit8, tak8-lang5 tioh8 chiau3 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, chhu2 iuN5-a2, chit8-ke chit8-chiah.  4). Na7 si7 chit8-ke e5 lang5 siuN-chio2, chit8-chiah iuN5-a2 chiah8-boe7-liau2, i tioh8 kap keh-piah e5 chhu3-piN, chiau3 lang5-giah8, saN-kap chhu2 chit8-chiah; lin2 pi7-pan7 iuN5-a2, tioh8 an3-sng3 tak8-lang5 sou2 oe7 chiah8 e5 liong7.  5). Lin2 e5 iuN5-a2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2; lin2 tioh8 tui3 mi5-iuN5-tiong, a2-si7 soaN-iuN5-tiong, chhu2 i, long2 thang;  6). lin2 tioh8 lau5 kau3 pun2-geh8 chap8-si3 jit8, hong5-hun e5 si5, I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 e5 cheng3-lang5 tioh8 thai5 iuN5-a2.  7). In tioh8 chhu2 tam7-poh8 huih, boah ti7 chiah8 iuN5-a2 hit keng chhu3, siang-peng5 e5 mng5-khia7 kap mng5-bai5.  8). Hit-mi5 tioh8 chiah8 iuN5-a2 e5 bah, eng7 he2 pek i, kap bo5-kaN3-piaN2 khou2-chhai3 chham-teh chiah8.  9). M7-thang chhiN-chhiN chiah8, koat-toan3 m7-thang eng7 chui2 chu2, tioh8 eng7 he2 pek; thau5, kha, kap ngou2-chong7 long2 tioh8 chiah8.  10). Long2 m7-thang lau5 ke3 cha2-khi2, na7 lau5 kau3 ke3 cha2-khi2 tioh8 eng7 he2 sio.  11). Lin2 tioh8 an2-ni chiah8 i; io ha5-toa3, kha chheng7-oe5, chhiu2 kiah8 koaiN2-a2, ia7 tioh8 koaN2-kin2 chiah8; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 poaN5-ke3-choeh.  12). In-ui7 hit-mi5 Goa2 beh pian3-kiaN5 Ai-kip8 toe7, phah-si2 Ai-kip8 toe7 it-chhe3 thau5-chiuN7-siN-e5, bo5-lun7 lang5 kap cheng-siN; koh beh sim2-phoaN3 Ai-kip8 it-chhe3 e5 siong7-te3; Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  13). Chit e5 huih ti7 lin2 sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 chhu3, beh choe3 lin2 e5 ki3-ho7; Goa2 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 huih, chiu7 tui3 lin2 poaN5-ke3--khi3; Goa2 phah Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si5, chai-e7 bo5 kau3 ti7 lin2, lai5 biat8 lin2.  14). Lin2 tioh8 eng7 chit-jit8 choe3 ki3-liam7, siu2 i choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 choeh; lin2 tioh8 tai7-tai7 siu2 chit e5 choeh, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 le7.  15). Lin2 tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2 chhit-jit8 ku2; thau5-chit8-jit8 tioh8 tui3 lin2 tak8 keng chhu3 tu5--khi3 kaN3; in-ui7 tui3 thau5-chit8 jit8 kau3 te7-chhit jit8, hoan7-na7 chiah8 u7 kaN3 e5, beh tui3 I2-sek-liat8-tiong tu5--khi3.  16). Thau5-chit8 jit8 lin2 tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7, chhit-jit8 ia7 tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7; chi2 nng7-jit8, tu5--khi3 pi7-pan7 tak8-lang5 sou2 tioh8 chiah8 e5 i2-goa7, bo5-lun7 sim2-mih8 kang long2 m7-thang choe3.  17). Lin2 tioh8 siu2 bo5-kaN3-choeh; in-ui7 Goa2 tu2-tu2 ti7 hit-jit8 chhoa7 lin2 e5 kun-tui7 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhut-lai5; sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 siu2 chit-jit8, tak8 se3-tai7 choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 le7.  18). Tui3 chiaN-geh8 chap8-si3 e5-hng kau3 ji7-it e5-hng, lin2 tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2.  19). Ti7 lin2 tak8 keng chhu3, chhit-jit8-lai7 m7-thang u7 kaN3; in-ui7 kiN3-na7 chiah8 u7 kaN3 e5 mih8, bo5-lun7 si7 kia3-kha-e5, a2-si7 pun2-toe7-e5, hit-lang5 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 hoe7-tiong tu5--khi3.  20). U7-kaN3 e5 mih8, lin2 long2 m7-thang chiah8; ti7 lin2 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2.
	21). Mou5-se chiu7 kio3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3 tiuN2-lo2 lai5, ka7 in kong2, Lin2 tak8-lang5 tioh8 chiau3 ke-khau2 chhu2 iuN5-a2, thai5 i choe3 poaN5-ke3-choeh.  22). Lin2 tioh8 theh8 chit8-pe2 e5 gu5-chhek-chhau2, un3 phun5-lai7 e5 huih, eng7 phun5-lai7 e5 huih boah mng5-bai5, kap siang-peng5 e5 mng5-khia7; lin2 bo5-lun7 sim2-mih8 lang5 m7-thang tui3 i e5 chhu3 chhut-mng5, tit8-kau3 bin5-a2-cha2-khi2.  23). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh pian3-kiaN5, phah-si2 Ai-kip8 lang5; I khoaN3-kiN3 huih ti7 mng5-bai5, kap siang-peng5 e5 mng5-khia7, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 beh poaN5-ke3 hit e5 mng5, m7-chun2 biat8 siN3-mia7-e5 jip8 lin2 e5 chhu3, lai5 phah-si2 lin2.  24). Chit e5 su7, lin2 tioh8 siu2 i, choe3 lin2 kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-sun eng2-oan2 e5 le7.  25). Au7-lai5 lin2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 I sou2 eng3-un2 siuN2-su3 lin2 hit e5 toe7, chiu7 tioh8 siu2 chit e5 le2.  26). Lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 na7 mng7 lin2, Ui7 siaN2-su7 kiaN5 chit e5 le2?  27). lin2 chiu7 tioh8 kong2, Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa poaN5-ke3-choeh e5 che3; tng I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 si5, I phah-si2 Ai-kip8 lang5, poaN5-ke3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 chhu3, kiu3 lan2 tak8-ke.  Tui3 an2-ni peh-siN3 aN3-thau5 keng3-pai3.  28). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 khi3 an2-ni kiaN5; Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5--e5, in chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.
	29). Kau3 poaN3-mi5 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiong Ai-kip8 toe7 sou2 u7 e5 toa7-kiaN2, chiu7-si7 tui3 che7-ui7 e5 Hoat-lo2 e5 toa7-kiaN2 kau3 kaN-hoan7 e5 toa7-kiaN2, i2-kip8 thau5-chui2-siN e5 cheng-siN, it-chin7 thai5-si2.  30). Hoat-lo2 kap it-chhe3 e5 jin5-sin5, kap Ai-kip8 e5 cheng3-lang5, mi5-si5 long2 khi2-lai5; ti7 Ai-kip8 u7 toa7 thi5-khau5 e5 siaN, in-ui7 bo5 chit8-ke bo5 si2-lang5.  31). Hoat-lo2 thau3-mi5 tiau3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2, Khi2--lai5, kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tioh8 tui3 goa2 e5 peh-siN3 tiong-kan chhut-khi3, chiau3 lin2 sou2 kong2 e5, khi3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  32). ia7 chiau3 lin2 sou2 kong2 e5, lian5 iuN5-kun5 gu5-kun5 toa3-toa3 khi3; ia7 tioh8 ka7 goa2 chiok-hok.  33). Ai-kip8 lang5 pek peh-siN3; kah in kin2-kin2 chhut in e5 toe7, kong2, Goan2 long2 si2--lah.  34). Peh-siN3 chiu7 theh8 bo5-kaN3 e5 chhiN-mi7, chiong chhiau-mi7 e5 khi3-ku7 pau ti7 saN-lai7, pe7 ti7 keng-thau5-teng2.  35). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 Mou5-se e5 oe7 kiaN5, tui3 Ai-kip8 tho2 gun5-khi3 kim-khi3 kap i-chiuN5.  36). Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 peh-siN3 tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiau3 in sou2-tho2--e5 hou7 in; tui3 an2-ni in chhiuN2 Ai-kip8 lang5.
	37). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Lan5-sek khi3 Sou-kat, tu5 gin2-a2 i2-goa7, pou7-kiaN5 e5 toa7-lang5 iok u7 lak8-chap8-ban7.  38). Koh u7 choe7-choe7 chap8-chok8 e5 lang5, ia7 u7 iuN5-kun5 gu5-kun5 choe7-choe7 cheng-siN kap in chiuN7-khi3.  39). In eng7 Ai-kip8 toa3--chhut-lai5 e5 chhiN-mi7 pek-choe3 bo5-kaN3-piaN2; bo5 hoat-kaN3, si7 in-ui7 siu7-pek chhut Ai-kip8, boe7-oe7 ian5-chhian5-tit, ia7 bo5 ui7 ka-ki7 pi7-pan7 sim2-mih8 chiah8-mih8.  40). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut-goa7 ti7 Ai-kip8 si3-pah saN-chap8 ni5.  41). Kau3 si3-pah saN-chap8 ni5 moa2, tu2-tu2 hit-jit8, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kun-tui7 long2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhut-lai5.  42). Chit-mi5 tioh8 ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa siu2 i, in-ui7 I chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 toe7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mi5, si7 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3 lang5 tai7-tai7 sou2 tioh8 siu2--e5.
	43). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2, PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 le7 si7 an2-ni;  44). goa7-pang lang5 long2 m7-thang chiah8 i; tok8-tok8 tak8-lang5 eng7 gun5 boe2 e5 lou5-pok8, i2-keng ka7 i kiaN5 kat-le2, chiu7 thang chiah8.  45). Kia3-kha-e5 kap chhiaN3-kang lang5 long2 m7-thang chiah8.  46). Tioh8 ti7 chit8 keng chhu3 chiah8 i, chit8 te3 bah ia7 m7-thang toa3-chhut chhu3-goa7; i e5 kut chit8-ki ia7 m7-thang phah-chih8.  47). I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 long2 tioh8 siu2 i.  48). Na7 u7 goa7-chok8 lang5 chhut-goa7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, ai3 siu2 poaN5-ke3-choeh lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, i sou2-u7 e5 ta-pou-lang5 tioh8 siu7 kat-le2, jian5-au7 i thang lai5 siu2, chiu7 kap pun2-chok8 e5 lang5 bo5 koh-iuN7; chong2-si7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5, long2 m7-thang chiah8 i.  49). Pun2-chok8 e5 lang5 kap goa7-chok8 e5 lang5 chhut-goa7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, long2 tang5-chit8-iuN7 e5 le7.  50). I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 e5 khi3 choe3.  51). Tng hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7, chhut Ai-kip8 toe7.

[13]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). I2-sek-liat8-tiong, bo5-lun7 lang5 kap cheng-siN, kiN3-na7 thau5-chiuN7 e5 toa7-kiaN2, long2 tioh8 hun-piat choe3-seng3, kui ti7 Goa2; in-ui7 pun2 si7 Goa2 e5.
	3). Mou5-se ka7 peh-siN3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 ki3-liam7 chit-jit8, chiu7-si7 lin2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7, tui3 choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke, chhut-lai5; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 chhoa7 lin2 tui3 chia chhut; u7 kaN3 e5 piaN2 long2 m7-thang chiah8.  4). Ti7 A-pit geh8-kan, chit-jit8 si7 lin2 chhut-lai5 e5 jit8.  5). Chiong-lai5 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhoa7 lin2 jip8 Ka-lam5, Hek, A-mou5-li7, Hi-bi7, Ia5-pou3-su, hiah e5 chok8 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 tui3 li2 e5 chou2-kong chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 hou7 li2, hit e5 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7, hit-si5 li2 tioh8 ti7 chit-geh8-kan siu2 chit e5 le2.  6). Li2 tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2 chhit-jit8; kau3 te7-chhit jit8 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 choeh.  7). Chi2 chhit-jit8 ku2 tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2; ti7 li2 e5 si3-keng2 lai7, m7-thang khoaN3-kiN3 li2 u7 he7-kaN3 e5 piaN2, ia7 m7-thang khoaN3-kiN3 li2 u7 kaN3-bu2.  8). Tng hit-jit8, li2 tioh8 ka7 li2 e5 kiaN2 kong2, Che si7 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 goa2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 si5, sou2 ka7 goa2 kiaN5 e5 su7.  9). Che beh ka7 li2 choe3 ki3-ho7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, choe3 ki3-liam7 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-hiah8; hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lut8-hoat siong5-siong5 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bat eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 chhoa7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8;  10). sou2-i2 tak8-ni5 kau3-ki5 li2 tioh8 siu2 chit e5 le7.
	11). Chiong-lai5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chiau3 I tui3 li2 kap li2 e5 chou2-kong sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5, chhoa7 li2 jip8 Ka-lam5 lang5 e5 toe7, chiong chit e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 li2;  12). hit-si5 li2 tioh8 chiong it-chhe3 thau5-thai e5 ta-pou-kiaN2 kap sou2 u7 thau5-chui2 kang e5 cheng-siN, kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; chiah-e5 long2 siok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  13). KiN3-na7 thau5-chui2-siN e5 lu5, tioh8 eng7 iuN5-a2 thoe3-siok8; na7 bo5 beh thoe3-siok8, chiu7 tioh8 kong3-chih8 i e5 am7-kun2; kiN3-na7 li2 thau5-chiuN7 e5 ta-pou-kiaN2 long2 tioh8 thoe3-siok8.  14). Jit8-au7 li2 e5 kiaN2 mng7 li2 kong2, Che si7 sim2-mih8 ian5-kou3? li2 tioh8 tui3 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, chhoa7 goan2 tui3 Ai-kip8, tui3 choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke, chhut-lai5.  15). Hit-si5 Hoat-lo2 kou3-chip m7-chun2 goan2 khi3, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 chiong Ai-kip8 toe7 sou2-u7 thau5-thai-e5, bo5-lun7 si7 lang5 e5 toa7-kiaN2, a2-si7 cheng-siN e5 thau5-chui2-e5, long2 hai7-si2; in-ui7 an2-ni, goa2 chiong thau5-chui2 e5 kang-e5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3-che3; tok8-tok8 goa2 e5 toa7-kiaN2 long2 eng7 thoe3-siok8.  16). Che beh choe3 ki3-ho7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, choe3 ki3-liam7 ha5 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-hiah8; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, chhoa7 goan2 tui3 Ai-kip8 chhut-lai5.
	17). Hoat-lo2 chun2 peh-siN3 khi3 e5 si5, Hui-li7-su7 toe7 e5 lou7 sui-jian5 khah-kun7, chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 bo5 chhoa7 in tui3 hia khi3; in-ui7 Siong7-te3 kong2, KiaN-liau2 peh-siN3 tu2-tioh8 kau-chian3, chiu7 the3-hoe2, to3-tng2-khi3 Ai-kip8.  18). Sou2-i2 Siong7-te3 chhoa7 peh-siN3 oan tui3 Ang5-hai2 khong3-ia2 hit-tiau5 lou7 khi3; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 long2 pai5 tui7-ngou2, tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhut-khi3.  19). Mou5-se toa3 Iok-sek e5 kut-thau5 kap i khi3; in-ui7 Iok-sek bat chhiat-chhiat kah I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu3-choa7, tui3 in kong2, Siong7-te3 tek-khak koan3-kou3 lin2, lin2 tioh8 toa3 goa2 e5 kut-thau5 tui3 chia saN-kap khi3.  20). In tui3 Sou-kat khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 kun7 khong3-ia2 e5 I2-thong2.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa kiaN5 ti7 in e5 thau5-cheng5, jit8--si5 ti7 hun5-thiau7-tiong chhoa7 in e5 lou7, mi5--si5 ti7 he2-thiau7-tiong kng-chio3 in; hou7 in jit8-mi5 long2 thang kiaN5.  22). Jit8--si5 e5 hun5-thiau7, mi5--si5 e5 he2-thiau7, long2 bo5 li7-khui peh-siN3 e5 thau5-cheng5.

[14]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 oat8-to3-tng2, chat-iaN5 ti7 Pi2-hap-hi-liok8 e5 thau5-cheng5, ti7 Bit8-toat8 kap hai2 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 Pa-lek8-se2-hun e5 thau5-cheng5, ti7 hit tui3-bin7 chat-iaN5 ti7 hai2-piN.  3). Hoat-lo2 beh gi7-lun7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, In ti7 toe7-tiong seh8 bo5 lou7, khong3-ia2 ka7 in ui5-khun3 teh.  4). Goa2 beh hou7 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7, i beh tui-jip in; Goa2 chiu7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 choan5-kun lai5 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng; Ai-kip8 lang5 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  In chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5.  5). U7 lang5 po3 Ai-kip8 ong5 kong2, Hit e5 peh-siN3 chau2-khi3; Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 jin5-sin5 tui3-thai7 hit e5 peh-siN3 e5 sim chiu7 pian3-oaN7, kong2, Lan2 chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khi3, bo5 koh hok8-sai7 lan2, che si7 sim2-mih8 ian5-kou3 ah?  6). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 pi7-pan7 i e5 chhia, toa3 i e5 peh-siN3 saN-kap khi3.  7). Ia7 toa3 lak8-pah tiuN tek8-piat8 chhia, kap Ai-kip8 sou2 u7 e5 chhia, tak8 tiuN chhia long2 u7 peng-thau5 teh koan2.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 e5 sim ngi7; i chiu7 tui-jip I2-sek-liat8 lang5; na7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kho3 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 chhut-khi3.  9). Ai-kip8 lang5 tui-jip in, Hoat-lo2 it-chhe3 e5 be2, chhia, kap i e5 be2-peng, kap i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7 ti7 hai2-piN oa2-kun7 Pi2-hap-hi-liok8, ti7 Pa-lek8-se2-hun e5 tui3-bin7, ti7 in an-iaN5 e5 sou2-chai7, jip-tioh8 in.  10). Hoat-lo2 kun7-oa2 e5 si5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 Ai-kip8 lang5 jip-oa2--lai5, chiu7 chin kiaN, au5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  11). In tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Kiam2 si7 Ai-kip8 bo5 thiong2-toe7, li2 chiah chhoa7 goan2 chhut-lai5 si2 ti7 khong3-ia2 mah? li2 siaN2-su7 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 goan2, chhoa7 goan2 chhut Ai-kip8 ah?  12). Goan2 ti7 Ai-kip8 kiam2 bo5 tui3 li2 an2-ni kong2, Boh8-tit chhap goan2, chhut-chai7 goan2 hok8-sai7 Ai-kip8 lang5 mah? In-ui7 hok8-sai7 Ai-kip8 lang5, khah-tit si2 ti7 khong3-ia2.  13). Mou5-se tui3 peh-siN3 kong2, M7-bian2 kiaN, choe3 lin2 khia7-teh, khoaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kin-a2-jit8 ui7-tioh8 lin2 sou2 beh kiaN5 e5 chin2-kiu3; in-ui7 lin2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 Ai-kip8 lang5, tek-khak eng2-oan2 bo5 koh khoaN3-kiN3.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ui7 lin2 kau-chian3, choe3 lin2 tiam7-tiam7, boh8 choe3-siaN.
	15). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 au5-kio3 Goa2 ah? li2 tioh8 kah I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chin3-cheng5 khi3.  16). Li2 kiah8 koaiN2-a2 chhun-chhiu2 ki2 hai2, lai5 pun-khui i; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 beh ti7 hai2-tiong kiaN5 ta-toe7;  17). tok8-tok8 Goa2, Goa2 beh hou7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 sim ngi7, in beh te3--loh8-khi3; Goa2 beh ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 choan5-kun, i e5 chhia, i e5 be2-peng, lai5 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng.  18). Goa2 ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 chhia, i e5 be2-peng, tit-tioh8 eng5-kng e5 si5, Ai-kip8 lang5 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  19). Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2, pun2 kiaN5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 iaN5-cheng5--e5, soa2 lai5 kiaN5 ti7 in e5 au7-bin7; hun5-thiau7 ia7 tui3 in e5 thau5-cheng5, soa2 lai5 khia7 ti7 in e5 au7-bin7,  20). ti7 Ai-kip8 iaN5 kap I2-sek-liat8 iaN5 e5 tiong-kan; hit-peng5 u7 hun5 u7 ou-am3, chit-peng5 mi5--si5 hoat-chhut kng; thong-mi5 nng7 peng5 boe7 saN-kun7.  21). Mou5-se chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 ki2 hai2, Ia5-ho5-hoa thong-mi5 hou7 tang-hong toa7 khi2, hou7 hai2 the3--khi3, chui2 chiu7 pun-khui, hai2 chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 ta-toe7.  22). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 loh8 hai2-tiong kiaN5 ta-toe7, chui2 ti7 in e5 siang-peng5 chiaN5-choe3 chhiuN5-piah.  23). Ai-kip8 lang5 tui-jip--in; Hoat-lo2 it-chhe3 e5 be2, chhia, kap be2-peng, long2 te3 in kau3 hai2-tiong.  24). Kau3 thiN beh kng e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 hun5 kap he2 e5 thiau7-tiong aN3-loh8, khoaN3 Ai-kip8 e5 kun-tui7, phah-loan7 in e5 tui7-ngou2;  25). koh hou7 in e5 chhia-lun5 lak-loh8, oh-tit kiaN5; ti3-kau3 Ai-kip8 lang5 kong2, Lan2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 to5-chau2, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7-tioh8 in kap Ai-kip8 lang5 kau-chian3.
	26). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 chhun-chhiu2 ki2 hai2, hou7 chui2 to3-tng2--lai5 im Ai-kip8 lang5, kap in e5 chhia, in e5 be2-peng.  27). Mou5-se chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 ki2 hai2; kau3 thiN chit8-e7 kng, hai2-chui2 koh chiau3-ku7; Ai-kip8 lang5 to5-chau2, chui2 chah8 ti7 in e5 thau5-cheng5; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 chiong Ai-kip8 lang5 chhia-to2 ti7 hai2-tiong.  28). Chui2 chiu7 hoan-lau5, im-bat8 hiah e5 chhia kap be2-peng; Hoat-lo2 e5 choan5-kun te3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 loh8 hai2--e5, lian5 chit8-e5 ia7 bo5 lau5-teh.  29). Chong2-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 hai2-tiong kiaN5 ta-toe7, chui2 ti7 in e5 siang-peng5 chiaN5-choe3 in e5 chhiuN5-piah.  30). Hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kiu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 thoat-li7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 chhiu2; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 sin-si ti7 hai2-piN.  31). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 kiaN5 e5 toa7-su7, chiu7 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; koh sin3-hok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap I e5 lou5-pok8 Mou5-se.

[15]	Hit-si5 Mou5-se kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhiuN3 chit e5 koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2;
	Goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 I chi3-koaiN5 chi3-toa7;
	Chiong be2 kap khia5-be2--e5 hiat ti7 hai2-tiong.
2).	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8, si7 goa2 e5 si-ko,
	Ia7 si7 choe3 goa2 chin2-kiu3 e5 Chu2; 
	I si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 beh o-lo2--I,
	Si7 goa2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 beh chun I choe3-toa7.
3).	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 chian3-su7;
	I e5 mia5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
4).	Hoat-lo2 e5 chhia, kap i e5 kun-peng, Ia5-ho5-hoa hiat i ti7 hai2-tiong;
	I tek8-piat8 keng2 e5 kun-tiuN2, long2 tim5 ti7 Ang5-hai2.
5).	Chhim-ian kham3--in;
	In chhin-chhiuN7 chioh8-thau5, tui7 kau3 chhim e5 sou2-chai7.
6).	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 tian2-chhut leng5-lek8, tit-tioh8 eng5-kng;
	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 phah-chhui3 tui3-tek8.
7).	Li2 hoat-chhut toa7 ui-giam5, chhia-to2 hiah-e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek Li2--e5;
	Li2 hoat-chhut toa7 siu7-khi3, sio-hui2 in chhin-chhiuN7 sio-chhau2.
8).	Li2 hoat-chhut phiN7-tiong e5 khi3, chui2 chiu7 na2-chheng3 na2-koaiN5,
	Toa7-chui2 khia7--khi2-lai5 chhin-chhiuN7 kui-tui;
	Hai2-tiong e5 chhim-chui2 kian-teng7.
9). 	Tui3-tek8 kong2,
	Goa2 beh tui in, goa2 beh jip-tioh8 in, goa2 beh pun sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8;
	Goa2 beh ti7 in lai5 chiok goa2 e5 sim-goan7;
	Goa2 beh puih8-to, goa2 e5 chhiu2 beh biat8 in.
10).	Li2 chit8-e7 pun5-hong, hai2 chiu7 kham3-bat8--in;
	In chhin-chhiuN7 ian5, tim5 ti7 toa7-chui2-tiong.
11).	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, chiah e5 siong7-te3 e5 tiong-kan, chi7-chui7 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 Li2?
	Chi7-chui7 chhin-chhiuN7 Li2, chi3-seng3 thang eng5-kng,
	Ui-giam5 thang o-lo2, kiaN5-chhut ki5-su7?
12).	Li2 chhun-chhut chiaN3-chhiu2,
	Toe7 chiu7 thun-biat8--in.
13).	Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3, chhoa7 Li2 sou2 kiu3-siok8 e5 peh-siN3;
	Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 koan5-leng5, chhoa7 in jip8 Li2 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7.
14).	Liat8-pang thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah;
	Khia7-khi2 ti7 Hui-li7-su7 toe7 e5, tu2-tioh8 thong3-khou2.
15).	Hit-si5 I2-tong e5 chok8-tiuN2 gong5-ngiah8;
	Mou5-ap eng-hiong5 e5 lang5 ti3-kau3 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah,
	Ka-lam5 toe7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, sim long2 siau-iuN5.
16).	Gong5-ngiah8 kiaN-hiaN5 kau3 ti7 in;
	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, in-ui7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5, in tiaN7-tiaN7 chhin-chhiuN7 chioh8-thau5,
	Theng3-hau7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 keng-ke3,
	Theng3-hau7 Li2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 peh-siN3 ke3--khi3.
17).	Li2 beh chhoa7 in jip8--khi3, chai-poe5 in ti7 Li2 e5 san2-giap8 e5 soaN,
	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, chiu7-si7 Li2 ui7 ka-ki7 sou2 pi7-pan7 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7,
	Chu2 ah, chiu7-si7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 kian3-lip8 e5 seng3-sou2.
18).	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh choe3-ong5, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.
19). In-ui7 Hoat-lo2 e5 be2, kap i e5 chhia, i e5 be2-peng, kau3 ti7 hai2-tiong, Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 hai2-chui2 hoan-lau5 im-bat8--in; tok8-tok8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 hai2-tiong kiaN5 ta-toe7.  20). A-lun5 e5 toa7-chi2 lu2 sian-ti Bi2-li7-am3, chhiu2--nih kiah8 lin-long-kou2, cheng3 hu7-lu2 ia7 te3 i chhut-khi3, kiah8 lin-long-kou2 thiau3-bu2.  21). Bi2-li7-am3 ho7 sou2-chhiuN3-e5 kong2, 
	Lin2 tioh8 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 I chi3-koaiN5 chi3-toa7;
	Chiong be2 kap khia5-be2--e5, hiat ti7 hai2-tiong.
	22). Mou5-se chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Ang5-hai2 chin3-cheng5 kiaN5; in chhut-khi3, kau3 Su-jiN2 e5 khong3-ia2; ti7 khong3-ia2 kiaN5 saN-jit8, chhe7 bo5 chui2.  23). Kau3 Ma2-lah8 e5 si5, Ma2-lah8 e5 chui2 boe7 lim--tit, in-ui7 chui2 khou2; sou2-i2 mia5 hit e5 toe7 kio3 Ma2-lah8.  24). Peh-siN3 chiu7 tui3 Mou5-se ai-oan3 kong2, Goan2 beh lim sim2-mih8 ah?  25). Mou5-se kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Ia5-ho5-hoa chi2-si7 i chit8 chang5 chhiu7, i chiu7 hiat i ti7 chui2--nih, chui2 chiu7 pian3-kam.  I ti7-hia, ui7 in teng7 lut8-le7 hoat-tou7, ti7-hia chhi3-giam7 in.  26). Koh kong2, Li2 na7 ti3-i3 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN, koh kiaN5 I sou2 khoaN3 choe3 hap8-gi5 e5 su7, liu5-sim thiaN I e5 kai3-beng7, siu2 I it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7, chiu7 Goa2 hou7 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 phoa3-piN7, tek-khak bo5 hou7 li2 tu2-tioh8; in-ui7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 i-ti7 li2--e5.
	27). In kau3 I2-lim5, ti7-hia u7 chap8-ji7 e5 chui2-choaN5, chhit-chap8 chang5 e5 cho2-chhiu7; in chiu7 ti7-hia e5 chui2-piN chat-iaN5.

[16]	In tui3 I2-lim5 khi2-sin, ti7 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 i2-au7, te7-ji7 geh8 chap8-gou7 jit8, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 kau3 I2-lim5 kap Se-nai2 e5 tiong-kan, Sin3 e5 khong3-ia2.  2). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 ti7 khong3-ia2 ai-oan3 Mou5-se A-lun5.  3). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 in kong2, M7-tat8-tioh8 goan2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 si2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2.  Hit-si5 goan2 u7 bah moa2-tiaN2, u7 piaN2 thang chiah8 kau3-pa2; lin2 chhoa7 goan2 chhut--lai5 kau3 chit e5 khong3-ia2, si7 beh hou7 chit e5 choan5-hoe7 long2 go7-si2.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh tui3 thiN loh8 bi2-niu5 hou7 lin2; peh-siN3 tioh8 chhut-khi3, tak8-jit8 khioh tak8-jit8 e5 giah8; Goa2 thang chhi3-giam7 in, khoaN3 in beh than3 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7 a2 m7.  5). Kau3 te7-lak8 jit8, in tioh8 chiong sou2 khioh jip8--lai5-e5, pi7-pan7 ho2-se3, pi2 tak8-jit8 sou2-khioh-e5 teng5-pe7 choe7.  6). Mou5-se A-lun5 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 kong2, Kau3 e5-hng lin2 beh chai, chhoa7 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  7). Bin5-a2-cha2-khi2 lin2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 lin2 ai-oan3 I; goan2 sng3 sim2-mih8, lin2 keng3-jian5 ai-oan3 goan2?  8). Mou5-se koh kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5-hng-si5 beh hou7 lin2 chiah8-bah, cha2-khi2-si5 beh hou7 lin2 chiah8-piaN2 kau3 pa2; in-ui7 lin2 ai-oan3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I long2 thiaN-kiN3; goan2 sng3 sim2-mih8? lin2 m7-si7 ai-oan3 goan2, si7 ai-oan3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  9). Mou5-se tui3 A-lun5 kong2, Li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chiu7-kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; in-ui7 I i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 lin2 e5 ai-oan3 lah.  10). A-lun5 tu2-tu2 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, in ng3 khong3-ia2 teh khoaN3, khoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng ti7 hun5-tiong hian2-hian7.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2,  12). Goa2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 ai-oan3; li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Kau3 hong5-hun e5 si5, lin2 beh chiah8-bah, cha2-khi2 beh u7 piaN2 thang chiah8-pa2; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  13). Kau3 e5-hng u7 ian-chhun pe--lai5, jia-kham3 iaN5-poaN5; thiN-kng-cha2 ti7 iaN5-poaN5 si3-ui5 e5 toe7-bin7, u7 chit8-teng5 e5 lou7-chui2.  14). Lou7-chui2 ta e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, khong3-ia2 e5 toe7-bin7 u7 soe3-soe3 iN5-iN5 e5 mih8; soe3 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 sng.  15). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3, m7-chai si7 sim2-mih8, tai7-ke saN-kap kong2, Che si7 sim2-mih8 ah? Mou5-se ka7 in kong2, Che chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 lin2 chiah8 e5 piaN2.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3--e5 si7 an2-ni; lin2 tioh8 chiau3 tak8-lang5 sou2 oe7 chiah8 e5 liong7 lai5 khioh, tak8-lang5 ui7 i pou3-piN5-lai7 e5 lang5, chiau3 i e5 lang5-giah8 lai5 khioh, chit8-lang5 chit8 go5-mui5-jiN2.  17). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5, u7-e5 khioh choe7, u7-e5 khioh chio2.  18). Kau3 eng7 go5-mui5-jiN2 niu5 i, khioh choe7--e5 bo5 chhun, khioh chio2--e5 ia7 bo5 khiam3; tak8-lang5 chiau3 in oe7 chiah8 e5 liong7 lai5 khioh i.  19). Mou5-se ka7 in kong2, Lang5 m7-thang chiong sou2 chhun--e5 lau5 kau3 ke3 cha2-khi2.  20). Chong2-si7 in bo5 thiaN Mou5-se e5 oe7, u7 lang5 lau5 kau3 ke3 cha2-khi2, chiu7 siN-thang7 chhau3-bi7; Mou5-se siu7-khi3 in.  21). In tak8 cha2-khi2, chiau3 tak8-lang5 oe7 chiah8 e5 liong7 khioh i; jit8-thau5 chit8-e7 phak8, chiu7 iuN5--khi3.  22). Kau3 te7-lak8 jit8, in khioh teng5-pe7 e5 giah8, tak8-lang5 nng7 go5-mui5-jiN2; choan5-hoe7 hiah e5 thau5-lang5 lai5 ka7 Mou5-se kong2.  23). Mou5-se ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, bin5-a2-jit8 si7 tiong7-iau3 e5 an-hioh, chiu7-si7 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa seng3 e5 an-hioh-jit8; lin2 ai3 pek--e5 chiu7 pek i, ai3 chu2--e5 chiu7 chu2 i; sou2-chhun--e5, tioh8 ka-ki7 siu--teh, lau5 kau3 ke3 cha2-khi2.  24). In chiu7 chiau3 Mou5-se sou2 hoan-hu3 siu-teh lau5 kau3 ke3 cha2-khi2, ia7 bo5 chhau3-bi7, lai7-bin7 ia7 bo5 thang5.  25). Mou5-se kong2, Lin2 kin-a2-jit8 chiah8 chit-e5, in-ui7 kin-a2-jit8 si7 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 an-hioh-jit8; lin2 ti7 chhan5-ia2, kin-a2-jit8 tek-khak chhe7-bo5.  26). Lak8-jit8-kan thang khioh, te7-chhit jit8 si7 an-hioh-jit8, hit-jit8 chiu7 bo5.  27). Te7-chhit-jit8 peh-siN3-tiong u7 lang5 chhut-khi3 khioh, ia7 chhe7-bo5.  28). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Lin2 m7-kheng2 siu2 Goa2 e5 beng7-leng7, Goa2 e5 lut8-hoat, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah?  29). Lin2 tioh8 khoaN3, Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng chiong an-hioh-jit8 siuN2-su3 lin2, sou2-i2 te7-lak8 jit8 I hou7 lin2 nng7-jit8 e5 bi2-niu5, te7-chhit jit8 tak8-lang5 tioh8 tiam3 ka-ki7 e5 sou2-chai7, long2 m7-thang chhut-khi3.  30). Tui3 an2-ni peh-siN3 chiu7 ti7 te7-chhit jit8 an-hioh.
	31). Chit e5 mih8, I2-sek-liat8-ke kio3 i choe3 ma2-na2; khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 oan5-sui-jin5, sek-ti3 si7 peh8--e5, chu-bi7 chhin-chhiuN7 chham-bit8 e5 piaN2.  32). Mou5-se kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni hoan-hu3, tioh8 chiong chit8 go5-mui5-jiN2 tiN7-tiN7 e5 ma2-na2 , lau5 kau3 lin2 e5 au7-tai7, hou7 in khoaN3 Goa2 tng-jit8 chhoa7 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8-toe7, ti7 khong3-ia2 sou2 hou7 lin2 chiah8 e5 piaN2.  33). Mou5-se ka7 A-lun5 kong2, Li2 theh8 chit8 e5 khi3-ku7, toe2 chit8 go5-mui5-jiN2 tiN7-tiN7 e5 ma2-na2, khng3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, lau5 kau3 lin2 e5 au7-tai7.  34). A-lun5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5, chiong ma2-na2 he7 ti7 kan-cheng3 e5 iok-kui7 cheng5 lau5-teh.  35). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiah8 ma2-na2 kiong7 si3-chap8 ni5 ku2, tit8-kau3 in kau3 ti7 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7.  In chiah8 ma2-na2, tit8-kau3 in kau3 Ka-lam5 e5 keng2-kai3.  36). Chit8 go5-mui5-jiN2 chiu7-si7 i-hoat e5 chap8-hun7-chit8.

[17]	I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7, chiau3 lou7-cham7, tui3 Sin3 e5 khong3-ia2, chin3-cheng5 kiaN5, ti7 Li7-hui-teng3 chat-iaN5, peh-siN3 bo5 chui2 thang lim.  2). Peh-siN3 chiu7 kap Mou5-se ke3-kau3 kong2, Hou7 goan2 u7 chui2 thang lim.  Mou5-se ka7 in kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 kap goa2 ke3-kau3, siaN2-su7 chhi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah?  3). Peh-siN3 ti7-hia chin chhui3-ta, ai3 lim chui2; chiu7 ai-oan3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 chhoa7 goan2 tui3 Ai-kip8 chiuN7--lai5, hou7 goan2 kap goan2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, goan2 e5 cheng-siN, long2 chhui3-ta si2 ah?  4). Mou5-se chiu7 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 tui3 chit e5 peh-siN3 beh chaiN2-iuN7 choe3 ah? in chha-put-to beh eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 goa2.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 choe3 peh-siN3 e5 thau5-cheng5 kiaN5, chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiuN2-lo2 kui2-na7 lang5 kap li2 khi3, li2 e5 chhiu2 tioh8 kiah8 cheng5-jit8 phah ho5-chui2 e5 koaiN2-a2.  6). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh khia7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 Ho5-liat8 e5 chioh8-poaN5-teng2; li2 phah hit e5 chioh8-poaN5, beh u7 chui2 tui3 hia lau5-chhut hou7 peh-siN3 lim.  Mou5-se chiu7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiuN2-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 an2-ni kiaN5.  7). I mia5 hit e5 sou2-chai7 kio3 Ma2-sat, koh kio3-choe3 Bi2-li7-pa; in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ke3-kau3, koh in-ui7 in chhi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 goan2 tiong-kan a2-bo5?
	8). Hit-si5 A-ma2-lek8 lang5 lai5 kau3 Li7-hui-teng3, kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kau-chian3.  9). Mou5-se ka7 Iok-su-a kong2, Li2 thoe3 lan2 keng2 lang5 chhut-khi3 kap A-ma2-lek8 lang5 kau-chian3; bin5-a2-jit8 goa2 chhiu2--nih beh kiah8 Siong7-te3 e5 koaiN2-a2, khia7 ti7 soaN-teng2.  10). Tui3 hit-tiap8 Iok-su-a chiau3 Mou5-se sou2 ka7 i kong2--e5 kiaN5; kap A-ma2-lek8 lang5 kau-chian3; Mou5-se A-lun5 kap Hou7-jiN2 long2 chiuN7 soaN-teng2.  11). Mou5-se chhiu2 kiah8-khi2 e5 si5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 khah-iaN5; chhiu2 sui5--loh8-khi3 e5 si5, A-ma2-lek8 lang5 chiu7 khah-iaN5.  12). Chong2-si7 Mou5-se chhiu2 sng; in chiu7 soa2 chioh8, lai5 he7 ti7 i e5 e7-bin7; i che7 ti7 chioh8-teng2, A-lun5 kap Hou7-jiN2 hu5 i e5 chhiu2, chit8-e5 ti7 chit-peng5, chit8-e5 ti7 hit-peng5; i e5 chhiu2 chiu7 chu7-chai7, tit8-tit8 kau3 jit8-loh8.  13). Iok-su-a eng7 to thai5 A-ma2-lek8 ong5 kap i e5 peh-siN3.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 beh chiong A-ma2-lek8 e5 mia5-ji7 tui3 thiN-e7 oan5-choan5 chhat-biat8 i; li2 tioh8 eng7 chit-e5 sia2 ti7 chheh--nih choe3 ki3-liam7, koh kong2 hou7 Iok-su-a thiaN.  15). Mou5-se khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, ho7 i e5 mia5 kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa-ni5-se;  16). koh kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng chiu3-choa7, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh tai7-tai7 kap A-ma2-lek8 lang5 kau-chian3.

[18]	Mou5-se e5 tiuN7-lang5, Bi2-tian5 e5 che3-si Iap8-thek-lo5, thiaN-kiN3 Siong7-te3 ui7 Mou5-se kap I e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 sou2-kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 su7.  2). Mou5-se e5 tiuN7-lang5 Iap8-thek-lo5 toa3 Mou5-se e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 Se-pho-lah8 lai5, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se cheng5 chhe i to3--khi3 e5;  3). koh toa3 i nng7 e5 kiaN2, chit8-e5 mia5-kio3 Kek-sun7; in-ui7 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 kia3-kha ti7 goa7-pang;  4). chit8-e5 mia5 kio3 I2-li7-i2-sia7; in-ui7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3 pang-chan7 goa2, kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 Hoat-lo2 e5 to.  5). Mou5-se e5 tiuN7-lang5, Iap8-thek-lo5, toa3 Mou5-se nng7 e5 kiaN2 kap i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, lai5 kau3 Siong7-te3 e5 soaN, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se ti7 khong3-ia2 chat-iaN5 e5 sou2-chai7;  6). ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 tiuN7-lang5 Iap8-thek-lo5, toa3 li2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap i nng7 e5 kiaN2, lai5 li2 chia.  7). Mou5-se chhut-khi3 ngia5-chih i e5 tiuN7-lang5, tui3 i kiok-kiong, kap i chim-chhui3, saN-kap mng7 peng5-an; chiu7 jip8 pou3-piN5.  8). Mou5-se chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 ian5-kou3 tui3 Hoat-lo2 kap Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 su7, i2-kip8 lou7--nih sou2 tu2-tioh8 it-chhe3 e5 ui5-lan5, kap Ia5-ho5-hoa chai2-iuN7 chin2-kiu3 in, long2 pai5-liat8 hou7 i e5 tiuN7-lang5 thiaN.  9). Iap8-thek-lo5 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khoan2-thai7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chhe3 e5 ho2-su7, kiu3 in thoat-li7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chiu7 chin hoaN-hi2.  10). Iap8-thek-lo5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 eng-kai o-lo2--e5, I kiu3 lin2 thoat-li7 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 chhiu2, ia7 thoat-li7 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2, kiu3 chit e5 peh-siN3 chhut Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 chhiu2-e7.  11). TaN goa2 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa pi2 chiah e5 siong7-te3 khah-toa7, chiu7-si7 tui3 in hiah e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 kiau-ngou7 khoan2-thai7 chit e5 peh-siN3 e5 su7.  12). Mou5-se e5 tiuN7-lang5, Iap8-thek-lo5, chiong sio-che3 kap pat8-ho7 e5 che3, hian3 hou7 Siong7-te3; A-lun5 kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiuN2-lo2 long2 lai5, kap Mou5-se e5 tiuN7-lang5 saN-kap chiah8 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5.
	13). Keh-jit8 Mou5-se che7-teh sim2-phoaN3 peh-siN3; peh-siN3 tui3 cha2-khi2 kau3 e5-hng, long2 khia7-oa2 ti7 Mou5-se e5 sin-piN.  14). Mou5-se e5 tiuN7-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 i tui3 peh-siN3 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, chiu7 kong2, Li2 tui3 peh-siN3 choe3-e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7 ah? li2 siaN2-su7 ka-ki7 che7-teh, cheng3 peh-siN3 tui3 cha2-khi2 kau3 e5-hng long2 khia7 ti7 li2 e5 sin-piN ah?  15). Mou5-se in3 i e5 tiuN7-lang5 kong2, Che si7 in-ui7 peh-siN3 kau3 goa2 chia, lai5 mng7 Siong7-te3.  16). In u7 tai7-chi3 e5 si5, chiu7 lai5 goa2 chia, goa2 chiu7 ti7 in siang-peng5 e5 tiong-kan ka7 in phoaN3-toan3, hou7 in chai Siong7-te3 e5 lut8-le7 kap hoat-tou7.  17). Mou5-se e5 tiuN7-lang5 tui3 i kong2, Li2 an2-ni choe3 m7-ho2.  18). Li2 kap li2 chiah e5 peh-siN3 oe7 chin sng2-sin; in-ui7 chit e5 su7 hou7 li2 siuN tang7, li2 ka-ki7 chit8-lang5 choe3-boe7-lai5.  19). TaN li2 tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7, goa2 thoe3 li2 phah-sng3, goan7 Siong7-te3 kap li2 ti7-teh; li2 tioh8 thoe3 peh-siN3 kau3 Siong7-te3 bin7-cheng5, chiong an3-kiaN7 chheng2-mng7 Siong7-te3;  20). koh tioh8 chiong lut8-le7 kap hoat-tou7 ka3-si7 in, chi2-si7 in sou2 tioh8 kiaN5 e5 lou7, sou2 tioh8 choe3 e5 su7.  21). Ia7 tioh8 tui3 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan, keng2 u7 chai5-leng5 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3, seng5-sit8 bo5 lam7-sam2, oan3-hun7 put-gi7 e5 chiN5, hit-ho7 lang5, siat-lip8 in choe3 peh-siN3 e5 si7-toa7, u7-e5 koan2 chit8 chheng lang5, u7-e5 koan2 chit8-pah lang5, u7-e5 koan2 gou7-chap8 lang5, u7-e5 koan2 chap8-lang5;  22). hou7 in chiau3-si5 sim2-phoaN3 peh-siN3; toa7-su7 tioh8 hou7 in kau3 li2 chia, sio2-su7 in thang ka-ki7 sim2-phoaN3; an2-ni li2 chiu7 khah kiam2-khin, in ia7 thang kap li2 saN-kap tam-tng.  23). Li2 na7 an2-ni kiaN5, Siong7-te3 ia7 an2-ni hoan-hu3 li2, li2 chiu7 chih-chai3 oe7-tiau5, chiah e5 peh-siN3 ia7 thang an-jian5 kau3 i e5 sou2-chai7.  24). Tui3 an2-ni Mou5-se thiaN-than3 i e5 tiuN7-lang5 e5 oe7, long2 chiau3 i sou2 kong2--e5 khi3 kiaN5.  25). Mou5-se tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong-kan keng2 u7 chai5-leng5 e5 lang5, siat-lip8 in choe3 peh-siN3 e5 si7-toa7, u7-e5 koan2 chit8-chheng lang5, u7-e5 koan2 chit8-pah lang5, u7-e5 koan2 gou7-chap8 lang5, u7-e5 koan2 chap8-lang5;  26). in chiau3-si5 sim2-phoaN3 peh-siN3, u7 oh-tit e5 an3-kiaN7 chiu7 kau3 Mou5-se hia; na7-si7 tak8-hang7 sio2-su7, in chiu7 ka-ki7 sim2-phoaN3.  27). Au7-lai5 Mou5-se sang3 i e5 tiuN7-lang5 khi2-sin, i chiu7 to3--khi3 pun2 sou2-chai7.

[19]	I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 liau2-au7 te7-saN geh8, tu2-tu2 hit-jit8, in chiu7 kau3 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2.  2). In li7-khui Li7-hui-teng3, lai5 kau3 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2, chiu7 ti7 khong3-ia2 chat-iaN5; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 ti7 hit e5 soaN e5 thau5-cheng5 chat-iaN5.  3). Mou5-se chiuN7 kau3 Siong7-te3 hia; Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 soaN--nih kio3 i kong2, Li2 tioh8 an2-ni ka7 Nga2-kok-ke kong2, thong-ti I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chai;  4). Goa2 tui3 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7, lin2 long2 khoaN3-kiN3; koh khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 chhin-chhiuN7 eng-chiau2 e5 sit8 pe7 lin2, toa3 lin2 lai5 kui ti7 Goa2.  5). TaN lin2 na7 sit8-chai7 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7, chun-siu2 Goa2 e5 iok, chiu7 ti7 liat8-kok-tiong lin2 beh choe3 Goa2 ka-ki7 e5 po2-poe3; in-ui7 choan5-toe7 long2 si7 Goa2-e5;  6). lin2 beh kui ti7 Goa2, choe3 che3-si e5 kok, choe3 seng3-kiat e5 peh-siN3.  Chiah e5 oe7 si7 li2 sou2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2--e5.
	7). Mou5-se lai5 chio-chip8 peh-siN3 tiong-kan e5 tiuN2-lo2, chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 i e5 oe7, long2 pai5-liat8 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5;  8). peh-siN3 long2 tang5-siaN in3 kong2, KiN3-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5 goan2 long2 beh chun-than3.  Mou5-se chiu7 chiong peh-siN3 e5 oe7 he5-hok Ia5-ho5-hoa.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ti7 bat8-hun5 e5 tiong-kan lim5-kau3 li2, hou7 peh-siN3 thiaN-kiN3 Goa2 kap li2 teh kong2, thang eng2-oan2 sin3 li2.  Mou5-se chiu7 chiong peh-siN3 e5 oe7 ka7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 khi3 peh-siN3 hia, kin-a2-jit8 bin5-a2-jit8 ka7 in hun-piat choe3-seng3, in ia7 tioh8 soe2-saN.  11). Tioh8 pi7-pan7 pian7 hu3 te7-saN jit8; in-ui7 te7-saN jit8, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5, kang3-lim5 ti7 Se-nai2 soaN.  12). Li2 tioh8 ti7 soaN e5 si3-ui5 ka7 peh-siN3 siat kai3-han7, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, m7-thang chiuN7-soaN, ia7 m7-thang bong i e5 kau-kai3; kiN3-na7 bong chit e5 soaN e5, tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2;  13). m7-thang eng7 chhiu2 bong--i, tioh8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 i, a2-si7 eng7 chiN3 sia7--i; bo5-lun7 si7 lang5 a2 cheng-siN, long2 boe7 oah8.  Kau3 sau3-kak e5 siaN thoa-tng5 e5 si5, in tioh8 chiuN7-lai5 soaN-kha.  14). Mou5-se loh8-soaN kau3 peh-siN3 hia, ka7 in hun-piat choe3-seng3; in chiu7 ka-ki7 soe2 saN.  15). I tui3 peh-siN3 kong2, Tioh8 pi7-pan7 pian7 hu3 te7-saN jit8, m7-thang chhin-kun7 hu7-jin5-lang5.
	16). Kau3 te7-saN jit8 thiN-kng-cha2, ti7 soaN-teng2 u7 lui5 tan5, sih-na3 kap bat8-hun5, koh sau3-kak e5 siaN chin-toa7; iaN5-lai7 e5 peh-siN3 long2 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.  17). Mou5-se chhoa7 peh-siN3 chhut iaN5-poaN5, ngia5-chih Siong7-te3; in long2 khia7 ti7 soaN-kha.  18). Thong Se-nai2 soaN long2 si7 he2-ian; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 he2-tiong kang3-lim5 ti7 soaN-teng2; soaN e5 he2-ian chheng3-koaiN5, chhin-chhiuN7 hui5-io5 e5 ian, pian3-soaN toa7 tin2-tang7.  19). Sau3-kak e5 siaN na2-tan5 na2-toa7, Mou5-se kong2-oe7, Siong7-te3 chhut-siaN in3 i.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa kang3-lim5 ti7 Se-nai2 soaN, ti7 soaN-be2-liu; Ia5-ho5-hoa tiau3 Mou5-se chiuN7 soaN-be2-liu; Mou5-se chiu7 chiuN7--khi3.  21).
