Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 loh8--khi3 kim3-kai3 peh-siN3, kiaN-liau2 in chhoan3-ke3-kai3, kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chia lai5 khoaN3, ti3-kau3 in choe7-choe7 lang5 si2;  22). lian5 chhin-kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 che3-si, ia7 tioh8 ka-ki7 hun-piat choe3-seng3, kiaN-liau2 Ia5-ho5-hoa hut-jian5 chhut--lai5 phah in.  23). Mou5-se tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Peh-siN3 boe7-oe7 chiuN7 Se-nai2 soaN, in-ui7 Li2 i2-keng kim3-kai3 goan2 kong2, Tioh8 ti7 soaN e5 si3-ui5 siat kai3-han7, hun-piat i choe3-seng3.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 i kong2, Khi3 ah, loh8--khi3; li2 tioh8 kap A-lun5 chiuN7--lai5; tok8-tok8 che3-si kap peh-siN3 m7-thang chhoan3-ke3-kai3 chiuN7 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5, kiaN-liau2 I hut-jian5 chhut-lai5 phah in.  25). Mou5-se chiu7 loh8--khi3, kau3 peh-siN3 hia, ka7 in kong2.

[20]	Siong7-te3 hoan-hu3 chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 kong2,  2). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3, bat chhoa7 li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7, tui3 choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke, chhut--lai5 e5.
	3). Goa2 i2-goa7, li2 m7-thang u7 pat8 e5 Siong7-te3.
	4). M7-thang ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 tiau-khek ngou2-siong7, put-lun7 thiN-teng2, toe7-chiuN7, kap toe7-e7 chui2-lai7 sou2-u7 e5 mih8, long2 m7-thang choe3 in e5 siong7;  5). m7-thang keng3-pai3 in, ia7 m7-thang hok8-sai7 in; in-ui7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3, toan3-toan3 m7 iong5-un2 eng7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 phit-phoe3 Goa2; oan3-hun7 Goa2--e5, Goa2 kui-kiu7 i e5 choe7, tui3 pe7 kau3 kiaN2 kau3 saN-si3 tai7;  6). thiaN3 Goa2, siu2 Goa2 kai3-beng7--e5, Goa2 si-un hou7 i, tit8-kau3 chheng-tai7.
	7). M7-thang lam7-sam2 chheng Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5; in-ui7 lam7-sam2 chheng I e5 mia5 e5 lang5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak bo5 liah8 i choe3 bo5-choe7.
	8). Tioh8 ki3-tit an-hioh-jit8, siu2 i choe3-seng3;  9). lak8-jit8-lai7 eng-kai tioh8-boa5, choe3 li2 it-chhe3 e5 kang;  10). tok8-tok8 te7-chhit-jit8, chiu7-si7 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 lai5 siu2 e5 an-hioh; chit-jit8 li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, cheng-siN, i2-kip8 tiam3 ti7 li2 tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, it-chhe3 e5 kang, long2 m7-thang choe3;  11). in-ui7 lak8-jit8-lai7, Ia5-ho5-hoa chhong3-cho7 thiN, toe7, hai2, kap hit tiong-kan ban7-mih8, te7-chhit jit8 chiu7 hioh; sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok ti7 an-hioh-jit8, siat-lip8 i choe3-seng3.
	12). Tioh8 hau3-keng3 li2 e5 lau7-pe7, li2 e5 lau7-bu2, hou7 li2 e5 jit8-chi2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, tit-tioh8 ku2-tng5.
	13). M7-thang hai7-si2 lang5.
	14). M7-thang kiaN5 kan-im5.
	15). M7-thang thau-theh8.
	16). M7-thang choe3 ke2 e5 kan-cheng3, ham7-hai7 li2 e5 chhu3-piN.
	17). M7-thang tham li2 e5 chhu3-piN e5 chhu3, ia7 m7-thang tham li2 e5 chhu3-piN e5 bou2, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, gu5, lu5, i2-kip8 li2 e5 chhu3-piN it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5.
	18). Cheng3 peh-siN3 khoaN3-kiN3 lui5-tan5, sih-na3, sau3-kak e5 siaN, koh soaN-teng2 chhut-ian, peh-siN3 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, hng7-hng7 khia7-teh;  19). tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Kiu5 li2 kap goan2 kong2, goan2 beh thiaN; m7-thang Siong7-te3 kap goan2 kong2, kiaN-liau2 goan2 oe7 si2.  20). Mou5-se tui3 peh-siN3 kong2, M7-bian2 kiaN; in-ui7 Siong7-te3 kang3-lim5 si7 beh chhi3-giam7 lin2 koh hou7 lin2 si5-siong5 keng3-ui3 I, bian2-tit lin2 hoan7-choe7.  21). Tui3 an2-ni peh-siN3 hng7-hng7 khia7-teh; Mou5-se chiu7 kiaN5-kun7 bat8-hun5, kau3 Siong7-te3 e5 sou2-chai7.
	22). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 an2-ni ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Lin2 i2-keng ka-ki7 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 tui3 thiN-teng2 kap lin2 kong2-oe7.  23). Lin2 m7-thang choe3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 phit-phoe3 Goa2; m7-thang ui7 ka-ki7 choe3 gun5 e5 siong7-te3, kim e5 siong7-te3.  24). Li2 tioh8 ka7 Goa2 khi2 thou5-toaN5, ti7 hit teng2-bin7 hian3 li2 e5 sio-che3, kap peng5-an-che3, kap li2 e5 gu5, li2 e5 iuN5; kiN3-na7 Goa2 hou7 lang5 ki3-liam7 Goa2 e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7, Goa2 beh kau3 li2 hia su3-hok li2.  25). Li2 na7 eng7 chioh8-thau5 ka7 Goa2 khi2-toaN5, m7-thang eng7 ke3-phah e5 chioh8 lai5 khi2; in-ui7 na7 ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7 tang7 li2 e5 ke-si, chiu7 phah la5-sam5--i.  26). Ia7 m7-thang eng7 kia7-a2-chan3 chiuN7 Goa2 e5 toaN5, bian2-tit lou7-hian7 li2 e5 e7-the2.

[21]	Li2 ti7 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 tioh8 lip8 e5 hoat-tou7 si7 an2-ni.
	2). Li2 na7 boe2 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 choe3 lou5-pok8, i beh hok8-sai7 li2, lak8-ni5 ku2, te7-chhit ni5 i thang chu7-iu5 peh8-peh8 chhut-khi3;  3). i na7 toaN-sin lai5, chiu7 toaN-sin chhut-khi3; i na7 u7 bou2, i e5 bou2 chiu7 kap i chhut-khi3;  4). i e5 chu2-lang5 na7 ka7 i chhoa7-bou2, bou2 ka7 i siN-kiaN2 a2 si7 cha-bou2-kiaN2, bou2 kap kiaN2-ji5 tioh8 kui chu2-lang5; i tioh8 toaN-sin chhut-khi3.  5). Siat-su2 lou5-pok8 beng5-beng5 kong2, Goa2 thiaN3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5, kap goa2 e5 bou2, goa2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, m7-ai3 chhut-khi3 chu7-iu5;  6). i e5 chu2-lang5 chiu7 tioh8 toa3 i kau3 koaN-hu2 hia, koh tioh8 chhoa7 i oa2-kun7 mng5, a2-si7 mng5-khia7, chu2-lang5 tioh8 eng7 chng3-a2 chng3 i e5 hi7-a2; i chiu7 eng2-oan2 hok8-sai7--i.
	7). Lang5 na7 boe7 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3 lu2-pi7, i bo5 thang chhin-chhiuN7 lou5-pok8 an2-ni chhut-khi3.  8). Chu2-lang5 na7 tiaN7-tioh8 siu--i, au7-lai5 khoaN3 bo5 teng3-i3, chiu7 tioh8 chun2 i siok8-sin; chu2-lang5 i2-keng phian3 i, chiu7 bo5 koan5 thang boe7 i hou7 goa7-pang lang5.  9). Chu2-lang5 na7 tiaN7-tioh8 i hou7 ka-ki7 e5 kiaN2, chiu7 tioh8 khoan2-thai7 i chhin-chhiuN7 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  10). Na7 u7 koh chhoa7 chit8-e5, chiu7 i e5 chiah8, chheng7, kap phoe3-hap8 e5 su7, iu5-goan5 m7-thang kiam2-chio2.  11). Na7 bo5 tui3 i kiaN5 chi2 saN-hang7, i chiu7 thang peh8-peh8 chhut-khi3, bian2 eng7 gun5 siok8.
	12). Phah-si2 lang5--e5 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.  13). Lang5 na7 m7-si7 bai5-hok8-teh thai5-lang5, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 kau ti7 i e5 chhiu2, Goa2 chiu7 ka7 li2 siat chit8 e5 sou2-chai7, i thang chau2-khi3 hia.  14). Lang5 na7 chu7-choan kong-kek i e5 chhu3-piN, eng7 khui2-khiat e5 ke3-bou5, chiu7 na7 ti7 Goa2 e5  toaN5, iah8 tioh8 liah8-khi3 hou7 i si2.
	15). Phah lau7-pe7 a2-si7 lau7-bu2--e5, tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.
	16). Koai2 lang5 khi3 boe7--e5, a2-si7 iau2 ti7 i e5 chhiu2, tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.
	17). Chiu3-chou2 lau7-pe7 a2-si7 lau7-bu2--e5, tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.
	18). Lang5 na7 oan-ke, chit-e5 eng7 chioh8-thau5 a2-si7 kun5-thau5-bu2 phah hit-e5, iau2 bo5 ti3-kau3 si2, put-ko3 to2 ti7 bin5-chhng5;  19). na7 oe7 koh khi2--lai5, oa3 koaiN2-a2 chhut-khi3, hit-e5 phah i--e5, thang sng3 bo5-choe7; tok8-tok8 tioh8 pe5 i boe7 choe3 kang e5 chiN5, ia7 tioh8 ka7-i i kau3 long2 ho2.
	20). Lang5 na7 eng7 thui5-a2 phah i e5 lou5-pok8, a2-si7 i e5 lu2-pi7, ti3-kau3 liam5-piN si2, i tek-khak tioh8 siu7 heng5-hoat8;  21). na7 ke3 chit8-nng7 jit8 chiah si2, chiu7 thang bian2 siu7 heng5-hoat8, in-ui7 si7 i e5 gun5 boe2-e5.
	22). Lang5 na7 saN-phah, siong-hai7 u7 sin-in7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, ti3-kau3 ka-lauh8-sin, au7-lai5 bo5 pat8-hang7 e5 hai7, hit-lang5 tioh8 hoat8-gun5, chiau3 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 tiong7-hu sou2 teng7--e5; ti7 koaN-hu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 hou7 i.  23). Na7 u7 pat8-hang7 e5 siong-hai7, chiu7 tioh8 eng7 mia7 pe5 mia7.  24). Bak8-chiu pe5 bak8-chiu, chhui3-khi2 pe5 chhui3-khi2, chhiu2 pe5 chhiu2,  25). kha pe5 kha, sio pe5 sio, siong pe5 siong, phah pe5 phah.
	26). Lang5 na7 phah-phaiN2 i e5 lou5-pok8, a2-si7 i e5 lu2-pi7, chit8-lui2 bak8-chiu, chiu7 tioh8 in-ui7 i e5 bak8-chiu pang3 i khi3 chu7-iu5.  27). Na7 phah-lak i e5 lou5-pok8, a2-si7 i e5 lu2-pi7, chit8 ki chhui3-khi2, chiu7 tioh8 in-ui7 i e5 chhui3-khi2 pang3 i khi3 chu7-iu5.
	28). Gu5 na7 tak-si2 chit8 e5 ta-pou-lang5, a2-si7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, tioh8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 hit chiah gu5, chong2-si7 m7-thang chiah8 i e5 bah; gu5 e5 chu2-lang5 sng3 bo5 choe7.  29). Siat-su2 hit chiah gu5 peng5-sou3 oe7 tak--lang5, u7 lang5 po3 i e5 chu2-lang5 chai, i keng3-jian5 bo5 chiong gu5 koaiN--teh, ti3-kau3 tak-si2 ta-pou-lang5 a2-si7 hu7-jin5-lang5; chiu7 tioh8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 hit chiah gu5, gu5 e5 chu2-lang5 ia7 tioh8 si2.  30). Na7 si7 gi2-tiaN7 eng7 gun5 siok8 siN3-mia7, chiu7 tioh8 chiau3 sou2 gi2-tiaN7--e5, lai5 siok8 i e5 siN3-mia7.  31). Gu5 bo5-lun7 tak-tioh8 lang5 e5 kiaN2 a2-si7 cha-bou2-kiaN2, tioh8 chiau3 chit e5 le7 pan7--i.  32). Gu5 na7 tak-tioh8 lou5-pok8 a2-si7 lu2-pi7, tioh8 eng7 gun5 saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8 hou7 in e5 chu2-lang5; ia7 tioh8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 gu5.
	33). Lang5 na7 hian-khui chiN2, a2-si7 kut8 chiN2, bo5 kham3-koa3, u7 gu5 a2-si7 lu5 poah8 ti7 hit lai7-bin7,  34). chiN2 e5 chu2-lang5 tioh8 pe5, ia7 tioh8 theh8 gun5 hou7 i e5 chu2; si2 e5 cheng-siN kui ka-ki7.
	35). Chit-lang5 e5 gu5 na7 tak-tioh8 hit lang5 e5 gu5, ti3-kau3 si2, in tioh8 boe7 oah8 e5 gu5, ke3-chiN5 piN5-pun, si2 e5 gu5 ia7 tioh8 piN5-pun.  36). Lang5 na7 chai chit chiah gu5 peng5-sou3 oe7 tak--lang5, chu2-lang5 keng3-jian5 bo5 chiong gu5 koaiN-teh, i chiu7 tioh8 eng7 gu5 pe5 gu5, si2 e5 gu5 kui ka-ki7.

[22]	Lang5 na7 thau-khan gu5, a2-si7 iuN5, bo5-lun7 thai5 a2-si7 boe7, chit8 chiah gu5 tioh8 pe5 i gou7 chiah, chit8 chiah iuN5 tioh8 pe5 si3-chiah.  2). Chhat8 na7 iah-khang, hou7 lang5 tu2-tioh8, ka7 i phah-si2, chiu7 bo5 sng3 i u7 phah-si2 lang5 e5 choe7.  3). Na7 jit8-thau5 i2-keng chhut, chiu7 sng3 i u7 phah-si2 lang5 e5 choe7.  Chhat8 tek-khak tioh8 pe5; na7 bo5 thang pe5, chhat8 tioh8 boe7 sin, lai5 ti2 i sou2 thau--e5.  4). Na7 i sou2 thau--e5, kiam2-chhai2 gu5, a2-si7 lu5, iuN5, iau2 oah8 ti7 i e5 chhiu2, chiu7 tioh8 pe5 teng5-pe7.
	5). Lang5 na7 ti7 chhan5--nih, a2-si7 phu5-to5-hng5, pang3 cheng-siN, chhut-chai7 i chiah8 pat8-lang5 e5 chhan5, chiu7 tioh8 eng7 ka-ki7 e5 chhan5--nih siong7 ho2--e5, kap phu5-to5-hng5 siong7 ho2--e5 lai5 pe5--i.
	6). Na7 he2 sio chhi3-phe3, soa3 sio-tioh8 tiu7-tui, a2-si7 iau2-be7 koah e5 tiu7, a2-si7 chhan5-hng5, chiu7 khi2-he2 e5 lang5 tek-khak tioh8 pe5.
	7). Lang5 na7 chiong gun5 a2-si7 mih8-kiaN7, kau-tai3 chhu3-piN kou3-siu2, chiah e5 mih8, na7 tui3 hit-lang5 e5 ke tioh8 chhat8 thau, chhat8 na7 liah8-tioh8, chhat8 tioh8 pe5 teng5-pe7;  8). chhat8 na7 liah8-bo5-tioh8, hit e5 ke-chu2 tioh8 kau3 koaN-hu2 bin7-cheng5, khoaN3 i u7 theh8 chhu3-piN e5 mih8-kiaN7 a2-bo5.  9). KiN3-na7 u7 ke3-sit, kiam2-chhai2 si7 ui7-tioh8 gu5, lu5, iuN5, a2-si7 ui7-tioh8 i-chiuN5 a2-si7 sim2-mih8 sit-loh8 e5 mih8, u7 lang5 jin7-tit si7 i-e5, siang-peng5 e5 an3-kiaN7 tioh8 kau3 koaN-hu2 e5 bin7-cheng5; koaN-hu2 na7 toan3-teng7 sim2-mih8 lang5 u7 choe7, hit-lang5 tioh8 pe5 i e5 chhu3-piN teng5-pe7.  10). Lang5 na7 chiong lu5, a2-si7 gu5, a2-si7 iuN5, a2-si7 pat8-ho7 cheng-siN, kau-tai3 chhu3-piN kou3-siu2, cheng-siN kiam2-chhai2 si2, a2-si7 siu7-siong, a2-si7 hou7 lang5 khan--khi3, bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3;  11). nng7-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, tioh8 ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu3-choa7, m7-bat theh8 chhu3-piN e5 mih8, goan5-chu2 chiu7 tioh8 soah, kou3-siu2 e5 lang5 m7-bian2 pe5.  12). Cheng-siN na7 tui3 kou3-siu2 e5 lang5 hiah hou7 lang5 thau--khi3, i chiu7 tioh8 pe5 goan5-chu2.  13). Na7 siu7 ia2-siu3 thiah-chhui3, kou3-siu2 e5 lang5 tioh8 toa3 i lai5 choe3 cheng3-ku3; sou2 thiah-chhui3--e5 chiu7 m7-bian2 pe5.
	14). Lang5 na7 tui3 chhu3-piN chioh sim2-mih8 mih8, sou2 chioh--e5 kiam2-chhai2 siu7-siong a2-si7 si2, goan5-chu2 bo5 saN-kap ti7-teh, i tek-khak tioh8 pe5.  15). Na7 goan5-chu2 saN-kap ti7-teh, i chiu7 m7-bian2 pe5; na7 si7 chou--e5, ia7 m7-bian2 pe5, in-ui7 pun2 u7 chou-chiN5.
	16). Lang5 na7 in2-iu2 be7 siu7 pheng3 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 kap i tang5-pang5, i tioh8 pheng3 i choe3-bou2.  17). Na7 i e5 lau7-pe7 koat-toan3 m7-kheng2 chiong cha-bou2-kiaN2 phoe3--i, i chiu7 tioh8 chiau3 chai7-sek-lu2 e5 pheng3-le2, hou7 i gun5.
	18). Choe3 ang-i5--e5, tioh8 hou7 i si2.
	19). KiN3-na7 kap siu3 im5--e5, tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.
	20). Bo5 choan-choan che3-su7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lai5 che3-su7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3--e5, tioh8 biat8--i.
	21). M7-thang khi-hu7 chhut-goa7 lang5, ia7 m7-thang ap-che3 i; in-ui7 lin2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ia7 bat choe3 chhut-goa7 lang5.  22). M7-thang phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 koaN2-hu7 kap kou-ji5.  23). Na7 sio2-khoa2 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7--in, in kiu5-kio3 Goa2, Goa2 tek-khak beh thiaN in e5 kiu5-kio3.  24). Ia7 beh toa7 siu7-khi3, eng7 to thai5--lin2; hou7 lin2 e5 bou2 choe3 koaN2-hu7, lin2 e5 kiaN2 choe3 kou-ji5.
	25). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong u7 song3-hiong lang5 kap lin2 khia7-khi2, li2 na7 chioh i gun5, li2 m7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 che3-chu2 khoan2-thai7 i, ia7 m7-thang theh8 i e5 li7-sek.  26). Li2 na7 theh8 chhu3-piN e5 i-chiuN5 choe3 chun2-tng3, jit8-loh8 chiu7 tioh8 heng5--i;  27). i chi2-u7 chit-kiaN7 thang kah, si7 i jia seng-khu e5 saN; na7 bo5, i beh chaiN2-iuN7 khun3? i kiu5--Goa2, Goa2 beh thiaN, in-ui7 Goa2 si7 chu5-pi--e5.
	28). M7-thang hui2-pong3 koaN-hu2; ia7 m7-thang me7 li2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 si7-toa7.  29). Li2 tioh8 tui3 sou2 siu-seng5 e5 gou7-kak, kap chiu2-khut-lai7 sou2 lau5-chhut e5 chiu2, theh8-lai5 hian3, m7-thang ian5-chhian5.  30). Li2 tioh8 chiong thau5-chiuN7 e5 kiaN2 kui ti7 Goa2; li2 e5 gu5, li2 e5 iuN5, ia7 tioh8 an2-ni; chhit-jit8 thang te3 i e5 bu2, ti7 poeh-jit8 tioh8 kui ti7 Goa2.  31). Lin2 tioh8 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 choe3 seng3 e5 peh-siN3; sou2-i2 chhan5--nih ia2-siu3 sou2 thiah-lih8 e5 bah, lin2 m7-thang chiah8, tioh8 hiat hou7 kau2.

[23]	M7-thang po3-iong5 iau5-gian5; m7-thang kap phaiN2-lang5 lian5-hap8 choe3 lam7-sam2 e5 kan-cheng3.  2). M7-thang te3 cheng3-lang5 kiaN5-phaiN2; ti7 saN-ko3 e5 su7, m7-thang phian-oa2 toa7-peng5, kong2 i e5 oe7, lai5 oan-ong2 cheng3-tit8.  3). M7-thang ti7 saN-ko3 e5 su7, than2-hou7 song3-hiong lang5.
	4). Na7 tu2-tioh8 li2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 gu5, a2-si7 lu5, sit-be5 lou7, tek-khak tioh8 khan to3--lai5 kau--i.  5). Na7 khoaN3-kiN3 oan3-hun7 li2 e5 lang5 e5 lu5 pe7-chai3 teh-to2, m7-thang kiaN5-khui, tioh8 kap i saN-kap pang3 lu5 sou2 chai3--e5.
	6). Song3-hiong lang5 u7 saN-ko3, li2 m7-thang phian-toan3.  7). Tioh8 li7-khui hu-ke2 e5 su7 hng7-hng7; m7-thang thai5 bo5-choe7 kap gi7 e5 lang5; in-ui7 phaiN2-lang5 Goa2 tek-khak bo5 sng3 i choe3 gi7.  8). M7-thang siu7 pou3-lou7, in-ui7 pou3-lou7 oe7 hou7 bak8-chiu kim e5 lang5 pian3 chhiN-mi5, koh oe7 chiong gi7-lang5 e5 oe7 peng2-to3-tng2.  9). M7-thang ap-che3 chhut-goa7 lang5; in-ui7 lin2 bat chhut-goa7 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, chai chhut-goa7 lang5 e5 sim.
	10). Lak8-ni5-lai7 li2 tioh8 cheng3-choh li2 e5 chhan5-hng5, siu-seng5 thou2-san2.  11). Tok8-tok8 te7-chhit ni5, tioh8 hou7 thou2-toe7 hioh-khun3 bo5 cheng3-choh, hou7 li2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong e5 song3-hiong lang5 u7 thang chiah8; sou2 chhun--e5 thang hou7 ia2-siu3 chiah8; li2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 kap kaN-na2-hng5, ia7 tioh8 an2-ni.  12). Lak8-jit8-lai7 li2 tioh8 choe3 li2 e5 kang, te7-chhit jit8 tioh8 an-hioh, hou7 gu5 lu5 thang hioh-khun3, ia7 hou7 lu2-pi7 e5 kiaN2 kap chhut-goa7 lang5 long2 thang iong2 cheng-lek8.  13). KiN3-na7 Goa2 tui3 lin2 kong2 e5 oe7, lin2 tioh8 kin2-sin7 siu2; pat8 e5 siong7-te3 e5 mia5, li2 m7-thang the5-khi2, ia7 m7-thang kong2 hou7 lang5 thiaN.  14). Chit8-ni5 saN-pai2 li2 tioh8 siu2-choeh hok8-sai7 Goa2.  15). A-pit geh8, li2 chhut Ai-kip8, kau3 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 ki5, tioh8 siu2 tu5-kaN3-choeh; chhit-jit8 ku2 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2, chiau3 Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5; tiau5-kiN3 Goa2 e5 lang5 m7-thang khang-chhiu2.  16). Koh u7 siu-koah e5 choeh, chiu7-si7 li2 ti7 chhan5--nih chai-cheng3, tui3 tioh8-boa5 tit-tioh8 khi2-thau5 sek8 e5 thou2-san2.  Koh u7 siu-khng3 e5 choeh, chiu7-si7 ni5-be2, lin2 siu-khng3 tui3 chhan5--nih tioh8-boa5 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5.  17). Chit8-ni5 saN-pai2, li2 it-chhe3 e5 ta-pou-teng tioh8 kau3 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.
	18). Che3-su7 Goa2 e5 seng-le2, i e5 huih m7-thang chham u7 kaN3 e5 mih8 lai5 hian3; ia7 m7-thang chiong Goa2 choeh-ki5 seng-le2 e5 iu5 lau5 kau3 ke3 cha2-khi2.  19). Toe7--nih te7-it khi2-thau5 sek8 e5 mih8, tioh8 sang3 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3.  Chu2 soaN-iuN5-a2 m7-thang eng7 i e5 bu2 e5 lin.
	20). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chhe Goa2 e5 su3-chia2 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5, ti7 lou7--nih po2-hou7 li2, chhoa7 li2 kau3 Goa2 sou2 pi7-pan7 e5 toe7.  21). Lin2 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 tioh8 kin2-sin7, thiaN-than3 i e5 oe7, m7-thang ui5-keh8 i; i bo5 beh sia3-bian2 lin2 e5 ke3-sit; in-ui7 i hong7 Goa2 e5 mia5.  22). Li2 na7 sit8-chai7 thiaN-than3 i e5 oe7, chiau3 Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 kong2--e5 khi3 kiaN5, Goa2 chiu7 choe3 li2 e5 kiu5-siu5 e5 kiu5-siu5, li2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 tui3-tek8.  23). Goa2 e5 su3-chia2 beh kiaN5 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5, chhoa7 li2 kau3 A-mou5-li7, Hek, Pi2-li7-se2, Ka-lam5, Hi-bi7, Ia5-pou3-su hiah e5 chok8 e5 toe7; Goa2 beh chian2-tu5 in.  24). In e5 siong7-te3 li2 m7-thang kui7-pai3, ia7 m7-thang hok8-sai7; m7-thang oh8 in e5 sou2-choe3, tioh8 it-chin7 hui2-biat8 in, phah-chhui3 in tiau-khek e5 thiau7.  25). Lin2 tioh8 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3; I tek-khak su3-hok ti7 li2 e5 bi2-niu5 kap li2 e5 chui2; koh Goa2 beh tu5--khi3 lin2 tiong-kan e5 phoa3-piN7.  26). Ia7 beh hou7 li2 e5 keng2-lai7, bo5 u7 ka-lauh8-thai--e5, bo5 u7 boe7 siN--e5; Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 he3-siu7 moa2-chiok.  27). Goa2 beh choe3 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5, lai5 si7-ui; li2 sou2 kau3 e5 sou2-chai7, hiah e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh hou7 in si2-bo5; koh beh hou7 li2 it-chhe3 e5 tui3-tek8 oat8-tng2-sin to5-chau2.  28). Goa2 beh chhe toa7-chiah-phang ti7 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5, koaN2-chhut Hi-bi7 lang5, Ka-lam5 lang5, Hek lang5, li7-khui li2.  29). Ti7 chit8-ni5-lai7 Goa2 bo5 beh tui3 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5 it-chin7 koaN2 in chhut, kiaN-liau2 thou2-toe7 pha-hng, ia2-siu3 ke-thiN choe7-choe7 lai5 hai7 lin2.  30). Goa2 beh chiam7-chiam7 tui3 lin2 e5 thau5-cheng5 koaN2 in chhut, theng3-hau7 lin2 lang5-giah8 ke-thiN choe7-choe7, lai5 seng5-siu7 hit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8.  31). Goa2 beh tiaN7-tioh8 li2 e5 keng2-kai3, tui3 Ang5-hai2 kau3 Hui-li7-su7 e5 hai2, koh tui3 khong3-ia2 kau3 Toa7-ho5.  In-ui7 Goa2 beh chiong hit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 kau ti7 lin2 e5 chhiu2, hou7 li2 chiong in tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut.  32). M7-thang kap in, i2-kip8 in e5 siong7-te3, lip8-iok.  33). M7-thang hou7 in khia7-khi2 li2 e5 thou2-toe7, kiaN-liau2 in hou7 li2 tek-choe7 Goa2; li2 na7 hok8-sai7 in e5 siong7-te3, che beh choe3 li2 e5 lo5-bang7.

[24]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 kap A-lun5, Na2-tap, A-pi2-hou7, kap I2-sek-liat8 tiuN2-lo2-tiong chhit-chap8 lang5, long2 tioh8 chiuN7 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chia, hng7-hng7 phak--loh8-khi3 pai3.  2). Tok8-tok8 Mou5-se thang chhin-kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ki5-u5 m7-thang chhin-kun7; peh-siN3 ia7 m7-thang kap i chiuN7-lai5.  3). Mou5-se kau3, chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa it-chhe3 e5 oe7, it-chhe3 e5 hoat-tou7, kong2 hou7 peh-siN3 thiaN; cheng3 peh-siN3 tang5-siaN in3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, goan2 beh long2 chun-than3.  4). Mou5-se chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, long2 sia2--khi2-lai5; thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, ti7 soaN-e7 khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3, khia7 chap8-ji7 ki thiau7.  5). Koh chhe I2-sek-liat8-tiong e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, khi3 hian3 sio-che3.  Ia7 eng7 gu5 choe3 peng5-an-che3, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  6). Mou5-se chiong huih e5 chit8-poaN3 toe2 ti7 phun5--nih, chit8-poaN3 hiu3 ti7 toaN5--nih.  7). Koh theh8 iok e5 chheh, thak8 hou7 peh-siN3 thiaN; in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5, goan2 beh long2 chun-than3 lai5 kiaN5.  8). Mou5-se chiong huih hiu3 peh-siN3, kong2, KhoaN3 ah, che si7 lip8-iok e5 huih, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 che it-chhe3 e5 oe7 kap lin2 sou2 lip8--e5.  9). Mou5-se, A-lun5, Na2-tap, A-pi2-hou7, kap I2-sek-liat8 tiuN2-lo2-tiong chhit-chap8-lang5, long2 chiuN7-khi3.  10). In khoaN3-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, I e5 kha-e7 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 piN5-phou e5 lam5-po2-chioh8, chhin-chhiuN7 thiN goan5-chit e5 kng-liang7.  11). I bo5 chhut-chhiu2 hai7 I2-sek-liat8 chun-kui3 e5 lang5; in khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3, in ia7 chiah8 ia7 lim.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 chiuN7-soaN chiu7-kun7 Goa2, tiam3 ti7-chia, Goa2 beh chiong chioh8-pi kap lut8-hoat, i2-kip8 kai3-beng7, Goa2 sou2 sia2--e5, siuN2-su3 li2, thang ka3-si7 in.  13). Mou5-se kap kun-sui5 i e5 Iok-su-a khi2-lai5; Mou5-se chiuN7 Siong7-te3 e5 soaN;  14). ka7 tiuN2-lo2 kong2, Lin2 tiam3 chia tan2 goan2, theng3-hau7 goan2 to3-tng2--lai5 lin2 chia; khoaN3 ah, A-lun5 Hou7-jiN2 kap lin2 ti7-teh; lang5 na7 u7 tai7-chi3, thang lai5 chhe7 in.  15). Mou5-se chiuN7 soaN, soaN u7 hun5 jia-kham3.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng theng5 ti7 Se-nai2 soaN, hun5 jia i lak8-jit8 ku2; te7-chhit jit8 I tui3 hun5-tiong kio3 Mou5-se.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa eng5-kng e5 khoan2-sit, chhin-chhiuN7 he2 sio ti7 soaN-teng2; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3.  18). Mou5-se jip8 hun5-tiong chiuN7-soaN; Mou5-se ti7 soaN-teng2 si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8-mi5.

[25]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Tioh8 hian3 le2-mih8 hou7 Goa2; kiN3-na7 sim sou2 kam-goan7--e5, lin2 thang ka7 i siu--lai5, choe3 le2-mih8 hou7 Goa2.  3). Sou2 tioh8 siu e5 le2-mih8, chiu7-si7 kim, gun5, tang5,  4). lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, iu3-toe7, soaN-iuN5-mng5,  5). ni2 ang5 e5 kang-iuN5-phe5, hai2-kau2 phe5,  6). cho7-kiap-chha5, tiam2 teng e5 iu5, phang-phang e5 phin2-liau7, thang choe3 ko-iu5 lai5 boah, ia7 choe3 phang-hiuN,  7). ang5-be2-lo2, kap pat8-iuN7 e5 po2-chioh8, thang siuN i2-hut-tek kap pou2-koa3.  8). In tioh8 ka7 Goa2 khi2 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7, hou7 Goa2 thang tiam3 ti7 in tiong-kan.  9). Chiau3 Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 chi2-si7 li2 e5, chiu7-si7 hoe7-bou7 e5 khoan2-sit, kap lai7-tiong khi2-ku7 khoan2-sit, lin2 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni lai5 cho7.
	10). In tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 chit8 e5 kui7, tng5 nng7-tiu2-poaN3, khoah tiu2-poaN3, koaiN5 tiu2-poaN3.  11). Li2 tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim pau, lai7-goa7 long2 tioh8 pau; si3-ui5 tioh8 khi2 kim-soaN3.  12). Li2 tioh8 ka7 i chu3 si3 e5 kim-khoan5, an ti7 i e5 si3-kha, chit-peng5 nng7-khoan5, hit-peng5 nng7-khoan5.  13). Tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 nng7 ki kng3, eng7 kim pau i.  14). Tioh8 chiong kng3 chhng ti7 kui7-piN e5 khoan5-lai7, thang eng7 lai5 kng kui7;  15). chiah e5 kng3 tioh8 siong5-siong5 ti7 kui7 e5 khoan5-lai7, m7-thang thiu--chhut-lai5.  16). Tioh8 eng7 Goa2 sou2 beh siuN2-su3 li2 e5 lut8-hoat he7 ti7 kui7-lai7.  17). Tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim choe3 si-un-sou2, tng5 nng7-tiu2-poaN3, khoah tiu2-poaN3.  18). Tioh8 eng7 kim choe3 nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng, eng7 phah e5 hoat choe3--i, ti7 si-un-sou2 e5 siang-thau5.  19). Chit-thau5 choe3 chit8 e5 ki-lou7-peng, hit-thau5 choe3 chit8 e5 ki-lou7-peng; siang-thau5 e5 ki-lou7-peng, kap si-un-sou2, tioh8 kui-te3, choe3 saN-lian5.  20). Nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng tioh8 koaiN5-koaiN5 thi2-khui sit8, eng7 in e5 sit8 jia si-un-sou2; in e5 bin7 tioh8 saN-tui3; ki-lou7-peng e5 bin7 tioh8 aN3 si-un-sou2.  21). Tioh8 chiong si-un-sou2 an ti7 kui7-teng2, koh chiong Goa2 sou2 beh siuN2-su3 li2 e5 lut8-hoat he7 ti7 kui7-lai7.  22). Goa2 beh ti7-hia kap li2 chu7-hoe7, koh beh tui3 si-un-sou2 teng2, chiu7-si7 tui3 hoat-kui7 teng2, nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng e5 tiong-kan, kap li2 kong2 Goa2 sou2 beh hoan-hu3 li2 thoan5 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chhe3 e5 su7.
	23). Li2 tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 chit8 te3 toh, tng5 nng7-tiu2, khoah chit8-tiu2, koaiN5 tiu2-poaN3.  24). Tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim pau, si3-ui5 khi2 kim-soaN3.  25). Toh e5 si3-ui5, kok choe3 chit8 pa-chiuN2 khoah e5 hoaiN5-niu5, hoaiN5-niu5-teng2 si3-ui5 khi2 kim-soaN3.  26). Li2 tioh8 choe3 si3 e5 kim-khoan5, an ti7 i e5 si3-kha e5 si3-kak.  27). An khoan5 e5 sou2-chai7 tioh8 oa2-kun7 hoaiN5-niu5, thang chhng-kng3 lai5 kng toh.  28). Tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 nng7 ki kng3 eng7 kim pau--i, thang eng7 lai5 kng toh.  29). Tioh8 choe3 poaN5, oaN2, poe, pan5, thang lai5 koan3-tian7, long2 tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim choe3.  30). Toh-teng2 siong5-siong5 he7 pai5-liat8 e5 piaN2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
	31). Li2 tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim choe3 chit8 e5 teng-tai5; teng-tai5 e5 cho7, kap tiong-thiau7, i e5 poe, i e5 bak8, i e5 hoe, long2 eng7 phah e5 hoat, choe3 kui-cho7.  32). Ti7 i e5 piN-a2 tioh8 pun-chhut lak8-ki; teng-tai5 e5 chit-peng5 tioh8 u7 saN-ki, teng-tai5 e5 hit-peng5 tioh8 u7 saN-ki.  33). Chit-peng5 mui2-ki u saN e5 poe, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 heng7-hoe, u7 bak8 u7 hoe; hit-peng5 mui2-ki ia7 u7 saN e5 poe, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 heng7-hoe, u7 bak8 u7 hoe; tui3 teng-tai5 pun-chhut e5 lak8-ki long2 si7 an2-ni.  34). Teng-tai5-thiau7 u7 si3 e5 poe, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 heng7-hoe, u7 i e5 bak8 kap i e5 hoe.  35). Nng7-ki e5 e7-bin7 u7 chit8 bak8 kap i saN-lian5, koh nng7-ki e5 e7-bin7 u7 chit8 bak8 kap i saN-lian5, koh nng7-ki e5 e7-bin7 u7 chit8-bak8 kap i saN-lian5; teng-tai5 sou2 chhut e5 lak8-ki long2 si7 an2-ni.  36). Hiah e5 bak8 kap hiah e5 ki, long2 kap i lian5 choe3 chit8-e5, long2 eng7 ho2-kim, chiau3 phah e5 hoat choe3.  37). Tioh8 ka7 i choe3 chhit e5 teng-choaN2, tioh8 tiam2 hiah e5 teng, hou7 i chio3-kng ti7 tui3-bin7.  38). Teng-tai5 e5 chian2 kap i e5 poaN5, long2 tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim choe3--i.  39). Choe3 teng-tai5 kap che it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, eng7 ho2-kim chit8 tha-lian5-tek.  40). Li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7 choe3 chiah e5 mih8-kiaN7, long2 tioh8 chiau3 ti7 soaN-teng2 chi2-si7 li2 e5 khoan2-sit.

[26]	Li2 choe3 hoe7-bou7 tioh8 eng7 chap8-pak e5 tiuN3; chiah e5 tiuN3 si7 eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, ia7 eng7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang chit-chiaN5 ki-lou7-peng, lai5 choe3--e5.  2). Mui2 pak tiuN3 tioh8 tng5 ji7-chap8 poeh tiu2, khoah si3-tiu2; tiuN3 long2 tioh8 chit8-iuN7 e5 chhun3-chhioh.  3). Chit gou7 pak tiuN3 tioh8 tak8-pak saN-lian5; hit gou7 pak tiuN3 ia7 tioh8 tak8-pak saN-lian5.  4). Ti7 chit e5 saN-lian5 e5 tiuN3, lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2, tioh8 choe3 lam5-sek e5 liu2-phan3; ti7 hit e5 saN-lian5 e5 tiuN3, lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2, iah8 tioh8 an2-ni choe3.  5). Li2 ti7 chit-nia2 tiuN3 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3; koh ti7 te7-ji7 nia2 tiuN3, saN-lian5 e5 piN-a2, ia7 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3; liu2-phan3 long2 tioh8 nng7-e5 nng7-e5 saN-tui3.  6). Koh tioh8 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 kim-kau lai5 kau, hou7 tiuN3 saN-lian5; chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 hoe7-bou7.
	7). Li2 tioh8 eng7 soaN-iuN5-mng5 chit chap8-it pak e5 tiuN3, choe3 hoe7-bou7-teng2 e5 pou3-piN5;  8). mui2 pak tiuN3 tioh8 tng5 saN-chap8 tiu2, khoah si3 tiu2; chap8-it pak tiuN3 long2 tioh8 chit8-iuN7 e5 chhun3-chhioh.  9). Tioh8 chiong gou7 pak tiuN3 lian5-choe3 chit8-pak, koh chiong lak8 pak tiuN3 lian5-choe3 chit8-pak, hit-e5 te7-lak8 pak e5 chit8-poaN3, hou7 i sui5-loh8 ti7 pou3-piN5 e5 thau5-cheng5.  10). Ti7 chit-e5 saN-lian5 e5 tiuN3, lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2, tioh8 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3, ti7 hit-e5 saN-lian5, lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2, ia7 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3.  11). Koh tioh8 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 tang5-kau, kau ti7 liu2-phan3, hou7 pou3-piN5 lian5 choe3 chit8-e5.  12). Pou3-piN5 e5 tiuN3 sou2 chhun sui5--loh8-lai5, chiu7-si7 sou2 chhun hit-e5 poaN3 pak tiuN3, tioh8 sui5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-au7.  13). Pou3-piN5 e5 tiuN3 sou2 chhun e5 tng5, chit-peng5 chit8 tiu2, hit-peng5 chit8 tiu2, tioh8 sui5 ti7 hoe7-bou7 e5 siang-peng5 lai5 jia--i.  14). Koh tioh8 eng7 ni2-ang5 kang e5 iuN5-phe5, choe3 pou3-piN5 e5 koa3; koh eng7 hai2-kau2-phe5 choe3 koa3 ti7 teng2-bin7.
	15). Li2 tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 hoe7-bou7 khia7 e5 pan2.  16). Khia7 e5 pan2 tng5 chap8-tiu2, khoah chit8 tiu2 poaN3.  17). Tak8 te3 pan2 tioh8 u7 nng7 e5 sun2 saN-pai5; hoe7-bou7 it-chhe3 e5 pan2 long2 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni choe3.  18). Tioh8 choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 pan2, lam5-peng5 e5 lam5--si3 ji7-chap8 te3 pan2.  19). Ti7 chiah-e5 ji7-chap8 te3 pan2 e5 e7-bin7, tioh8 choe3 si3-chap8 e5 gun5-khu7; chit8 te3 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7 lai5 chheng7 i nng7 ki sun2; koh chit8 te3 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 ia7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7 lai5 chheng7 i nng7 ki sun2.  20). Hoe7-bou7 te7-ji7-bin7, chiu7-si7 pak-bin7, ia7 tioh8 choe3 pan2 ji7-chap8 te3, kap in e5 gun5-khu7 si3-chap8-e5;  21). chit e5 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7, hit e5 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 ia7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7.  22). Hoe7-bou7 e5 au7-bin7, chiu7-si7 sai-bin7, tioh8 choe3 lak8 te3 pan2.  23). Hoe7-bou7 au7-bin7 e5 nng7 e5 kak-thau5, tioh8 choe3 nng7 te3 pan2.  24). Pan2 e5 e7-tng5, nng7-e5 saN-tang5, tit8-kau3 teng2-bin7 te7-it e5 khoan5, long2-si7 ka-nng5 e5; nng7-te3 long2 si7 an2-ni, beh choe3 kak-thau5 e5 lou7-eng7.  25). Tioh8 u7 poeh e5 pan2, kap chap8-lak8 e5 gun5-khu7; chit e5 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7, hit-e5 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 ia7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7.
	26). Li2 tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 hoaiN5-kong5; ui7-tioh8 hoe7-bou7 chit-peng5 e5 pan2 choe3 gou7-ki;  27). ui7-tioh8 hoe7-bou7 hit-peng5 e5 pan2 choe3 gou7-ki, koh ui7 hoe7-bou7-au7 e5 sai-bin7 choe3 gou7-ki.  28). Pan2 e5 tui3-tiong hit ki hoaiN5-kong5, tioh8 tui3 chit-thau5 thau3 kau3 hit-thau5.  29). Pan2 tioh8 eng7 kim pau; koh tioh8 choe3 pan2 e5 kim-khoan5 lai5 tho3-kong5; kong5 ia7 tioh8 eng7 kim pau.  30). Tioh8 chiau3 ti7 soaN-teng2 chi2-si7 li2 e5 khoan2-sit khi2 hoe7-bou7.
	31). Li2 tioh8 eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, chit tiuN3-li5; chit e5 tiuN3-li5 eng7 ki5-khiau3 e5 kang, chit-chiaN5 ki-lou7-peng, lai5 choe3--e5.  32). Li2 tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 si3 ki thiau7, eng7 kim pau i, lai5 tiau3 tiuN3-li5; thiau7 e5 kau tioh8 kim--e5; thiau7 ti7 si3 e5 gun5-khu teng2.  33). Li2 tiau3 tiuN3-li5 tioh8 ti7 kau e5 e7-toe2 e5 sou2-chai7, chiong hoat-kui7 kng-jip8 tiuN3-li5-lai7, chit e5 tiuN3-li5 si7 ka7 lin2 keh-khui seng3-sou2 kap chi3-seng3-sou2.  34). Koh tioh8 chiong si-un-sou2 an ti7 chi3-seng3-sou2 lai7 e5 hoat-kui7-teng2.  35). Li2 tioh8 eng7 toh he7 ti7 tiuN3-li5-goa7; ia7 eng7 teng-tai5 he7 ti7 hoe7-bou7 e5 lam5--si3, kap toh saN-tui3; hit e5 toh tioh8 he7 ti7 pak--si3.
	36). Li2 tioh8 eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, eng7 siu3-hoe e5 kang, choe3 pou3-piN5 mng5 e5 mng5-li5.  37). Tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 ka7 mng5-li5 choe3 gou7 ki thiau7, eng7 kim pau--i, thiau7 e5 kau tioh8 kim--e5.  Koh tioh8 ka7 thiau7 chu3 gou7 e5 tang5-khu7.

[27]	Li2 tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 toaN5, tng5 gou7 tiu2 khoah gou7 tiu2; chit e5 toaN5 si7 su3-hong--e5, koaiN5 saN tiu2.  2). Tioh8 ti7 toaN5 e5 si3-kak-thau5 choe3 si3 ki kak, kap toaN5 saN-lian5 choe3 chit8-e5, eng7 tang5 pau i.  3). Tioh8 choe3 phun5, lai5 siu i e5 hu, koh choe3 i e5 thuh-a2, i e5 poaN5, i e5 chhe, i e5 he2-tiaN2, i it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, long2 eng7 tang5 choe3.  4). Tioh8 eng7 tang5 ka7 i choe3 chit8 e5 bang7, ti7 bang7 e5 si3-kak choe3 si3 e5 tang5 khoan5.  5). Eng7 bang7 he7 ti7 toaN5 si3-bin7 ui5-io-pan2 e5 e7-bin7, hou7 bang7 thau3 kau3 toaN5 e5 poaN3-io.  6). tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 ka7 toaN5 choe3 kng3, eng7 tang5 pau i.  7). Hiah e5 kng3 tioh8 chhng ti7 khoan5-lai7, kng3 tioh8 ti7 toaN5 e5 siang-peng5, lai5 kng--i.  8). Tioh8 eng7 pan2 choe3 toaN5, tiong-ng khang-khak; long2 tioh8 chiau3 soaN-teng2 chi2-si7 li2 e5 khoan2-sit lai5 choe3.
	9). Li2 tioh8 choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 tiuN5; tiuN5 e5 lam5-bin7 e5 lam5--si3, tioh8 eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3 ui5 ti7 chit8-peng5, tng5 chit8-pah tiu2.  10). I e5 thiau7 ji7-chap8 ki, tang5-khu7 ji7-chap8 e5; thiau7 e5 kau kap hoaiN5-koaiN, long2 tioh8 eng7 gun5 choe3 i.  11). Pak-bin7 ia7 tioh8 u7 ui5, tng5 chit8-pah tiu2; i e5 thiau7 ji7-chap8 ki, tang5-khu7 ji7-chap8-e5; thiau7 e5 kau kap hoaiN5-koaiN, long2 tioh8 eng7 gun5 choe3.  12). TiuN5 e5 sai-bin7 tioh8 u7 ui5, khoah gou7-chap8 tiu2; ui5 e5 thiau7 chap8-ki, khu7 chap8-e5.  13). TiuN5 e5 tang-bin7 e5 tang--si3 khoah gou7-chap8 tiu2.  14). Mng5 chit-peng5 e5 ui5 tioh8 chap8-gou7 tiu2, ui5 e5 thiau7 saN-ki, khu7 saN-e5.  15). Mng5 hit-peng5 e5 ui5 ia7 tioh8 chap8-gou7 tiu2; ui5 e5 thiau7 saN-ki, khu7 saN-e5.  16). TiuN5 e5 mng5 tioh8 u7 mng5-li5, khoah ji7-chap8 tiu2, tioh8 eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, eng7 siu3-hoe e5 kang choe3; thiau7 si3-ki, khu7 si3-e5.  17). TiuN5 si3-ui5 it-chhe3 e5 thiau7, long2 tioh8 u7 gun5 e5 hoaiN5-koaiN, gun5 e5 kau, tang5 e5 khu7.  18). TiuN5 e5 tng5 chit8-pah tiu2, khoah tak8-bin7 gou7-chap8 tiu2, koaiN5 gou7 tiu2; ui5 tioh8 eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3; i e5 khu7 long2 eng7 tang5 choe3.  19). Hoe7-bou7 sou2 eng7 tak8-hang7 e5 khi3-ku7, kap sou2 teng3 e5 teng, i2-kip8 tiuN5-lai7 sou2 teng3 e5 teng, long2 tioh8 eng7 tang5 choe3.
	20). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, chiong hit-e5 ui7-tioh8 beh chio3-kng sou2 khoeh-chheng e5 kaN-na2-iu5, theh8--lai5 hou7 li2, hou7 teng siong5-siong5 tiam2-teh.  21). Ti7 hoe7-bou7-tiong hoat-kui7-cheng5 e5 tiuN3-li5 goa7, A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2, tui3 e5-hng kau3 thiN-kng tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 liau7-li2--i; si7 choe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tai7-tai7 eng2-oan2 e5 le7.

[28]	Li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, hou7 li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2, lai5 li2 chia, thang choe3 che3-si, hok8-sai7 Goa2, chiu7-si7 A-lun5, kap A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 Na2-tap, A-pi2-hou7, I2-li7-a-sat, I2-tha-ma2.  2). Li2 tioh8 ka7 li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 choe3 seng3 e5 saN, hou7 i eng5-kng koh sui2.  3). Koh tioh8 hoan-hu3 it-chhe3 sim u7 ti3-hui7--e5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 eng7 ti3-hui7 e5 sin5 sou2 chhiong-moa2 e5 lang5, ka7 A-lun5 choe3 saN, hun-piat i choe3-seng3, thang choe3 che3-si hok8-sai7 Goa2.  4). In sou2 tioh8 choe3 e5 saN, chiu7-si7 pou2-koa3, i2-hut-tek, goa7-phau3, u7-hoe e5 lai7-saN, bo7, io-toa3.  In tioh8 ka7 li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 choe3 seng3 e5 saN, hou7 i choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7 Goa2.  5). In tioh8 eng7 kim, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap iu3-toe7 choe3--i.
	6). In tioh8 eng7 kim, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, eng7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang choe3 i2-hut-tek.  7). Tioh8 u7 phi-kian nng7 te3, lian5 ti7 siang-peng5, hou7 i saN-lian5.  8). I2-hut-tek teng2-bin7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang sou2 chit e5 toa3, tioh8 kap i tang5 chit8-iuN7 e5 choe3-hoat; hou7 i saN-lian5 choe3 chit8-e5; eng7 kim, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, i2-kip8 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3--e5.  9). Tioh8 theh8 nng7 te3 ang5-be2-lo2, ti7 teng2-bin7 khek I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5;  10). Lak8 e5 mia5 ti7 chit-te3 po2-chioh8, ki5-u5 lak8 e5 mia5 ti7 hit-te3 po2-chioh8, long2 chiau3 in chhut-si3 e5 chhu3-su7.  11). Tioh8 eng7 khek po2-chioh8 e5 chhiu2-kang, chhin-chhiuN7 khek-in3, chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5, khek chi2 nng7-te3 po2-chioh8, jip8 ti7 kim-cho5--nih.  12). Tioh8 chiong chi2 nng7-te3 po2-chioh8, an ti7 i2-hut-tek e5 phi-kian-teng2, ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3 ki3-liam7-chioh8.  A-lun5 tioh8 ti7 nng7 e5 keng-thau5 pe7 in e5 mia5, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, choe3 ki3-liam7.  13). Tioh8 eng7 kim choe3 nng7 te3 cho5.  14). Koh eng7 ho2-kim, chhin-chhiuN7 phah soh-a2, lai5 choe3 nng7 tiau5 lian7-a2, chiong chiah-e5 phah-chiaN5 e5 lian7-a2, an ti7 hiah e5 cho5--nih.
	15). Li2 tioh8 eng7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang, choe3 chit8-e5 phoaN3-toan3 e5 pou2-koa3; tioh8 kap i2-hut-tek tang5 chit8-iuN7 e5 choe3-hoat; eng7 kim, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7 i2-kip8 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3--i.  16). Pou2-koa3 tioh8 su3-hong, au2 siang-teng5; tng5 chit8-liah8, khoah chit8-liah8.  17). Li2 tioh8 jip8 chiah e5 po2-chioh8 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7, u7 po2-chioh8 si3-choa7; chit8-choa7 si7 ang5-po2-chioh8, ng5-gek8, chhiah-gek8, che si7 te7-it-choa7.  18). Te7-ji7-choa7 si7 lek8-po2-chioh8, lam5-gek8, kim-kong-chioh8.  19). Te7-saN-choa7 si7 chi2-sek e5 be2-lo2, peh8-be2-lo2, chi2-sek chui2-chiN.  20). Te7-si3-choa7 si7 chhiN-gek8, ang5-be2-lo2, phek-gek8; che long2 tioh8 jip8 ti7 kim-cho5-lai7.  21). Chiah e5 po2-chioh8 chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5, kiong7 chap8-ji7 te3, chhin-chhiuN7 khek-in3, mui2-te3 khek chit8 e5 mia5, ui7-tioh8 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3 lai5 choe3--i.  22). Tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim phah lian7-a2, chhin-chhiuN7 soh-a2, an ti7 pou2-koa3.  23). Ti7 pou2-koa3 tioh8 choe3 nng7 e5 kim-khoan5, chiong chi2 nng7 e5 khoan5 an ti7 pou2-koa3 e5 siang-thau5.  24). Tioh8 chiong sou2 phah hit nng7 tiau5 kim lian7-a2, lian5 ti7 pou2-koa3 siang-thau5 nng7 e5 khoan5.  25). Eng7 sou2 phah nng7 tiau5 lian7-a2 e5 siang-thau5, lian5 ti7 nng7 e5 cho5, an ti7 i2-hut-tek phi-kian e5 thau5-cheng5.  26). Li2 tioh8 choe3 nng7 e5 kim-khoan5, he7 ti7 pou2-koa3 siang-thau5 e5 kiN5, kun7 i2-hut-tek ng3-lai7 hit-peng5.  27). Koh tioh8 choe3 nng7 e5 kim-khoan5, an ti7 i2-hut-tek phi-kian e7-bin7 e5 thau5-cheng5, oa2-kun7 saN-lian5 e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 i2-hut-tek ki5-khiau2 e5 kang sou2 chit e5 toa3 e5 teng2-bin7.  28). In tioh8 eng7 lam5-sek e5 iu3-toa3, chiong pou2-koa3 e5 khoan5 kap i2-hut-tek e5 khoan5 pak8 saN-lian5, hou7 i liam5 ti7 i2-hut-tek ki5-khiau2 e5 kang sou2 chit e5 toa3, hou7 pou2-koa3 kap i2-hut-tek bo5 li7-phang7.  29). A-lun5 jip8 seng3-sou2 e5 si5, tioh8 chiong phoaN3-toan3 e5 pou2-koa3 sou2 khek I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5, toa3 ti7 i e5 heng-cheng5, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, siong5-siong5 choe3 ki3-liam7.  30). Li2 tioh8 chiong OU-leng5 kap Thou2-beng5, he7 ti7 phoaN3-toan3 e5 pou2-koa3-lai7; A-lun5 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 e5 si5, hiah-e5 tioh8 ti7 i e5 heng-cheng5.  A-lun5 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 siong5-siong5 chiong I2-sek-liat8 e5 phoaN3-toan3 koa3 ti7 heng-cheng5.
	31). Li2 tioh8 choe3 i2-hut-tek lai7-bin7 e5 goa7-phau3, kui-nia2 si7 lam5-sek--e5.  32). Phau3 teng2-bin7 e5 tui3-tiong, tioh8 ui7-tioh8 thau5-khak lau5 chit8 e5 nia2-khang; khang e5 chiu-ui5 chit nia2-ian7, chhin-chhiuN7 chian3-kah e5 nia2-khang, bian2-tit phoa3 lih8.  33). Phau3 chiu-ui5 e5 e7-kha-pou5, tioh8 eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, choe3 siah8-liu5; ti7 phau3 chiu7-ui5, siah8-liu5 e5 tiong-kan, tioh8 u7 kim ham5-leng5.  34). Chit8-liap8 kim ham5-leng5, chit8-liap8 siah8-liu5, ti7 phau3 chiu-ui5 e5 e7-kha-pou5.  35). A-lun5 hok8-sai7 e5 si5, tioh8 chheng7--i; i jip8 seng3-sou2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5, i2-kip8 chhut-lai5 e5 si5, u7 siaN thang thiaN-kiN3, hou7 i bian2 si2.
	36). Tioh8 eng7 ho2-kim choe3 chit8 e5 pai5, chiau3 khek-in3 e5 hoat-tou7, khek ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7 kong2, CHOE3-SENG3 KUI IA5-HO5-HOA.  37). Tioh8 eng7 chit8-tiau5 lam5-sek e5 iu3-toa3, chiong i pak8 ti7 bo7-teng2, chiu7-si7 ti7 bo7 e5 thau5-cheng5.  38). Chit e5 pai5 tioh8 ti7 A-lun5 e5 thau5-hiah8, hou7 A-lun5 tam-tng seng3-mih8 e5 choe7, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, ti7 it-chhe3 seng3 e5 le2-mih8, sou2 hun-piat choe3-seng3--e5; chit e5 pai5 tioh8 siong5-siong5 ti7 i e5 thau5-hiah8, hou7 in ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 chiap-lap8.  39). Tioh8 eng7 iu3-toe7 chit u7-choa7 e5 lai7-saN; tioh8 eng7 iu3-toe7-pou3 choe3-bo7; koh eng7 siu3-hoe e5 kang, choe3 io-toa3.
	40). Li2 tioh8 ka7 A-lun5 chiah e5 kiaN2 choe3 lai7-saN, choe3 io-toa3, choe3 pau thau5-khak e5 kun, hou7 in eng5-kng koh sui2.  41). Tioh8 chiong chiah-e5 ka7 li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 chheng7, koh eng7 iu5 boah--in, kiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2, hun-piat in choe3-seng3, hou7 in choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7 Goa2.  42). Tioh8 ka7 in choe3 iu3-toe7-pou3 e5 khou3, jia in e5 e7-the2; khou3 tioh8 tui3 io kau3 toa7-thui2;  43). A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 jip8 hoe7-bou7, a2-si7 chiu7-kun7 toaN5, beh ti7 seng3-sou2 hok8-sai7 e5 si5, tioh8 chheng7--i; bian2-tit in tam-tng choe7 lai5 si2; che si7 beh ka7 A-lun5 kap i e5 hou7-e3 choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 le7.

[29]	Li2 hun-piat in choe3-seng3, choe3 che3-si hok8-sai7 Goa2, tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5; chhu2 chit8-chiah kang e5 gu5-a2, nng7-chiah bo5 ha5-chhu5 kang e5 mi5-iuN5,  2). koh bo5-kaN3-piaN2, kap kiau2-iu5 e5 bo5-kaN3-piaN2, kap boah-iu5 bo5-kaN3 e5 poh8-piaN2, long2 tioh8 eng7 ho2 e5 mi7-hun2 choe3--e5.  3). Chiah e5 piaN2 tioh8 he7 ti7 chit8 kha kheng, toe2 ti7 kheng--nih toa3--lai5, koh khan hit chiah kang e5 gu5 kap nng7 chiah kang e5 mi5-iuN5 lai5.  4). Tioh8 hou7 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2 kau3 hoe7-bou7 e5 mng5-khau2 eng7 chui2 soe2 in.  5). Tioh8 theh8 hiah e5 i-hok8 lai5, chiong lai7-saN kap i2-hut-tek lai7-bin7 e5 goa7-phau3, kap i2-hut-tek, lian5 pou2-koa3, ka7 A-lun5 chheng7; ia7 eng7 ki5-kha2 e5 kang sou2 chit i2-hut-tek e5 toa3 ka7 i ha5;  6). eng7 bo7 ti3 ti7 i e5 thau5-khak, chiong seng3 e5 bian2-liu5 thah8 ti7 bo7 e5 teng2-bin7.  7). Tioh8 eng7 boah e5 iu5 to3 ti7 i e5 thau5-khak lai5 boah i.  8). Tioh8 hou7 i e5 kiaN2 lai5, ka7 in chheng7 lai7-saN.  9). Koh eng7 toa3 ha5 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2, ka7 in pau thau5-khak e5 kun; in chiau3 eng2-oan2 e5 le7 tit-tioh8 che3-si e5 chit; koh tioh8 ka7 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2 kiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2.
	10). Li2 tioh8 khan hit chiah kang e5 gu5 kau3 hoe7-bou7-cheng5; A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2 tioh8 hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 gu5 e5 thau5-khak-teng2.  11). Li2 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 hoe7-bou7 e5 mng5-khau2, thai5 hit chiah gu5;  12). chhu2 i e5 huih tam7-poh8, eng7 chng2-thau5-a2 boah ti7 toaN5 e5 si3-kak; chiong huih long2 piaN3 ti7 toaN5-kha--nih.  13). Tioh8 chiong it-chhe3 ngou2-chong7 e5 iu5, kap koaN-teng2 e5 bang7-se, kap nng7 liap8 io-chi2, i2-kip8 io-chi2 e5 iu5, long2 sio ti7 toaN5-teng2.  14). Tok8-tok8 gu5 e5 bah, kap i e5 phe5, i e5 pun3, long2 tioh8 eng7 he2 sio ti7 iaN5-goa7; si7 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3.
	15). Li2 tioh8 khan chit8 chiah kang e5 mi5-iuN5 lai5; A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2 tioh8 hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 hit chiah iuN5 e5 thau5-khak-teng2.  16). Tioh8 thai5 hit chiah iuN5, chiong i e5 huih hiu3 ti7 toaN5 e5 si3-ui5.  17). Tioh8 chiong iuN5 chhiat chit8-te3 chit8-te3, soe2 ngou2-chong7 kap thui2, lok ti7 chhiat kui te3 e5 bah kap thau5 e5 teng2-bin7.  18). Tioh8 chiong kui chiah iuN5 sio ti7 toaN5-teng2, si7 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sio-che3; si7 phang-phang--e5, eng7 he2 sio hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 che3.  19). Li2 tioh8 chiong te7-ji7 chiah kang e5 mi5-iuN5 khan--lai5; A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2 tioh8 hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 iuN5 e5 thau5-khak-teng2.  20). Li2 tioh8 thai5 hit chiah iuN5, chhu2 i e5 huih tam7-poh8, boah ti7 A-lun5 chiaN3-peng5 e5 hi7-a2-sui5, kap i chiah e5 kiaN2, chiaN3-peng5 e5 hi7-a2-sui5, koh boah ti7 in chiaN3-chhiu2 e5 toa7-pou7-bu2, kap chiaN3-kha e5 toa7-pou7-bu2; koh chiong huih hiu3 ti7 toaN5 e5 si3-ui5.  21). Li2 tioh8 chhu2 toaN5-teng2 e5 huih tam7-poh8 kap boah e5 iu5, hiu3 ti7 A-lun5 kap i e5 saN, koh hiu3 ti7 i e5 kiaN2 kap i e5 kiaN2 e5 saN; i kap i e5 saN, i e5 kiaN2 kap i e5 kiaN2 e5 saN, long2 hun-piat choe3 seng3.  22). Koh tioh8 chhu2 hit chiah iuN5 e5 iu5, kap i e5 pui5 e5 be2, kap kham3 ngou2-chong7 e5 iu5, kap koaN-teng2 e5 bang7-se, nng7 liap8 io-chi2, i2-kip8 io-chi2 e5 iu5, kap chiaN3-peng5 e5 thui2 (che si7 chiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2 e5 iuN5);  23). koh tui3 hit-khia he7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 toe2 bo5-kaN3-piaN2 e5 kheng-a2-lai7, theh8 chit8 te3 piaN2, chit8 te3 kiau2-iu5 e5 piaN2, chit8-te3 poh8-piaN2;  24). long2 he7 ti7 A-lun5 e5 chhiu2 kap i e5 kiaN2 e5 chhiu2, io5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, choe3 io5-che3.  25). Li2 tioh8 tui3 in e5 chhiu2 chih--lai5, sio ti7 toaN5-teng2 sio-che3 e5 teng2-bin7, choe3 phang-phang ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; si7 eng7 he2 sio hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 che3.  26). A-lun5 siu7 siat-lip8 e5 le2 sou2 hian3 kang e5 iuN5, li2 tioh8 chhu2 i e5 heng, io5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, choe3 io5-che3; che si7 li2 e5 hun7-giah8.  27). KiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2 sou2 hian3 kang e5 iuN5, hit e5 io5-che3 e5 heng kap ku2-che3 e5 thui2, chiu7-si7 sou2 io5--e5, sou2 ku2-khi2--e5, li2 tioh8 hun-piat i choe3-seng3, chiu7-si7 siok8 ti7 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2--e5.  28). Che tioh8 choe3 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2-sun tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 tit-tioh8 eng2-oan2 e5 hun7-giah8; in-ui7 si7 ku2-che3; tioh8 tui3 I2-se-liat8 lang5 peng5-an-che3 e5 tiong-kan choe3 ku2-che3; chiu7-si7 in hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ku2-che3.  29). A-lun5 e5 seng3-saN tioh8 lau5 hou7 i au7-tai7 e5 kiaN2-sun, thang chheng7 i lai5 siu7 boah-iu5, ia7 chheng7 i lai5 siu7 siat-lip8.  30). I e5 kiaN2, hit e5 soa3-chiap i tng che3-si e5, tak8-pai2 jip8 hoe7-bou7, ti7 seng3-sou2 hok8-sai7 e5 si5, tioh8 chheng7 chhit-jit8 ku2.  31). KiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2 sou2 hian3 kang e5 iuN5 e5 bah, li2 tioh8 ti7 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7 chu2 i.  32). A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 tioh8 ti7 hoe7-bou7 e5 mng5-khau2 chiah8 chit chiah iuN5 e5 bah kap kheng-a2-lai7 e5 piaN2.  33). In tioh8 chiah8 sou2 eng7 lai5 siok8-choe7 e5 mih8, hou7 in tam-tng chit, ia7 hun-piat in choe3-seng3; tok8-tok8 goa7-lang5 m7-thang chiah8, in-ui7 che si7 seng3-mih8.  34). Hit e5 kiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2 sou2 hian3 e5 bah a2-si7 piaN2, na7 u7 lau5 kau3 keh cha2-khi2--e5, li2 tioh8 chiong sou2 lau5--e5 eng7 he2 sio i; m7-thang chiah8 i, in-ui7 si7 seng3 e5 mih8.  35). Li2 tioh8 chiau3 Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 hoan-hu3-e5 kiaN5 ti7 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2; kiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2 tioh8 chhit-jit8 ku2.  36). Tak8-jit8 tioh8 hian3 kang e5 gu5 chit8-chiah choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; li2 ui7 toaN5 siok8-choe7 e5 si5 chiu7 hou7 i chheng-khi3; ia7 tioh8 ka7 i boah-iu5, hun-piat i choe3-seng3.  37). Li2 tioh8 ui7 toaN5 siok8-choe7 chhit-jit8 ku2, hou7 i chiaN5-seng3; toaN5 chiu7 chiaN5 choe3 chi3-seng3; kiN3-na7 bong--tioh8 i--e5 long2 hun-piat choe3-seng3.
	38). Li2 sou2 tioh8 hian3 ti7 toaN5--nih-e5 si7 chiah-e5; chiu7-si7 be7 moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 nng7-chiah, tak8-jit8 tioh8 hian3;  39). cha2-khi2-si5 tioh8 hian3 chit8-chiah; hong5-hun e5 si5 tioh8 hian3 hit-chiah.  40). Li2 tioh8 eng7 iu3 e5 mi7-hun2 chit8 i-hoat chap8-hun7 e5 chit8, eng7 khoeh-ho2 e5 iu5 chit8-him si3-hun7 e5 chit8 tiau-ho5--e5, kap chit8 chiah iuN5-a2 saN-tang5 hian3; koh eng7 chiu2 chit8-him si3-hun7 e5 chit8 choe3 koan3-tian7.  41). Iau2 hit chiah e5 iuN5-a2 tioh8 ti7 hong5-hun e5 si5 lai5 hian3, tioh8 chiau3 cha2-khi2-si5 e5 sou3-che3 kap koan3-tian7 e5 le2 liau7-li2 i, choe3 phang-phang, eng7 he2 sio lai5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 che3.  42). Che beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 hoe7-bou7 e5 mng5-khau2, choe3 lin2 tak8 se3-tai7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3; Goa2 beh ti7-hia kap lin2 siong-hoe7, kap li2 kong2-oe7.  43). Goa2 beh ti7-hia kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 siong-hoe7, hoe7-bou7 chiu7 beh in-ui7 Goa2 e5 eng5-kng chiaN5-choe3 seng3.  44). Goa2 beh hou7 hoe7-bou7 kap toaN5 choe3-seng3; ia7 beh hou7 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2 choe3-seng3, choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7 Goa2.  45). Goa2 beh tiam3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3.  46). In beh chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3, si7 chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 toe7; thang hou7 Goa2 tiam3 ti7 in tiong-kan; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3.

[30]	Li2 tioh8 choe3 chit8 cho7 toaN5, thang sio hiuN; eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 i;  2). tng5 chit8 tiu2, khoah chit8 tiu2, khoan2-sit su3-hong-e5; koaiN5 nng7 tiu2; i hiah e5 kak tioh8 kap toaN5 lian5 choe3 chit8-te3.  3). ToaN5 kap i e5 teng2-bin7, kap i e5 si3-ui5, kap i hiah e5 kak, long2 eng7 ho2-kim pau--i; ia7 tioh8 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 khi2 kim-soaN3.  4). Li2 tioh8 choe3 nng7 e5 kim-khoan5 an ti7 khi2-soaN3 e5 e7-bin7, tioh8 choe3 ti7 toaN5 e5 siang-peng5, nng7 ki hoaiN5-koaiN e5 teng2-bin7, chiah e5 khoan5 tioh8 choe3 chhng-kng3 e5 lou7-eng7, thang kng toaN5.  5). Tioh8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 kng3, eng7 kim pau in.  6). Li2 tioh8 eng7 toaN5 he7 ti7 oa2-kun7 hoat-kui7 e5 tiuN3-li5-cheng5, ti7 hoat-kui7 teng2 si-un-sou2 e5 thau5-cheng5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 beh kap li2 siong-hoe7 e5 sou2-chai7.  7). A-lun5 ti7 toaN5-teng2 tioh8 sio phang-liau7 sou2 choe3 e5 hiuN; tak8 cha2-khi2 i cheng2-tun3 teng e5 si5 tioh8 sio i.  8). Kau3 hong5-hun A-lun5 tiam2-teng e5 si5, ia7 tioh8 sio i; si7 choe3 lin2 tak8 se3-tai7 siong5-siong5 sio e5 hiuN ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  9). Ti7 chit e5 toaN5-teng2 m7-thang hian3 pat8-ho7 e5 hiuN; ia7 m7-thang hian3 sio-che3 kap sou3-che3; ia7 m7-thang koan3-tian7 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7.  10). A-lun5 tioh8 chit8-ni5 chit8-pai2 ti7 toaN5-teng2 e5 kak siok8-choe7; i chit8-ni5 chit8-pai2 tioh8 eng7 siok8-choe7-che3 e5 huih ti7 toaN5-teng2 siok8-choe7; tak8 se3-tai7 tioh8 an2-ni; chit e5 toaN5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 choe3 chi3-seng3.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  12). Li2 sng3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 lang5-giah8, chiau3 in tiong-kan sou2 chiuN7-sng3--e5, li2 sng3 in e5 si5, in tak8-lang5 tioh8 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7 eng7 siok8-hoe5 e5 ke3-chiN5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; bian2-tit li2 sng3 in e5 si5, ti7 in tiong-kan u7 chai-e7.  13). KiN3-na7 ke3--khi3, kui ti7 hiah e5 chiuN7-sng3--e5, tak8-lang5 tioh8 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 pheng5 theh8-chhut poaN3 sia3-khek-lek8 e5 gun5; chi2 poaN3 sia3-khek-lek8 si7 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5; chit8 sia3-khek-lek8 si7 ji7-chap8 e5 kui3-lah8.  14). KiN3-na7 ke3--khi3 kui ti7 hiah e5 chiuN7-sng3--e5, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7 e5, tioh8 chiong chit-e5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  15). Ui7-tioh8 siok8-hoe5 lin2 e5 siN3-mia7 chiong chit-e5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 si5, ho2-giah8 lang5 m7-thang chhut khah-choe7, song3-hiong lang5 ia7 m7-thang chhut khah-chio2; tak8-lang5 chun2-chun2 chhut poaN3 sia3-khek-lek8.  16). Li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 siu chit e5 siok8-hoe5 e5 gun5, choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 lou7-eng7; thang ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3 ki3-liam7, lai5 siok8-hoe5 lin2 e5 siN3-mia7.
	17). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  18). Li2 tioh8 eng7 tang5 choe3 soe2-tng7 e5 phun5, i e5 cho7 ia7 tioh8 eng7 tang5 choe3, thang eng7 i soe2-tng7; tioh8 he7 i ti7 hoe7-bou7 kap toaN5 e5 tiong-kan; lai7-bin7 tioh8 toe2 chui2.  19). A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 beh ti7-hia soe2 in e5 chhiu2, in e5 kha.  20). In jip8 hoe7-bou7, a2-si7 chiu7-kun7 toaN5-cheng5 hok8-sai7, eng7 he2 sio-che3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 si5, tioh8 eng7 chui2 soe2, bian2-tit si2-bo5.  21). In tioh8 an2-ni soe2-chhiu2 soe2-kha, bian2-tit si2-bo5; che si7 choe3 in tiaN7-tioh8 e5 le7, chiu7-si7 choe3 i kap i e5 hou7-e3 tak8 se3-tai7 eng2-oan2 e5 le7.
	22). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  23). Li2 tioh8 chhu2 siong7-phin2 e5 hiuN-liau7, chiu7-si7 choan e5 but8-ioh8, gou7-pah sia3-khek-lek8, phang e5 jiok8-kui3 chit8-poaN3, chiu7-si7 nng7-pah gou7-chap8, phang e5 chhiong-pou5 nng7-pah gou7-chap8,  24). tim5-hiuN gou7-pah, long2 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 pheng5, kap kaN-na2-iu5 chit8-him.  25). Li2 tioh8 eng7 i choe3 thang boah e5 seng3-iu5, chiu7-si7 chiau3 choe3 phang-bi7 e5 hoat tiau-ho5 i; si7 beh choe3 thang boah e5 seng3-iu5.  26). Tioh8 eng7 chit e5 iu5 boah hoe7-bou7 kap hoat-kui7,  27). toh kap toh-teng2 it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, teng-tai5 kap teng-tai5 e5 khi3-ku7, i2-kip8 hiuN-toaN5,  28). sio-che3 e5 toaN5 kap i it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, soe2-tng7 e5 phun5 kap i e5 cho7.  29). Li2 tioh8 hou7 in choe3-seng3, hou7 in chiaN5-choe3 chi3-seng3; kiN3-na7 bong--tioh8 i-e5 long2 hun-piat choe3-seng3.  30). Li2 tioh8 eng7 iu5 boah A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2, hou7 in choe3-seng3, thang choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7 Goa2.  31). Li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Chit e5 iu5 beh choe3 Goa2 e5 seng3-iu5, choe3 boah e5 lou7-eng7, kau3 lin2 tak8 se3-tai7.  32). M7-thang to3 ti7 lang5 e5 seng-khu, ia7 m7-thang chiau3 chit-e5 tiau-ho5 e5 hoat choe3 kap chit8-e5 saN chhin-chhiuN7 e5; chit e5 iu5 si7 seng3, lin2 ia7 tioh8 liah8 i choe3-seng3.  33). KiN3-na7 tiau-ho5 kap chit-e5 saN chhin-chhiuN7, a2-si7 eng7 i boah ti7 goa7-lang5 e5 seng-khu e5, beh tui3 i e5 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan siu7 chian2-tu5.
	34). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 chhu2 phang e5 hiuN-liau7, chiu7-si7 na2-tat8, ti2-he5-lek8, hek-pi7-na2; chiah e5 phang-phang e5 hiuN-liau7, kap chheng e5 ju2-hiuN, tak8-iuN7 chhin3 piN5-tang7;  35). li2 tioh8 eng7 chiah-e5 choe3 hiuN, chiau3 choe3 phang-bi7 e5 hoat lai5 choe3 phang-liau7, eng7 iam5 tiau-ho5, hou7 i chheng-khi3 koh seng3;  36). chit e5 hiuN li2 tioh8 theh8 tam7-poh8, cheng hou7 i chin iu3, he7 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 hoat-kui7 cheng5; Goa2 beh ti7-hia kap li2 siong-hoe7; lin2 tioh8 liah8 i choe3 chi3-seng3.  37). Lin2 sou2 choe3 e5 hiuN m7-thang chiau3 chit e5 tiau-ho5 e5 hoat, ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 lai5 choe3; lin2 tioh8 liah8 i choe3-seng3, kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  38). KiN3-na7 choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 chit-khoan2 e5 hiuN, ai3 beh phiN7-phang e5, beh tui3 i e5 peh-siN3-tiong siu7 chian2-tu5.

[31]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). KhoaN3 ah, Iu5-tai7 chi-phai3, Hou7-jiN2 e5 sun, OU-li7 e5 kiaN2, Pi2-sat-liat8, Goa2 i2-keng chi2-mia5 lai5 tiau3 i;  3). Goa2 eng7 Siong7-te3 e5 sin5 chhiong-moa2 i, hou7 i u7 ti3-hui7, u7 chhang-mia5, u7 chai-bat, oe7 choe3 tak8-iuN7 e5 kang;  4). oe7 siuN7-chhut ki5-khiau2 e5 kang, lai5 choe3 kim, gun5, tang5, hiah e5 mih8;  5). ia7 oe7 khek po2-chioh8 lai5 jip8 i; ia7 oe7 khek chha5, oe7 choe3 tak8-iuN7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang.  6). Goa2 ia7 phai3 Tan3 e5 chi-phai3, A-hi-sat-boat e5 kiaN2, A-ho5-li7-a-pek, kap i saN-kap choe3; kiN3-na7 sim-lai7 u7 ti3-hui7 e5, Goa2 koh siuN2-su3 ti3-hui7 ti7 in e5 sim, hou7 in oe7 choe3 Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2 e5;  7). chiu7-si7 hoe7-bou7, hoat-kui7, kap hi2 teng2-bin7 e5 si-un-sou2, i2-kip8 pou3-piN5 it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7,  8). toh kap toh-teng2 e5 khi3-ku7, ho2-kim e5 teng-tai5 kap i it-chhe3 e5 khi2-ku7,  9). i2-kip8 hiuN-toaN5, sio-che3 e5 toaN5 kap i it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, i2-kip8 soe2-tng7 e5 phun5 kap i e5 cho7;  10). cheng-kong e5 i-hok8, che3-si A-lun5 e5 seng3-saN kap i e5 kiaN2 e5 saN, hou7 in choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7;  11). thang boah e5 iu5, i2-kip8 seng3-sou2 sou2 eng7 phang-liau7 e5 hiuN; chiau3 Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, in tioh8 choe3.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  13). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Lin2 tek-khak tioh8 siu2 Goa2 hiah e5 an-hioh-jit8; in-ui7 che si7 Goa2 kap lin2 e5 tiong-kan e5 cheng3-ku3, kau3 ti7 lin2 tak8 se3-tai7, hou7 lin2 chai Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, hou7 lin2 chiaN5-seng3 e5.  14). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 siu2 an-hioh-jit8, in-ui7 si7 lin2 e5 seng3-jit8, kiN3-na7 hoan7-tioh8 chit-jit8--e5, tioh8 hou7 i si2; hoan7-na7 ti7 chit-jit8 choe3 kang--e5, tioh8 tui3 i e5 peh-siN3-tiong siu7 chian2-tu5.  15). Lak8-jit8 tioh8 choe3-kang, tok8-tok8 te7-chhit jit8 si7 an-hioh e5 toa7-jit8, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 seng3-jit8; hoan7-na7 ti7 an-hioh-jit8 choe3-kang--e5, tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.  16). Sou2-i2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tioh8 siu2 an-hioh-jit8, tai7-tai7 kin2-sin7 chit e5 an-hioh-jit8, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.  17). Che si7 Goa2 kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong-kan eng2-oan2 e5 cheng3-ku3; in-ui7 lak8-jit8-lai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhong3-cho7 thiN toe7, te7-chhit jit8 chiu7 hioh-khun3 lai5 chheng-eng5.
	18). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Se-nai2 soaN kap Mou5-se kong2-oe7 beng5-pek8, chiu7 chiong nng7 te3 iok-pi hou7--i, si7 Siong7-te3 eng7 chng2-thau5-a2 sia2 e5 chioh8-pi.

[32]	Peh-siN3 khoaN3-kiN3 Mou5-se ian5-chhian5 bo5 loh8 soaN, peh-siN3 chiu7 chu7-chip8 kau3 A-lun5 hia, tui3 i kong2, Khi2--lai5, ka7 goan2 chng siong7-te3, thang kiaN5 ti7 goan2 e5 thau5-cheng5; in-ui7 hit e5 Mou5-se, chiu7-si7 chhoa7 goan2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhut-lai5, hit e5 lang5, goan2 m7-chai i tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8.  2). A-lun5 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 e5 bou2, lin2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, hi7-a2 sou2 koa3 e5 kim khoan5, pak i, theh8--lai5 hou7 goa2.  3). Peh-siN3 chiu7 long2 pak in hi7-a2--nih e5 kim-khoan5, theh8 lai5 hou7 A-lun5.  4). A-lun5 tui3 in e5 chhiu2 chih--lai5, chu3 chit8 chiah gu5-a2, eng7 chhiam3-to-a2 tiau-khek--i; in chiu7 kong2, I2-sek-liat8 ah, che si7 li2 e5 siong7-te3, chhoa7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5.  5). A-lun5 khoaN3-liau2, chiu7 ti7 gu5-a2 e5 bin7-cheng5 khi2-toaN5; A-lun5 koh soan-pou3 kong2, Bin5-a2-jit8 tioh8 siu2-choeh hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  6). Keh jit8 chheng-cha2, in khi2--lai5, hian3 sio-che3 kap peng5-an-che3; peh-siN3 chiu7 che7-teh lim-chiah8, khi2-lai5 kun2-chhio3.
	7). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Khi3 ah, li2 loh8-khi3; in-ui7 li2 e5 peh-siN3, chiu7-si7 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhoa7 chhut--lai5 e5, i2-keng pai7-hoai7 ka-ki7.  8). In kin2-kin2 li7-khui Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 in e5 lou7, ui7 ka-ki7 chu3-chiaN5 chit8 chiah gu5-a2, kui7-pai3--i, hian3-che3--i, kong2, I2-sek-liat8 ah, che chiu7-si7 chhoa7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 siong7-te3.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 chit e5 peh-siN3, khoaN3 ah, si7 am7-kun2 ngi7 e5 peh-siN3.  10). Li2 taN chhut-chai7 Goa2, Goa2 beh toa7 siu7-khi3 in, biat8-bo5 in; eng7 li2 chiaN5-choe3 toa7-kok.  11). Mou5-se chiu7 tui3 i e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu5-cheng5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 siaN2-su7 toa7 siu7-khi3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, si7 Li2 eng7 toa7 khui3-lat8 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhoa7 chhut--lai5-e5?  12). SiaN2-su7 hou7 Ai-kip8 lang5 u7 oe7 kong2, I chhoa7 in chhut-khi3, si7 beh hai7--in, hai7-si2 in ti7 soaN-tiong, tui3 toe7-chiuN7 tu5-biat8 in? kiu5 Li2 he5-sim tng2-i3, soah Li2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, bo5 kang3 chai-e7 hou7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3.  13). Ki3-liam7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, I2-sek-liat8, Li2 bat ki2 ka-ki7 tui3 in chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 lin2 e5 hou7-e3 chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-teng2 e5 chhiN hiah-choe7; koh Goa2 sou2 kong2 chit e5 choan5-toe7, Goa2 beh siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 hou7-e3, beh choe3 in eng2-oan2 e5 giap8.  14). Tui3 an2-ni Ia5-ho5-hoa the3-hoe2, bo5 kang3-loh8 I cheng5 sou2 kong2 e5 chai-e7, hou7 I e5 peh-siN3.
	15). Mou5-se oat8-tng2-sin loh8 soaN, chhiu2 theh8 nng7 te3 iok-pi, chiah e5 pi nng7-bin7 long2 u7 sia2; chit-bin7 hit-bin7 long2 u7 sia2-ji7.  16). Pi si7 Siong7-te3 choe3--e5, ji7 si7 Siong7-te3 sia2--e5, khek ti7 pi--nih.  17). Iok-su-a chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 peh-siN3 han2-hoa7 e5 siaN, chiu7 tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Ti7 iaN5-tiong u7 kau-chian3 e5 siaN.  18). I kong2, Goa2 sou2 thiaN-kiN3 m7-si7 thai5-iaN5 tek-seng3 e5 siaN, ia7 m7-si7 thai5-su au5-kio3 e5 siaN, chiu7-si7 chhiuN3-koa e5 siaN.  19). KiaN5 kun7 iaN5-poaN5, khoaN3-kiN3 gu5-a2, koh khoaN3-kiN3 lang5 teh thiau3-bu2, Mou5-se chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, tui3 i e5 chhiu2 hiat nng7 te3 chioh8-pi, chih8 ti7 soaN-kha.  20). Koh chiong in sou2 chu3 e5 gu5-a2, eng7 he2 sio, geng2 choe3 hun2, ia7 ti7 chui2-bin7, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 lim--i.  21). Mou5-se tui3 A-lun5 kong2, Chit e5 peh-siN3 tui3 li2 choe3 sim2-mih8, li2 chiah hou7 in ham7-loh8 tang7-choe7?  22). A-lun5 kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 boh8-tit toa7 siu7-khi3; chiah e5 peh-siN3 koat-i3 choe3 phaiN2, si7 li2 sou2 chai--e5.  23). In tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 ka7 goan2 chng siong7-te3, thang kiaN5 ti7 goan2 e5 thau5-cheng5, in-ui7 hit e5 Mou5-se, chiu7-si7 chhoa7 goan2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhut-lai5, hit e5 lang5, goan2 m7 chai i tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8.  24). Goa2 tui3 in kong2, KiN3-na7 u7 kim--e5, pak--khi2-lai5; in chiong kim hou7 goa2, goa2 hiat i ti7 he2--nih, chit chiah gu5-a2 chiu7 chhut-lai5.  25). Mou5-se khoaN3-kiN3 peh-siN3 hong3-chhiong3, in-ui7 A-lun5 pang3 chhut-chai7 in, hou7 in ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 tiong-kan siu7 ki-chhi3,  26). Mou5-se khia7 ti7 iaN5-poaN5 e5 mng5, kong2, Chi7-chui7 oa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, thang lai5 goa2 chia; Li7-bi7 lang5 chiu7 long2 chu7-chip8 ti7 i hia.  27). I tui3 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kong2, Lin2 tak8-lang5 tioh8 chhah to ti7 toa7-thui2--nih, ong2-lai5 ti7 iaN5-tiong, tui3 chit e5 mng5 kau3 hit e5 mng5, tak8-lang5 thai5-si2 i e5 hiaN-ti7, kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7, i2-kip8 i e5 chhu3-piN.  28). Li7-bi7 lang5 chiau3 Mou5-se e5 oe7 kiaN5; hit-jit8 peh-siN3-tiong si2--e5 iok-liok8 saN-chheng lang5.  29). Mou5-se kong2, Lin2 hian3 ka-ki7 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tak8-lang5 kong-kek i e5 kiaN2, i e5 hiaN-ti7 , kin-a2-jit8 tit-tioh8 I su3-hok lin2.
	30). Ke3-jit8 Mou5-se tui3 peh-siN3 kong2, Lin2 u7 hoan7 tang7-choe7, goa2 taN beh chiuN7--khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia, kiam2-chhai2 thang ka7 lin2 siok8-choe7.  31). Mou5-se to3-tng2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia kong2, Ai--ah, chit e5 peh-siN3 hoan7 tang7-choe7, ui7 ka-ki7 choe3 kim e5 siong7-te3.  32). TaN Li2 na7 beh sia3-bian2 in e5 choe7; na7 m7, kiu5 Li2 tui3 Li2 sou2 sia2 e5 chheh, chhat--khi3 goa2 e5 mia5.  33). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Sim2-mih8 lang5 tek-choe7 Goa2 chiu7 tui3 Goa2 e5 chheh chhat i e5 mia5.  34). TaN li2 khi3 chhoa7 chit e5 peh-siN3 khi3 Goa2 sou2 ka7 li2 kong2 e5 sou2-chai7; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 e5 su3-chia2 beh kiaN5 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5; tok8-tok8 kau3 Goa2 pan7-choe7 e5 jit8, Goa2 beh pan7 in e5 choe7.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa kang3 chai-e7 hou7 peh-siN3, in-ui7 in cho7 gu5-a2, chiu7-si7 A-lun5 sou2 cho7--e5.

[33]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 bat chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 A-peh-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, kong2, Beh chiong thou2-toe7 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 hou7-e3; taN li2 khi3 ah, li2 kap li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 sou2 chhoa7 chhut-lai5 e5 peh-siN3, tioh8 tui3 chia chiuN7-khi3 hit e5 toe7.  2). Goa2 beh chhe su3-chia2 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5; Goa2 beh koaN2-chhut Ka-lam5, A-mou5-li7, Hek, Pi2-li7-se2, Hi-bi7, Ia5-pou3-su hiah e5 chok8,  3). chhoa7 li2 kau3 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7; in-ui7 Goa2 m7 kap li2 chiuN7-khi3, ui7-tioh8 li2 si7 am7-kun2 ngi7 e5 peh-siN3; kiaN-liau2 Goa2 ti7 lou7--nih biat8-bo5 li2.  4). Peh-siN3 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 phaiN2 siau-sit chiu7 iu-bun7; bo5 lang5 chng-thaN7.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Lin2 si7 am7-kun2 ngi7 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 na7 chit8-bak8-nih-ku2 kau3 lin2 tiong-kan, Goa2 tek-khak chau5-biat8 lin2; taN tioh8 chiong lin2 seng-khu e5 chng-thaN7 pak--khi2-lai5, Goa2 chiu7 chai Goa2 beh chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 lin2.  6). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 ti7 Ho5-liat8 soaN i2-au7, chiu7 chiong seng-khu e5 chng-thaN7 thng3--khi2-lai5.  7). Mou5-se chiong pou3-piN5 tah ti7 iaN5-goa7, li7-khui iaN5 u7 hiah-hng7; i chheng chit e5 pou3-piN5 choe3 hoe7-bou7, hoan7-na7 chhe7-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5, chiu7 kau3 iaN5-goa7 e5 hoe7-bou7 hia.  8). Tng Mou5-se chhut-khi3 kau3 Pou3-piN5 e5 si5, cheng3 peh-siN3 chiu7 long2 khi2--lai5, tak8-lang5 khia7 ti7 in e5 pou3-piN5-khau2, teh khoaN3 Mou5-se, kau3 i jip8 Pou3-piN5.  9). Mou5-se jip8 Pou3-piN5 e5 si5, hun5-thiau7 chiu7 loh8-lai5, khia7 ti7 Pou3-piN5 e5 mng5-cheng5; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 kap Mou5-se kong2-oe7.  10). Cheng3 peh-siN3 khoaN3-kiN3 hun5-thiau7 khia7 ti7 Pou3-piN5 e5 mng5-cheng5, peh-siN3 chiu7 long2 khi2-lai5, tak8-lang5 ti7 in e5 pou3-piN5 mng5-khau2 kui7-pai3.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa kap Mou5-se bin7 tui3 bin7 kong2-oe7, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 kap peng5-iu2 kong2-oe7 chit8-poaN-iuN7.  Mou5-se to3-tng2-lai5 iaN5-lai7; tok8-tok8 kun-sui5 i e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a bo5 li7-khui Pou3-piN5.
	12). Mou5-se tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Li2 tui3 goa2 kong2, Chiong chit e5 peh-siN3 chhoa7 chiuN7-khi3, chong2-si7 bo5 hou7 goa2 chai Li2 beh chhe chi7-chui7 kap goa2 saN-kap khi3.  Chi2-u7 kong2, Goa2 eng7 mia5 keng2-tiau3 li2, li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ia7 tit-tioh8 un-tian2.  13). Goa2 taN na7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 lou7 chi2-si7 goa2, hou7 goa2 bat Li2, thang ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2; Li2 tioh8 siau3-liam7 chit-chok8 si7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh chhin-sin kap li2 khi3, hou7 li2 peng5-an.  15). Mou5-se tui3 I kong2, Li2 na7 bo5 chhin-sin kap goa2 khi3, chiu7 m7-thang chhoa7 goan2 tui3-chia chiuN7-khi3.  16). Tui3 chaiN2-iuN7 oe7 chai, goa2 kap Li2 e5 peh-siN3 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2? kiam2 m7-si7 tui3 Li2 kap goan2 saN-kap khi3, hou7 goa2 kap Li2 e5 peh-siN3 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 ban7 peh-siN3 u7 hun-piat mah?  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 sou2 kong2 chit e5 su7, Goa2 ia7 beh choe3--i; in-ui7 li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, koh Goa2 eng7 mia5 keng2-tiau3 li2.  18). I kong2, Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 e5 eng5-kng.  19). I kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 un-hui7 keng-ke3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, ia7 soan-pou3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Goa2 beh si-un ti7 Goa2 sou2 si-un--e5, Goa2 beh lin5-bin2 ti7 Goa2 sou2 lin5-bin2--e5.  20). Koh kong2, Li2 boe7-oe7 khoaN3 Goa2 e5 bin7, in-ui7 bo5 lang5 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 ia7 oe7 oah8.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3-ah, kun7 Goa2 chia u7 sou2-chai7, li2 tioh8 khia7 ti7 chioh8-poaN5-teng2;  22). tng Goa2 e5 eng5-kng keng-ke3 e5 si5, Goa2 beh ka7 li2 he7 ti7 chioh8-poaN5 phang7-lai7, eng7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 jia--li2; theng3-hau7 Goa2 ke3--khi3;  23). jian5-au7 Goa2 beh kiu Goa2 e5 chhiu2 to3-tng2, li2 chiu7 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 e5 ka-chiah-au7; chong2-si7 boe7-tit-thang khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 e5 bin7.

[34]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 phah nng7-te3 chioh8-pi, kap i2-cheng5--e5 saN-tang5, li2 cheng5 sou2 phah-phoa3 hiah e5 pi; hi2 teng2-bin7 e5 ji7, Goa2 beh sia2 ti7 chiah e5 pi.  2). Bin5-a2-cha2-khi2 li2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 pian7; thau3-cha2 li2 tioh8 chiuN7 Se-nai2 soaN; ti7-hia, ti7 soaN-be2-liu, khia7 ti7 Goa2 bin7-cheng5,  3). M7-thang u7 lang5 kap li2 chiuN7--lai5; pian3-soaN long2 m7-thang khoaN3-kiN3 u7 lang5, ti7 soaN-kha ia7 m7-thang hou7 gu5-kun5 iuN5-kun5 chiah8-chhau2.  4). I chiu7 phah nng7 te3 chioh8-pi, kap i2-cheng5--e5 saN-tang5; Mou5-se thau3-cha2 khi2--lai5, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 i e5, chiuN7-khi3 Se-nai2 soaN, chhiu2--nih theh8 nng7 te3 chioh8-pi.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa che7-hun5 lim5-kau3, kap i khia7 ti7-hia, soan-pou3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i e5 bin7-cheng5 keng-ke3, soan-pou3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa, Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 u7 lin5-bin2, u7 un-tian2 e5 Siong7-te3, bo5 khoai3 siu7-khi2, koh u7 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8;  7). ui7 chheng-ban7 lang5 chun5 chu5-ai3, sia3-bian2 choe7-koa3, ke3-sit kap choe7-ok; koat-toan3 bo5 liah8 u7-choe7--e5 choe3 bo5 choe7; beh kui-kiu7 i e5 choe7, tui3 pe7 kau3 kiaN2, kau3 sun, kau3 saN-si3-tai7.  8). Mou5-se kin2-kin2 aN3-loh8 toe7 keng3-pai3, kong2,  9). Chu2 ah, goa2 na7 tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, kiu5 Chu2 ti7 goan2 tiong-kan saN-kap kiaN5; in-ui7 che si7 am7-kun2 ngi7 e5 peh-siN3; koh kiu5 Li2 sia3-bian2 goan2 e5 choe7-koa3, kap goan2 e5 choe7-ok, liah8 goan2 choe3 Li2 e5 san2-giap8.
	10). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh lip8-iok, beh ti7 li2 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiaN5 ki5-biau7 e5 su7, si7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok-tiong sou2 be7-bat kiaN5--e5; ti7 li2 si3-ui5 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, chiu7 beh khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2-choe3; in-ui7 Goa2 tui3 li2 sou2 kiaN5--e5, si7 thang kiaN e5 su7.  11). Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2--e5, li2 tioh8 chip-siu2; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut A-mou5-li7, Ka-lam5, Hek, Pi2-li7-se2, Hi-bi7, Ia5-pou3-su hiah e5 chok8.  12). Li2 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, m7-thang kap li2 sou2 khi3 hit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 lip8-iok, kiaN-liau2 chiaN5-choe3 lin2 tiong-kan e5 lo5-bang7.  13). Chiu7-si7 tioh8 thiah in e5 che3-toaN5, phah-chhui3 in tiau-khek e5 thiau7, chho3 in e5 A-sia3-lah8.  14). M7-thang keng3-pai3 pat8 e5 Siong7-te3; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 chheng-choe3 Tok8-chun, i si7 tok8-chun e5 Siong7-te3;  15). kiaN-liau2 li2 kap hit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 lip8-iok, in te3 in e5 siong7-te3 kiaN5 sia5-im5, che3-su7 in e5 siong7-te3, u7 lang5 kio3 li2, li2 chiu7 chiah8 i e5 che3-mih8;  16). koh kiaN-liau2 li2 ka7 li2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7 in e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3-bou2, in e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 te3 in e5 siong7-te3 kiaN5 sia5-im5, hou7 li2 e5 kiaN2 ia7 te3 in e5 siong7-te3 kiaN5 sia5-im5.  17). Li2 m7-thang ui7 ka-ki7 chu3-cho7 chiah e5 siong7-te3.
	18). Li2 tioh8 siu2 tu5-kaN3-choeh.  Chiau3 Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2--e5, ti7 A-pit geh8-lai7 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8-ki5, chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2 chhit-jit8, in-ui7 li2 ti7 A-pit geh8-lai7 chhut Ai-kip8.  19). KiN3-na7 thau5-thai--e5, long2 si7 Goa2-e5, it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN thau5-chui2--e5, bo5-lun7 si7 gu5, si7 iuN5, kang-e5 long2 si7 Goa2-e5.  20). Thau5-chui2 e5 lu5 tioh8 eng7 iuN5-a2 thoe3-siok8; na7 bo5 thoe3-siok8, chiu7 tioh8 kong3-chih8 i e5 am7-kun2.  KiN3-na7 li2 thau5-chiuN7 e5 kiaN2, long2 tioh8 siok8-hoe5.  Lang5 lai5 kiN3 Goa2 m7-thang khang-chhiu2.
	21). Li2 lak8-jit8 tioh8 choe3 kang, te7-chhit jit8 tioh8 an-hioh; ti7 chai-cheng3 siu-koah e5 si5 ia7 tioh8 an-hioh.  22). Beh8 khi2-thau5 sek8, siu-koah e5 si5, tioh8 siu2 chhit-chhit-jit8 choeh.  Koh ti7 ni5-be2, tioh8 siu2 siu-khng3 e5 choeh.  23). Lin2 it-chhe3 e5 ta-pou-teng, tioh8 chit8-ni5 saN-pai2 lai5 kiN3 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3.  24). Goa2 beh tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut goa7-pang lang5, khui-khoah li2 e5 keng2-kai3; li2 chit8-ni5 saN-pai2 chiuN7-khi3 kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 si5, tek-khak bo5 lang5 tham li2 e5 thou2-toe7.  25). Li2 m7-thang chiong Goa2 e5 seng-le2 e5 huih, chham u7 kaN3 e5 mih8 lai5 hian3; poaN5-ke3-choeh e5 che3-mih8 ia7 m7-thang lau5 kau3 ke3 cha2-khi2.  26). Toe7--nih te7-it khi2-thau5 sek8 e5 mih8, tioh8 sang3 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3.  Chu2 soaN-iuN5-a2 m7-thang eng7 i e5 bu2 e5 lin.
	27). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 sia2 chiah e5 oe7, in-ui7 Goa2 si7 chiau3 chiah e5 oe7 kap li2 i2-kip8 I2-sek-liat8 lip8-iok.  28). Mou5-se kap Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7-hia si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5, bo5 chiah8 piaN2 bo5 lim chui2.  I chiong chit e5 iok e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 chap8-tiau5-kai3, sia2 ti7 nng7 te3 pi.
	29). Mou5-se loh8 Se-nai2 soaN e5 si5, i e5 chhiu2 theh8 nng7 te3 iok-pi, i loh8-soaN e5 si5, i e5 bin7, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap i kong2-oe7, chiu7 sia7-chhut kng, Mou5-se ka-ki7 m7-chai.  30). A-lun5 kap I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Mou5-se e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, i e5 bin7 sia7-chhut kng; in chiu7 kiaN, m7-kaN2 oa2-kun7 i.  31). Mou5-se kio3 in lai5, A-lun5 kap hoe7-tiong chiah e5 thau5-lang5 chiu7 long2 to3-tng2 kau3 i hia; Mou5-se chiu7 kap in kong2-oe7.  32). Jian5-au7 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 long2 chin3-cheng5 lai5; i chiu7 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Se-nai2 soaN kap i sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, long2 hoan-hu3 in.  33). Mou5-se kap in kong2 oe7 beng5-pek8, chiu7 eng7 phe3 ta3-bin7.  34). Chong2-si7 Mou5-se jip8-khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 kap I kong2-oe7, phe3 chiu7 hian--khi2-lai5, kau3 i chhut--lai5.  I chhut--lai5 e5 si5, chiu7 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3--e5, ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2.  35). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Mou5-se e5 bin7, Mou5-se e5 bin7 sia7-chhut kng, Mou5-se koh eng7 phe3 ta3-bin7, theng3-hau7 kau3 i jip8-khi3 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2-oe7 phe3 chiu7 hian--khi2-lai5.

[35]	Mou5-se chio-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7, tui3 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 e5 oe7, kah lin2 tioh8 kiaN5--e5, chiu7-si7 chiah-e5.  2). Lak8-jit8 tioh8 choe3-kang, te7-chhit jit8 si7 lin2 e5 seng3-jit8, si7 toa7 e5 an-hioh-jit8, lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; hoan7-na7 ti7 chit-jit8 choe3-kang--e5, tioh8 hou7 i si2.  3). Tng an-hioh-jit8, ti7 lin2 tak8 keng chhu3-lai7 m7-thang khi2-he2.
	4). Mou5-se tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 e5 oe7, si7 an2-ni kong2,  5). Lin2 tiong-kan tioh8 theh8 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; kiN3-na7 sim goan7--e5, thang theh8 i lai5, choe3 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 le2-mih8;  6). chiu7-si7 kim, gun5, tang5, lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, iu3-toe7,  7). soaN-iuN5-mng5, ni2-ang5 e5 iuN5-kang2-phe5, hai2-kau2-phe5,  8). cho7-kiap-chha5, tiam2-teng e5 iu5, phang e5 liau7, thang choe3 boah e5 iu5 kap phang-hiuN,  9). ang5-be2-lo2 kap pat8-iuN7 e5 po2-chioh8, thang siuN ti7 i2-hut-tek kap pou2-koa3.  10). Lin2 tiong-kan kiN3-na7 sim u7 ti3-hui7--e5, long2 tioh8 lai5 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa it-chhe3 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5;  11). chiu7-si7 hoe7-bou7, i e5 pou3-piN5, kap i e5 koa3, i e5 kau, i e5 pan2, i e5 hoaiN5-kong5, i e5 thiau7, i e5 khu7;  12). kui7, kap i e5 kng3, si-un-sou2, kap jia-chah8 e5 tiuN3-li5;  13). toh kap i e5 kng3, kap i e5 khi3-ku7, kap pai5-liat8 e5 piaN2;  14). tiam2-kng e5 teng-tai5 kap i e5 khi3-ku7, teng-choaN2 kap tiam2-kng e5 iu5;  15). hiuN-toaN5 kap i e5 kng3, boah e5 iu5, kap phang-hiuN, i2-kip8 hoe7-bou7 mng5 e5 mng5-li5;  16). sio-che3 e5 toaN5 kap i tang5 e5 bang7, kap i e5 kng3, i2-kip8 i it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, soe2-tng7 e5 phun5 kap i e5 cho7;  17). tiuN5 e5 tiuN3-ui5, kap i e5 thiau7, in e5 khu7, kap tiuN5-mng5 e5 mng5-li5;  18). hoe7-bou7 sou2 teng3 e5 teng, kap tiuN5 sou2 teng3 e5 teng, kap in e5 soh;  19). cheng-kong e5 i-hok8, ti7 seng3-sou2 chheng7 lai5 hok8-sai7--e5, chiu7-si7 che3-si A-lun5 e5 seng3-saN kap i e5 kiaN2 e5 saN, chheng7 lai5 tam-tng che3-si e5 chit.
	20). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 tui3 Mou5-se e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut-khi3.  21). KiN3-na7 siu7 kam2-tong7, tui3 sim hoaN-hi2--e5, long2-chong2 lai5, theh8 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, eng7 lai5 choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 kang, kap it-chhe3 e5 lou7-eng7, ia7 eng7 lai5 choe3 seng3-saN.  22). KiN3-na7 chhut ti7 sim hoaN-hi2--e5, ta-pou hu7-jin5 long2 lai5, tak8-e5 chiong kim-khi3, chiu7-si7 heng-cheng5 e5 pin2-chiam, hi7-kau, phah-in3 e5 chhiu2-chi2, kap chhiu2-khoan5; che si7 tak8-lang5 chiong i e5 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  23). KiN3-na7 lang5 u7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, iu3-toe7, soaN-iuN5-mng5, ni2-ang5 e5 iuN5-kang2-phe5, hai2-kau2-phe5, long2 theh8-lai5.  24). KiN3-na7 hian3 gun5 kap tang5, choe3 le2-mih8--e5, long2 theh8-lai5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; kiN3-na7 u7 cho7-kiap-chha5 thang choe3 sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7--e5, ia7 theh8--lai5.  25). KiN3-na7 sim-lai7 u7 ti3-hui7 e5 hu7-lu2, chhin-chhiu2 phang2 soaN3, chiong sou2 phang2 e5 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap iu3-toe7 long2 theh8--lai5.  26). KiN3-u7 ti3-hui7 e5 sim siu7 kam2-tong7 e5 hu7-lu2, chiu7 phang2 soaN-iuN5-mng5.  27). Chiah e5 thau5-lang5 chiong ang5-be2-lo2, kap pat8-iuN7 e5 po2-chioh8, thang siuN ti7 i2-hut-tek kap pou2-koa3--e5, long2 theh8-lai5.  28). Koh theh8 hiuN-liau7 kap iu5, thang eng7 i lai5 tiam2 teng, choe3 boah e5 iu5, choe3 phang e5 hiuN.  29). I2-sek-liat8 lang5, bo5-lun7 lam5-lu2, kiN3-na7 sim hoaN-hi2 hian3 le2-mih8 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, long2 hoaN-hi2 theh8 le2-mih8 lai5, choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok-tiong7 Mou5-se sou2 hoan-hu3 in choe3 it-chhe3 e5 kang.
	30). Mou5-se tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Lin2 khoaN3, Iu5-tai7 e5 chi-phai3 Hou7-jiN2 e5 sun, OU-li7 e5 kiaN2 Pi2-sat-liat8, Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng chi2 mia5 tiau3 i.  31). Koh eng7 Siong7-te3 e5 sin5 chhiong-moa2 i, hou7 i u7 ti3-hui7, u7 chhang-mia5, u7 chai-bat, oe7 choe3 tak8-iuN7 e5 kang;  32). oe7 siuN7-chhut ki5-khiau2 e5 kang, lai5 choe3 kim, gun5, tang5 hiah e5 mih8,  33). ia7 oe7 khek po2-chioh8 lai5 jip8--i; ia7 oe7 khek chha5, oe7 choe3 tak8-iuN7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang.  34). Koh hou7 i kap Tan3 e5 chi-phai3, A-hi-sat-boat e5 kiaN2 A-ho5-li7-a-pek, sim u7 leng5-khiau3, oe7 ka3-si7 lang5.  35). Chiah e5 lang5 I eng7 ti3-hui7 chhiong-moa2 in e5 sim; hou7 in oe7 choe3 tak8-iuN7 e5 kang, bo5-lun7 tiau-khek e5 kang, ki5-khiau2 e5 kang, eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap iu3-toe7, siu3 hoe--e5, chit-pou3--e5, tak8-iuN7 e5 kang long2 oe7 choe3, ia7 oe7 siuN7-chhut ki5-khiau2 e5 kang.

[36]	Pi2-sat-liat8 kap A-ho5-li7-a-pek, kap long2-chong2 sim u7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 ti3-hui7 chhang-mia5 hou7 in chai choe3 seng3-sou2 tak8-iuN7 lou7-eng7 e5 kang--e5, long2 tioh8 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3--e5 choe3 kang.
	2). Mou5-se tiau3 Pi2-sat-liat8, A-ho5-li7-a-pek, kap kiN3-na7 sim u7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 lai5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 ti3-hui7 siuN2-su3 in e5 sim, sim siu7 kam2-tong7 lai5 choe3-kang--e5.  3). In tui3 Mou5-se theh8 it-chhe3 e5 le2-mih8, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ui7-tioh8 choe3 seng3-sou2 kap lai7-bin7 sou2 eng7 e5 mih8 theh8--lai5-e5.  Peh-siN3 tak8 cha2-khi2 iu5-goan5 eng7 kam-sim hian3 e5 le2-mih8 theh8-lai5 hou7--i.  4). KiN3-na7 choe3 seng3-sou2 e5 kang chiah-e5 u7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5, long2 chiam7-theng5 in sou2 choe3 e5 kang;  5). lai5 tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Peh-siN3 sou2 theh8--lai5-e5, pi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beng7-leng7 choe3 e5 kang sou2 tioh8 eng7 e5 liau7, ke3-giah8 u7 chhun.  6). Mou5-se chhut-beng7, in chiu7 soan-pou3 ti7 choan5-iaN5, kong2, Bo5-lun7 lam5-lu2 boh8-tit koh choe3 sim2-mih8 lai5, hian3 hou7 seng3-sou2; tui3 an2-ni chou2-chi2 peh-siN3 bo5 koh theh8--lai5.  7). In-ui7 in sou2 u7 e5 chhai5-liau7, kau3-giah8 thang choe3 it-chhe3 sou2 tioh8 choe3 chiah e5 kang, soa3 u7 chhun.
	8). In tiong-kan kiN3-na7 sim u7 ti3-hui7 choe3-kang--e5, eng7 chap8-pak e5 tiuN3 choe3 hoe7-bou7; chiah e5 tiuN3 si7 eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7; ia7 eng7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang chit-chiaN5 ki-lou7-peng choe3--i.  9). Mui2 pak tiuN3 tng5 ji7-chap8-poeh tiu2, khoah si3-tiu2; tiuN3 long2 si7 chit8-iuN7 e5 chhun3-chhioh.  10). Chit gou7 pak tiuN3, i chhong3 hou7 in tak8 pak saN-lian5; hit gou7 pak tiuN3 ia7 tak8-pak saN-lian5.  11). Ti7 chit-e5 saN-lian5 e5 tiuN3, lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2 choe3 lam5-sek e5 liu2-phan3; ti7 hit-e5 saN-lian5 e5 tiuN3, lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2 ia7 an2-ni choe3.  12). I ti7 chit nia2 tiuN3 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3, koh ti7 te7-ji7 nia2 tiuN3 saN-lian5 e5 piN-a2, ia7 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3; liu2-phan3 long2 nng7-e5 nng7-e5 saN-tui3.  13). Koh choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 kim-kau, eng7 i lai5 kau hou7 tiuN3 saN-lian5; chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 hoe7-bou7.
	14). I koh eng7 soaN-iuN5-mng5 chit chap8-it pak e5 tiuN3, choe3 hoe7-bou7-teng2 e5 pou3-piN5;  15). mui2-pak tiuN3 tng5 saN-chap8 tiu2, khoah si3-tiu2; chap8-it pak tiuN3 long2 chit8-iuN7 e5 chhun3-chhioh.  16). Chiong gou7 pak tiuN3 lian5-choe3 chit8-pak, koh chiong lak8 pak tiuN3 lian5-choe3 chit8-pak.  17). Ti7 chit e5 saN-lian5 e5 tiuN3 lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2, i choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3, ti7 hit e5 saN-lian5 lou7-be2 pak e5 piN-a2 ia7 choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 liu2-phan3.  18). I koh choe3 gou7-chap8 e5 tang5-kau, hou7 pou3-piN5 lian5-choe3 chit8-e5.  19). Koh eng7 ni2-ang5 e5 iuN5-phe5 choe3 pou3-piN5 e5 koa3; koh eng7 hai2-kau2-phe5 koa3 ti7 teng2-bin7.
	20). I eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 hoe7-bou7 khia7 e5 pan2.  21). Khia7 e5 pan2 tng5 chap8-tiu2, khoah chit8-tiu2-poaN3.  22). Tak8 te3 pan2 u7 nng7 e5 sun2 saN-pai5; hoe7-bou7 it-chhe3 e5 pan2 long2 chiau3 an2-ni choe3.  23). I choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 pan2, lam5-peng5 e5 lam5--si3 ji7-chap8 te3 pan2;  24). ti7 chiah e5 ji7-chap8 te3 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 choe3 si3-chap8 e5 gun5-khu7; chit8 te3 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7 lai5 chheng7 i nng7 ki sun2; koh chit8 te3 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 ia7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7 lai5 chheng7 i nng7 ki sun2.  25). Hoe7-bou7 te7-ji7 bin7, chiu7-si7 pak-bin7, ia7 choe3 pan2 ji7-chap8-te3,  26). kap in e5 gun5-khu7 si3-chap8-e5; chit e5 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7, hit e5 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 ia7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7.  27). Hoe7-bou7 e5 au7-bin7, chiu7-si7 sai-bin7, ia7 choe3 lak8 te3 pan2.  28). Hoe7-bou7 au7-bin7 e5 nng7 e5 kak-thau5, choe3 nng7 te3 pan2.  29). Pan2 e5 e7-tng5, nng7-e5 saN-tang5, tit8-kau3 teng2-bin7 te7-it e5 khoan5 long2 si7 ka-nng5-e5; nng7 e5 kak-thau5 e5 pan2 long2 si7 an2-ni choe3.  30). U7 poeh e5 pan2, kap chap8-lak8 e5 gun5-khu7; tak8 te3 pan2 e5 e7-bin7 u7 nng7 e5 khu7.  31). I eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 hoaiN5-kong5; ui7-tioh8 hoe7-bou7 chit-peng5 e5 pan2 choe3 gou7-ki,  32). ui7-tioh8 hoe7-bou7 hit-peng5 e5 pan2 choe3 gou7-ki; koh ui7-tioh8 hoe7-bou7-au7 sai-bin7 e5 pan2 choe3 gou7-ki.  33). Pan2 e5 tui3-tiong hit ki hoaiN5-kong5, hou7 i tui3 chit-thau5 kau3 hit-thau5.  34). Pan2 eng7 kim pau; koh choe3 pan2 e5 kim-khoan5 lai5 tho3 kong5; kong5 ia7 eng7 kim pau.
	35). Koh eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 chit tiuN3-li5; chit e5 tiuN3-li5 eng7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang chit-chiaN5 ki-lou7-peng lai5 choe3--e5.  36). Koh eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 ui7-tioh8 i choe3 si3 ki thiau7, eng7 kim pau i; in e5 kau si7 kim--e5; koh ui7-tioh8 in chu3 si3 e5 gun5-khu7.  37). Eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, eng7 siu3-hoe e5 kang choe3 pou3-piN5 mng5 e5 mng5-li5,  38). kap i gou7 ki thiau7, kap in e5 kau; in e5 thiau7-tau2 kap hoaiN5-koaiN eng7 kim pau i; hit gou7 e5 khu7 si7 tang5--e5.

[37]	Pi2-sat-liat8 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 kui7, tng5 nng7-tiu2-poaN3, khoah tiu2-poaN3, koaiN5 tiu2-poaN3;  2). lai7-goa7 eng7 ho2-kim pau i, si3-ui5 khi2 kim-soaN3,  3). ti7 i e5 si3-kha ka7 i chu3 si3 e5 kim-khoan5; chit-peng5 nng7 khoan5, hit-peng5 nng7 khoan5.  4). Eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 nng7 ki kng3, eng7 kim pau i.  5). Chiong kng3 chhng ti7 kui7-piN e5 khoan5-lai7, thang kng kui7.  6). Eng7 ho2-kim choe3 si-un-sou2, tng5 nng7-tiu2-poaN3, khoah tiu2-poaN3.  7). Eng7 kim choe3 nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng; eng7 chhia e5 hoat choe3 i, ti7 si-un-sou2 e5 siang-thau5;  8). chit-thau5 chit8 e5 ki-lou7-peng, hit-thau5 chit8 e5 ki-lou7-peng; nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng ti7 si-un-sou2 e5 siang-thau5 kap i lian5-choe3 chit8-te3.  9). Nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng koaiN5-koaiN5 thi2-khui sit8, eng7 in e5 sit8 jia si-un-sou2, in e5 bin7 saN-tui3; ki-lou7-peng e5 bin7 aN3 si-un-sou2.
	10). I eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 toh, tng5 nng7-tiu2, khoah chit8-tiu2, koaiN5 tiu2-poaN3;  11). eng7 ho2-kim pau i, si3-ui5 ka7 i khi2 kim-soaN3.  12). Toh e5 si3-ui5 kok choe3 chit8 pa-chiuN2 khoah e5 hoaiN5-niu5; hoaiN5-niu5-teng2 si3-ui5 khi2 kim-soaN3.  13). Ka7 i chu3 si3 e5 kim-khoan5, an ti7 i e5 si3-kha e5 si3-kak.  14).
