An khoan5 e5 sou2-chai7 oa2-kun7 hoaiN5-niu5, thang chhng-kng3 lai5 kng toh.  15). Eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 nng7 ki kng3, eng7 kim pau i, thang kng toh.  16). Ia7 choe3 toh-teng2 e5 khi3-ku7, i e5 poaN5, oaN2, pan5, poe, thang lai5 koan3-tian7, long2 eng7 ho2-kim choe3.
	17). I eng7 ho2-kim choe3 teng-tai5; teng-tai5 e5 cho7 kap tiong-thiau7, i e5 poe7, i e5 bak8, i e5 hoe, long2 eng7 phah e5 hoat, choe3 kui-cho7;  18).  i e5 piN-a2 pun-chhut lak8-ki; teng-tai5 e5 chit-peng5 u7 saN-ki, teng-tai5 e5 hit-peng5 u7 saN-ki;  19). chit-peng5 mui2-ki u7 saN e5 poe, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 heng7-hoe, u7 bak8 u7 hoe; hit-peng5 mui2-ki ia7 u7 saN e5 poe, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 heng7-hoe, u7 bak8 u7 hoe; tui3 teng-tai5 pun-chhut e5 lak8-ki long2 si7 an2-ni.  20). Teng-tai5 thiau7 u7 si3 e5 poe, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 heng7-hoe, u7 i e5 bak8, kap i e5 hoe.  21). Nng7-ki e5 e7-bin7 u7 chit8-bak8 kap i saN-lian5; koh nng7-ki e5 e7-bin7 u7 chit8-bak8 kap i saN-lian5; koh nng7-ki e5 e7-bin7 u7 chit8-bak8 kap i saN-lian5; teng-tai5 sou2 chhut e5 lak8-ki long2 si7 an2-ni.  22). Hiah e5 bak8 kap hiah e5 ki long2 kap i lian5-choe3 chit8-e5; long2 eng7 ho2-kim, chiau3 phah e5 hoat choe3.  23). Ia7 ka7 i choe3 chhit e5 teng-choaN2, kap i e5 chian2, kap i e5 poaN5, long2 eng7 ho2-kim choe3 e5.  24). Choe3 teng-tai5 kap it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7 eng7 ho2-kim chit8 tha-lian5-tek.
	25). I eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 hiuN-toaN5, tng5 chit8-tiu2, khoah chit8-tiu2, khoan2-sit su3-hong--e5; koaiN5 nng7-tiu2; i hiah e5 kak kap toaN5 lian5-choe3 chit8-te3.  26). ToaN5 kap i e5 teng2-bin7, kap i e5 si3-ui5, kap i hiah e5 kak, long2 eng7 ho2-kim pau i, ia7 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 khi2 kim-soaN3.  27). Koh ka7 i choe3 nng7 e5 kim-khoan5, an ti7 khi2-soaN3 e5 e7-bin7, ti7 toaN5 e5 siang-peng5 nng7 ki hoaiN5-koaiN e5 teng2-bin7; chiah e5 khoan5 si7 choe3 chhng-kng3 e5 lou7-eng7, thang kng toaN5.  28). Eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 kng3, eng7 kim pau in.  29). Koh chiau3 choe3 phang-bi7 e5 hoat choe3 thang boah e5 seng3-iu5, kap phang-liau7 chheng-kiat e5 hiuN.

[38]	I eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 sio-che3 e5 toaN5; tng5 gou7-tiu2, khoah gou7-tiu2, chit e5 toaN5 si7 su3-hong--e5; koaiN5 saN-tiu2.  2). Ti7 toaN5 e5 si3 kak-thau5 choe3 si3 ki kak, kap toaN5 saN-lian5 choe3 chit8-e5, eng7 tang5 pau i.  3). Koh choe3 toaN5 it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, i e5 phun5, thuh-a2, poaN5, chhe, he2-tiaN2; it-chhe3 e5 khi2-ku7 long2 eng7 tang5 choe3.  4). Koh ui7-tioh8 toaN5 eng7 tang5-bang7 choe3 chit8 e5 chan5, an ti7 toaN5 si3-bin7 ui5-io-pan2 e5 e7-bin7, hou7 i thau3-kau3 toaN5 e5 poaN3-io.  5). Ui7-tioh8 tang5 e5 chan5 e5 si3-kak chu3 si3 e5 khoan5, choe3 chhng-kng3 e5 lou7-eng7.  6). Eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 kng3, eng7 tang5 pau in.  7). Chiong kng3 chhng ti7 toaN5 siang-peng5 e5 khoan5-lai7, eng7 i lai5 kng toaN5; ia7 eng7 pan2 choe3 toaN5, toaN5 si7 khang-khak.
	8). I eng7 tang5 choe3 soe2-tng7 e5 phun5, kap tang5-cho7; si7 eng7 hoe7-bou7 mng5-cheng5 choe3-kang e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 tang5-kiaN3 choe3--e5.  9). I choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 tiuN5; hit e5 tiuN5 e5 lam5--si3, eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3 ui5, chit8-pah tiu2.  10). Ui5 e5 thiau7 ji7-chap8 ki, tang5-choe3 e5 khu7 ji7-chap8-e5; thiau7 e5 kau kap hoaiN5-koaiN si7 eng7 gun5 choe3--e5.  11). Pak-bin7 ia7 chit8-pah tiu2, ui5 e5 thiau7 ji7-chap8 ki, tang5-choe3 e5 khu7 ji7-chap8 e5; thiau7 e5 kau kap hoaiN5-koaiN si7 eng7 gun5 choe3--e5.  12). Sai-bin7 u7 ui5 gou7-chap8 tiu2, ui5 e5 thiau7 chap8-ki, khu7 chap8-e5; thiau7 e5 kau kap hoaiN5-koaiN si7 eng7 gun5 choe3--e5.  13). Tang-bin7 e5 tang--si3 gou7-chap8 tiu2.  14). Mng5 chit-peng5 e5 ui5 chap8-gou7 tiu2, ui5 e5 thiau7 saN-ki, u7 khu7 saN-e5.  15). Hit-peng5 ia7 si7 an2-ni; tiuN5-mng5 e5 cho2-iu7, kok u7 ui5 chap8-gou7 tiu2; ui5 e5 thiau7 saN-ki, khu7 saN-e5.  16). TiuN5 si3-bin7 e5 tiuN3-ui5 long2 si7 eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3.  17). Thiau7 e5 khu7 si7 tang5--e5, thiau7 e5 kau kap hoaiN5-koaiN si7 gun5--e5; thiau7-tau2 si7 eng7 gun5 pau--e5; tiuN5 long2 chong2 e5 thiau7 si7 eng7 gun5 e5 hoaiN5-koaiN chheng7 saN-lian5-e5.  18). TiuN5-mng5 e5 mng5-li5 si7 eng7 siu3-hoe e5 kang, eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7 kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3--e5; tng5 ji7-chap8 tiu2, koaiN5 gou7 tiu2, kap tiuN5 e5 ui5 saN-phoe3.  19). In e5 thiau7 si3-ki, tang5 e5 khu7 si3-e5, thiau7 e5 kau si7 gun5--e5, thiau7-tau2 si7 gun5 pau--e5, hoaiN5-koaiN si7 gun5--e5.  20). Hoe7-bou7 i2-kip8 tiuN5-lai7 si3-ui5 sou2 teng3 e5 teng, long2 si7 tang5--e5.
	21). Chit e5 hoe7-bou7 si7 cheng3-ku3 e5 hoe7-bou7; hit tiong-kan Li7-bi7 lang5 sou2 beh eng7 mih8-kiaN7 e5 chong2-giah8, si7 chiau3 Mou5-se sou2 hoan-hu3, keng-ke3 che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2, I2-tha-ma2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 sng3--e5.  22). KiN3-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5, Iu5-tai7 e5 chi-phai3, Hou7-jiN2 e5 sun, OU-li7 e5 kiaN2, Pi2-sat-liat8 long2 choe3--i.  23). Kap i saN-kap choe3--e5, u7 Tan3 e5 chi-phai3, A-hi-sat-boat e5 kiaN2, A-ho5-li7-a-pek, i si7 gau5 tiau-khek, koh ki5-khiau2 e5 sai-hu7, koh oe7 eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7 kap iu3-toe7 lai5 siu3-hoe.
	24). Choe3 seng3-sou2 it-chhe3 e5 kang sou2 eng7 e5 kim, chiu7-si7 lang5 sou2 hian3 e5 kim, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 pheng5, u7 ji7-chap8-kau2 tha-lian5-tek, koh chhit-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8.  25). Hoe7-tiong siu7 sng3 e5 lang5 sou2 chhut e5 gun5, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 pheng5, u7 chit8-pah tha-lian5-tek, koh chit8-chheng chhit-pah chhit-chap8 gou7 sia3-khek-lek8.  26). KiN3-na7 ke3--khi3 kui ti7 hiah e5 ke3-sng3--e5, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, u7 lak8-chap8-ban7 lian5 saN-chheng gou7-pah gou7-chap8 lang5, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 pheng5, tak8-lang5 chhut-gun5 poaN3 sia3-khek-lek8, chiu7-si7 chit8 pi2-ka.  27). Eng7 hit-e5 chit8-pah tha-lian5-tek e5 gun5, chu3 seng3-sou2 e5 khu7, kap tiuN3-li5-thiau7 e5 khu7; chit8 pah tha-lian5-tek choe3 chit8-pah e5 khu7, chit8 e5 khu7 eng7 chit8 tha-lian5-tek.  28). Eng7 hit e5 chit8-chheng chhit-pah chhit-chap8-gou7 sia3-khek-lek8 e5 gun5, choe3 thiau7 e5 kau, ia7 pau thiau7-tau2, ia7 choe3 i e5 hoaiN5-koaiN.  29). Sou2 hian3 e5 tang5, u7 chhit-chap8 tha-lian5-tek, koh nng7-chheng si3-pah sia3-khek-lek8.  30). Eng7 chit e5 tang5 choe3 hoe7-bou7 mng5 e5 khu7, kap tang5-toaN5, kap i e5 tang5-bang7 e5 chan5, kap toaN5 long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7,  31). i2-kip8 tiuN5 si3-ui5 e5 khu7, kap tiuN5-mng5 e5 khu7, kap hoe7-bou7 long2-chong2 sou2 teng3 e5 teng, kap tiuN5 si3-ui5 sou2 teng3 e5 teng.

[39]	In eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7 choe3 cheng-kong e5 i-hok8, ti7 seng3-sou2 chheng7 lai5 hok8-sai7, koh ka7 A-lun5 choe3 seng3-saN, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.
	2). I eng7 kim kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, choe3 i2-hut-tek.  3). In chiong kim tui5 choe3 poh8-phiN3, chian2 choe3 soaN3, chham ti7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap iu3-toe7 eng7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang choe3--e5.  4). Koh ka7 i choe3 phi-kian lai5 lian5--i, hou7 i siang-peng5 saN-lian5.  5). Hit teng2-bin7 ki5-khiau2 e5 kang chit e5 toa3, sou2 eng7 lai5 ha5--e5, kap i2-hut-tek tang5-chit8-iuN7 e5 choe3-hoat, kap i lian5-choe3 chit8-te3, eng7 kim kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3--i; chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.
	6). Koh tok ang5-be2-lo2 jip8 ti7 kim-cho5--nih, chiau3 khek-in3 e5 hoat, khek I2-sek-liat8 hiah e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5 ti7 hit teng2-bin7;  7). an ti7 i2-hut-tek e5 phi-kian, ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3 ki3-liam7 e5 chioh8; chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.
	8). I eng7 ki5-khiau2 e5 sai-hu7 e5 chhiu2-kang choe3 pou2-koa3, kap i2-hut-tek tang5 chit8-iuN7 e5 choe3-hoat; eng7 kim, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7 choe3--e5.  9). Pou2-koa3 si7 su3-hong--e5; au2 choe3 siang-teng5; tng5 chit8-liah8, khoah chit8-liah8, si7 siang-teng5--e5.  10). Teng2-bin7 jip8 po2-chioh8 si3-choa7, chit8-choa7 si7 ang5-po2-chioh8, ng5-gek8, ang5-gek8; che si7 te7-it choa7.  11). Te7-ji7 choa7 si7 lek8-po2-chioh8, lam5-po2-chioh8, kim-kong-chioh8.  12). Te7-saN choa7 si7 chi2-sek e5 be2-lo2, peh8-sek e5 be2-lo2, chi2-sek e5 chui2-chiN.  13). Te7-si3 choa7 si7 lek8-gek8, ang5-be2-lo2, phek-gek8; chiah-e5 long2 jip8 ti7 kim-cho5-lai7.  14). Chiah e5 po2-chioh8 chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5, kiong7 chap8-ji7 te3, chhin-chhiuN7 khek in3, mui2-te3 khek chit8 e5 mia5, ui7-tioh8 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3 lai5 choe3--i.  15). In eng7 ho2-kim phah lian7-a2, chhin-chhiuN7 soh-a2, an ti7 pou2-koa3.  16). In koh choe3 nng7 e5 kim-cho5 kap nng7 e5 kim-khoan5, chiong chi2 nng7 e5 khoan5 an ti7 pou2-koa3 e5 siang-thau5.  17). Chiong sou2 phah hit nng7 tiau5 kim-lian7-a2, lian5 ti7 siang-thau5 nng7 e5 khoan5.  18). Eng7 sou2 phah nng7-tiau5 lian7-a2 e5 siang-thau5, lian5 ti7 nng7 e5 cho5, an ti7 i2-hut-tek phi-kian e5 thau5-cheng5.  19). Choe3 nng7 e5 kim-khoan5, he7 ti7 pou2-koa3 siang-thau5 e5 kiN5, kun7 i2-hut-tek ng3-lai7 hit-peng5.  20). Koh choe3 nng7 e5 kim-khoan5, an ti7 i2-hut-tek phi-kian e7-bin7 e5 thau5-cheng5, oa2-kun7 saN-lian5 e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 i2-hut-tek ki5-khiau2 e5 kang sou2 chit e5 toa3 e5 teng2-bin7.  21). In eng7 lam5-sek e5 iu3-toa3, chiong pou2-koa3 e5 khoan5 kap i2-hut-tek e5 khoan5 pak8 saN-lian5, hou7 i liam5 ti7 i2-hut-tek ki5-khiau2 e5 kang sou2 chit e5 toa3; hou7 pou2-koa3 kap i2-hut-tek bo5 li7-phang7; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.
	22). I eng7 chit-pou3 e5 kang choe3 i2-hut-tek lai7-bin7 e5 goa7-phau3, kui-nia2 si7 lam5-sek.  23). Phau3 e5 tui3-tiong choe3 chit8 e5 nia2-khang; khang e5 chiu-ui5 chit nia2-ian7, chhin-chhiuN7 chian3-kah e5 nia2-khang, bian2-tit phoa3-lih8.  24). Phau3 e5 e7-kha-pou5, eng7 lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, kap ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, choe3 siah8-liu5.  25). Koh eng7 ho2-kim choe3 ham5-leng5, eng7 ham5-leng5, kaN5 siah8-liu5, he7 ti7 phau3 si3-ui5 e5 e7-kha-pou5, siah8-liu5 e5 tiong-kan;  26). chit8-liap8 ham5-leng5, chit8-liap8 siah8-liu5, chit8-liap8 ham5-leng5, chit8-liap8 siah8-liu5, ti7 phau3 si3-ui5 e5 e7-kha-pou5, thang chheng7 lai5 hok8-sai7; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.
	27). In eng7 chit-chiaN5 e5 iu3-toe7-pou3, ka7 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2 choe3 lai7-saN.  28). Ia7 choe3 iu3-toe7-pou3 e5 bo7, kap iu3-toe7-pou3 sui2-sui2 pau thau5-khak e5 kun, eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7-pou3 choe3-khou3.  29). Koh eng7 ke3-phang2 e5 iu3-toe7, kap lam5-sek, chi2-sek, chu-ang5-sek e5 liau7, eng7 siu3-hoe e5 chhiu2-kang, choe3 io-toa3; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se e5.
	30). In eng7 ho2-kim choe3 seng3 e5 bian2-liu5 e5 pai5, chiau3 khek-in3 e5 hoat; khek-ji7 ti7 hit teng2-bin7, kong2, CHOE3 SENG3 KUI IA5-HO5-HOA.  31). Koh eng7 lam5-sek e5 toa3, chiong pai5 pak8 ti7 bo7-teng2; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.
	32). Tui3 an2-ni chu7-chip8 e5 hoe7-bou7 it-chhe3 e5 kang long2 choe3 beng5-pek8, hoan7-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se e5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 an2-ni choe3.
	33). In sang3 kau3 Mou5-se hia, chiu7-si7 hoe7-bou7, pou3-piN5, kap long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7, i e5 kau, pan2, kong5, thiau7, khu7;  34). ni2-ang5 iuN5-kang2-phe5 e5 koa3, hai2-kau2-phe5 e5 koa3, kap jia-chah8 e5 tiuN3-li5,  35). hoat-kui7 kap i e5 kng3, kap si-un-sou2;  36). toh kap i long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7, kap pai5-liat8 e5 piaN2;  37). ho2-kim e5 teng-tai5, kap i e5 teng-choaN2, chiu7-si7 pai5-liat8 e5 teng-choaN2, kap i long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7, kap tiam2 kng e5 iu5;  38). kim-toaN5, boah e5 iu5, phang e5 hiuN-liau7, pou3-piN5-mng5 e5 mng5-li5;  39). tang5-toaN5, kap i e5 tang5 e5 chan5, i e5 kng3, kap i long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7, soe2-tng7 e5 phun5 kap i e5 cho7,  40). tiuN5 e5 tiuN3-ui5 kap i e5 thiau7, i e5 khu7, tiuN5-mng5 e5 mng5-li5, eng7 e5 soh, teng3 e5 teng, kap pou3-piN5 kap hoe7-bou7-lai7 it-khai3 choe3 lou7-eng7 e5 khi3-ku7;  41). cheng-kong e5 i-hok8, ti7 seng3-sou2 chheng7 lai5 hok8-sai7, kap che3-si A-lun5 e5 seng3-saN, i2-kip8 i e5 kiaN2 e5 saN, choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7.  42). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se it-chhe3 e5 oe7, choe3 it-chhe3 e5 kang.  43). Mou5-se khoaN3-kiN3 it-chhe3 e5 kang, khoaN3 ah, in i2-keng choe3-chiaN5, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3--e5, in chiau3 an2-ni choe3; Mou5-se chiu7 ka7 in chiok-hok.

[40]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). ChiaN-geh8 chhoe-it, li2 tioh8 khi2 chu7-chip8 e5 hoe7-bou7.  3). Li2 tioh8 he7 hoat-kui7 ti7 hit lai7-bin7, eng7 tiuN3-li5 jia-chah8--i.  4). Kng toh jip8--khi3, pai5-siat teng2-bin7 e5 mih8; kng teng-tai5 jip8-khi3, tiam2 i e5 teng.  5). Kng sio-hiuN e5 kim-toaN5, he7 ti7 hoat-kui7-cheng5, koa3 hoe7-bou7 mng5 e5 mng5-li5.  6). Chiong sio-che3 e5 toaN5, he7 ti7 chu7-chip8 e5 hoe7-bou7 mng5-cheng5.  7). Chiong soe2-tng7 e5 phun5, he7 ti7 hoe7-bou7 kap toaN5 e5 tiong-kan, toe2 chui2 ti7 phun5-lai7.  8). Koh ti7 si3-ui5 khia7 tiuN5-ui5, koa3 tiuN5-mng5 e5 mng5-li5.  9). Eng7 boah e5 iu5 boah hoe7-bou7, kap ki5-tiong hoan7 sou2-u7--e5, hun-piat i kap long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7 choe3-seng3; i chiu7 choe3-seng3.  10). Koh boah sio-che3 e5 toaN5, kap i long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7, hun-piat toaN5 choe3-seng3; toaN5 chiu7 choe3 chi3-seng3.  11). Ia7 tioh8 boah soe2-tng7 e5 phun5, hun-piat i choe3-seng3.  12). Koh tioh8 chhoa7 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2, kau3 hoe7-bou7 mng5-cheng5, eng7 chui2 ka7 in soe2.  13). Ia7 ka7 A-lun5 chheng7 seng3-saN, koh eng7 iu5 boah i, hun-piat i choe3-seng3, hou7 i choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7 Goa2.  14). Koh chhoa7 i hiah e5 kiaN2 lai5, ka7 in chheng7 lai7-phau3.  15). Tioh8 ka7 in boah-iu5, chhin-chhiuN7 boah in lau7-pe7 chit8-iuN7, hou7 in choe3 che3-si lai5 hok8-sai7 Goa2; in siu7 boah-iu5 beh eng2-oan2 choe3 che3-si, kau3 tak8 se3-tai7.  16). Mou5-se an2-ni kiaN5; long2 si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 i e5 lai5 kiaN5.
	17). Te7-ji7 ni5 chiaN-geh8 chhoe-it, hoe7-bou7 chiu7 khia7--khi2-lai5.  18). Mou5-se khia7 hoe7-bou7 he7 hiah e5 khu7, khia7 hiah e5 pan2, chhng hiah e5 hoaiN5-kong5, khia7 hiah e5 thiau7.  19). Ti7 hoe7-bou7 teng2 tah pou3-piN5, chiong pou3-piN5 e5 koa3, kham3 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.  20). Koh eng7 lut8-hoat he7 ti7 kui7-lai7, eng7 kng3 chhng ti7 kui7--nih, he7 si-un-sou2 ti7 kui7-teng2.  21). Kng kui7 jip8 hoe7-bou7, koa3 jia-chah8 e5 tiuN3-li5, jia-chah8 hoat-kui7, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.  22). Koh chiong toh he7 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7, ti7 hoe7-bou7 e5 pak--si3, ti7 tiuN3-li5 goa7;  23). hi2 teng2-bin7 eng7 piaN2 pai5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.  24). Koh he7 teng-tai5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7, kap toh saN-tui3, ti7 hoe7-bou7 e5 lam5-peng5.  25). Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 tiam2-teng; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.  26). Koh he7 kim-toaN5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 e5 tiuN3-li5 cheng5;  27). ti7 hit teng2-bin7 sio phang-liau7 e5 hiuN; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.  28). Koh koa3 hoe7-bou7 mng5 e5 mng5-li5.  29). Ti7 chu7-chip8 e5 hoe7-bou7 mng5-cheng5, he7 sio-che3 e5 toaN5, chiong sio-che3 kap sou3-che3 hian3 ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.  30). He7 soe2-tng7 e5 phun5 ti7 hoe7-bou7 kap toaN5 e5 tiong-kan, phun5-lai7 toe2 chui2, thang soe2-tng7.  31). Mou5-se kap A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2, ti7-hia soe2-chhiu2 soe2-kha.  32). In jip8 hoe7-bou7 e5 si5, a2-si7 chiu7-kun7 toaN5 e5 si5, chiu7 soe2; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se--e5.  33). Ti7 hoe7-bou7 kap toaN5 e5 si3-ui5, khia7 tiuN3-ui5, ia7 koa3 tiuN3-ui5 mng5 e5 mng5-li5; an2-ni Mou5-se chiu7 oan5-kang.
	34). Hit-si5 hun5 jia-kham3 hoe7-bou7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng chhiong-moa2 hoe7-bou7.  35). Mou5-se boe7-oe7 jip8 hoe7-bou7, in-ui7 hun5 theng5 ti7 hit teng2-bin7; koh Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng chhiong-moa2 ti7 hoe7-bou7.  36). Hun5 tui3 hoe7-bou7 siu chiuN7-khi3 e5 si5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 khi2-sin kiaN5 in e5 lou7-cham7.  37). Hun5 na7 bo5 siu chiuN7-khi3, in chiu7 bo5 khi2-sin kiaN5, tit8-tit8 kau3 hun5 siu chiuN7-khi3.  38). Jit8--si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hun5 ti7 hoe7-bou7 teng2, mi5--si5 hit tiong-kan u7 he2, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5; ti7 in sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7-cham7 long2 si7 an2-ni.
